
α.1.1 KAh Solomon wunnaumonuh David menehkheau ut wutass8tam8onganit, & Jehovahoh um-Manitt8moh wetomuk, kah úmmuttáe mishéheuh.
E.1.1 And Solomon the son of David was strengthened in his kingdom, and the LORD his God was with him, and magnified him exceedingly.

α.1.2 Neit Solomon ken8nau wame Israeloh, muttannongane kah pasuk8e mugquompuh, kah wussittumwaénúh, kah nish$noh nanawunnuaénin ut wame Israel, keiche wut8shinneunk.
E.1.2 Then Solomon spake unto all Israel, to the captains of thousands and of hundreds, and to the judges, and to every governor in all Israel, the chief of the fathers.

α.1.3 Neit Solomon kah wame weeche mukkinneunk, auog qunuhqui ayeuonganit ut Gibeon, newutche na ohtop, wut-tabernaklum God, ne Moses wuttinneuhmoh Jehovah, ayikup ut touohkomukqut.
E.1.3 So Solomon, and all the congregation with him, went to the high place that was at Gibeon; for there was the tabernacle of the congregation of God, which Moses the servant of the LORD had made in the wilderness.

α.1.4 Qut wut-Arkum God, David uppaudtauun wutch Kirjath-jearim, ut ayeuonganit ne David quagquoshwehtamwontog: newutche, 8wekukkontamun ut Jerusalem.
E.1.4 But the ark of God had David brought up from Kirjathjearim to the place which David had prepared for it: for he had pitched a tent for it at Jerusalem.

α.1.5 Kah wonk brasse Altar, ne Bezaleel wunnaumonuh Uri, wunnaumonuh Hur kesteunkup, upponumun anaquohtag wuttabernakleum Jehovah: k[a]h Solomon kah mukkinneonk, wunnat8tomwehteatinneau.
E.1.5 Moreover the brasen altar, that Bezaleel the son of Uri, the son of Hur, had made, he put before the tabernacle of the LORD: and Solomon and the congregation sought unto it.

α.1.6 Kah Solomon na wuttin kuhkuhque[n], en brasse Altarut anaquabit Lord, ne ohtag ut mukkinneáe kommukqut, kah na wutut magun nequt muttannonganog kodtash chikohtae mag8ongash.
E.1.6 And Solomon went up thither to the brasen altar before the LORD, which was at the tabernacle of the congregation, and offered a thousand burnt offerings upon it.

α.1.7 Ne nohkog God naéhtauau Solomonoh, kah wuttinuh, wehquetumah, teaguas woh anumauun.
E.1.7 In that night did God appear unto Solomon, and said unto him, Ask what I shall give thee.

α.1.8 Kah Solomon unnau Godoh, kummishe monanum David n8sh, kah kenompass8tamwáhhin:
E.1.8 And Solomon said unto God, Thou hast shewed great mercy unto David my father, and hast made me to reign in his stead.

α.1.9 Yeuyeu woi Jehovah Manit, kukquoshomáonk n8sh David menehketeauunach: newutche kukketass8tamwáheh ut missinninnuut onatuh puppissiyeuut wutch mataánukeg.
E.1.9 Now, O LORD God, let thy promise unto David my father be established: for thou hast made me king over a people like the dust of the earth in multitude.

α.1.10 Eyeu waantamwahheh, kah wahteauwáheh, onk woh nussohham, kah woh nuppetutteam, ut anaquabhettit yeug missinninnûog, newutche howan wâussumont yeu kummissinninneumoh mataánunutche?
E.1.10 Give me now wisdom and knowledge, that I may go out and come in before this people: for who can judge this thy people, that is so great?

α.1.11 Kah God unnau Solomonoh, newutche yeu ohteau kuttahhut, kah matta k8wehquetum8h wenauwetuonk, ohtóonk, asuh quttianittuonk, asuh uppomantam8ongan8 kummatwomog, asuh matta k8wehquetum8 sepepomantamóonk, qut k8wehquetum waantamóonk kah wahteóonk, onk woh k8sum nummissinninneumog, neg adt ketass8tamuhkónun.
E.1.11 And God said to Solomon, Because this was in thine heart, and thou hast not asked riches, wealth, or honour, nor the life of thine enemies, neither yet hast asked long life; but hast asked wisdom and knowledge for thyself, that thou mayest judge my people, over whom I have made thee king:

α.1.12 Waantamóonk kah wahteauonk kittinnumontean, kah kuttinnumoush wenauwetuonk, kah ohtóonk, kah quttianittuonk, ne matta howae ketass8t ahtó8k negonuhkunkquean, asuh matta pish asukungquean ne weyane ohto8un.
E.1.12 Wisdom and knowledge is granted unto thee; and I will give thee riches, and wealth, and honour, such as none of the kings have had that have been before thee, neither shall there any after thee have the like.

α.1.13 Neit Solomon 8m qunuhqui ayeuonganit ne ut Gibeon en Jerusalem, wutch anaquohtag mukkinneáe kommuk, kah ketass8tam88 ut Israel.
E.1.13 Then Solomon came from his journey to the high place that was at Gibeon to Jerusalem, from before the tabernacle of the congregation, and reigned over Israel.

α.1.14 Kah Solomon mukkinnum chariotsash, kah horsesoh na8mukqutcheg: kah ohtau nequt muttannonganogkodtash, kah yaue pasuk88[a]sh chariotsash, kah nabo neese muttannonganogkussuog horsesoh na8mukqutcheg, neh pononcheh ut chariotse keitotanehtu kah weeche ketass8t ut Jerusalem.
E.1.14 And Solomon gathered chariots and horsemen: and he had a thousand and four hundred chariots, and twelve thousand horsemen, which he placed in the chariot cities, and with the king at Jerusalem.

α.1.15 Kah ketass8t silver kah gold onatuhteau qussukquanash ut Jerusalem, kah Cedaruhtugquash 8natuhheyeu8ash 8nouhkoiyeue Sycamoruhtukqut wutche muttaáneuk.
E.1.15 And the king made silver and gold at Jerusalem as plenteous as stones, and cedar trees made he as the sycomore trees that are in the vale for abundance.

α.1.16 Kah Solomon wutauau horsesoh wutch Egypt, kah hashabpe tuttuppinuh, ketass8t wutanaqushaeneumoh attumunaog hashabpe tuttuppinuh neanôadtinit.
E.1.16 And Solomon had horses brought out of Egypt, and linen yarn: the king's merchants received the linen yarn at a price.

α.1.17 Kah nemskomwog, kah sohh8wuttóog wutch Egypt Chariot wutch nequtta tahshe pasuk88ash silver sheklsash, kah pasu[kh]orse, wutch nequt pasuk88 kah napanna tahshinchagkodtash, kah ne wuttinne sohh8wunoneau horsesoh wutch wame Hittitse ketass8tamwut, kah wutch Syriae ketass8tamwut, nashpe wunnutchegan8out.
E.1.17 And they fetched up, and brought forth out of Egypt a chariot for six hundred shekels of silver, and an horse for an hundred and fifty: and so brought they out horses for all the kings of the Hittites, and for the kings of Syria, by their means.

α.2.1 KAh Solomon pak[od]tantam ayimunat wetu wutch 8wesuonk Jehovah kah wutass8tam8onganekommuk.
E.2.1 And Solomon determined to build an house for the name of the LORD, and an house for his kingdom.

α.2.2 Kah Solomon ogkemau nesausuk tahshinchage muttannonganog kussuog wosketompoh 8weassu[na]oont, kah shwosuk tahshinchage muttannonog kussuog, wanagittohhôsitcheg ut wadchuuhkontu: kah nishwe muttannonganog kussuog, kah nequtta tahshe pasuk88og, nanawunoncheg.
E.2.2 And Solomon told out threescore and ten thousand men to bear burdens, and fourscore thousand to hew in the mountain, and three thousand and six hundred to oversee them.

α.2.3 Kah Solomon negont8au en Hyram Tyre ketass8t n8wau, neanheop David n8sh, kah kenegonchhuontamauop Cedaroh, 8wekuhkonat, wutayinneat, (ne unnehe.)
E.2.3 And Solomon sent to Huram the king of Tyre, saying, As thou didst deal with David my father, and didst send him cedars to build him an house to dwell therein, even so deal with me.

α.2.4 Kusseh, nutayim wetu ut 8wesuonganit Jehovah num-Manitt8m, n8neetupanatamwae aninnumauonat, kah chikohsumunat wetemungquok, ut anaquabit, kah wutche nagwutteae nahtitteáe petukqunneg, kah wutche chikohtae mag8ongash, nompoaeu kah wunnonkquaeu, Sabothdayeu, kah wuske nepauzsaeu kah ut miyae ummishadtupp8onganehtu Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, yeu micheme yeu8 ut Israel.
E.2.4 Behold, I build an house to the name of the LORD my God, to dedicate it to him, and to burn before him sweet incense, and for the continual shewbread, and for the burnt offerings morning and evening, on the sabbaths, and on the new moons, and on the solemn feasts of the LORD our God. This is an ordinance for ever to Israel.

α.2.5 Kah wetu ne ayim, missi: newutche ánuukken8mau kum$Manitt8mun wame Manitt8h.
E.2.5 And the house which I build is great: for great is our God above all gods.

α.2.6 Qut howan tapenug 8wekuhkauonat, newutche kesuk, kah ukkesuk8mo kesukquog matta wuttapeouh? neit howan nen noh woh wekuhkauog? qut webe chikohsumunat wetemungquok ut anaquabit.
E.2.6 But who is able to build him an house, seeing the heaven and heaven of heavens cannot contain him? who am I then, that I should build him an house, save only to burn sacrifice before him?

α.2.7 Newutche yeuyeu nawutch negonshhuwontamah wosketomp, nôhtoe anakausuontog gold, kah silver, kah brasse, kah Iron, kah Purple, kah Crimson, kah 8nôagk, kah noh nôhtoe kohk[ók]ausit, weeche n[ò]htoe anuhkausitcheg neg weetomutcheg ut Judah, kah ut Jerusalem, neh n8sh David quagquoshwunumpuh.
E.2.7 Send me now therefore a man cunning to work in gold, and in silver, and in brass, and in iron, and in purple, and crimson, and blue, and that can skill to grave with the cunning men that are with me in Judah and in Jerusalem, whom David my father did provide.

α.2.8 Kah wonk negonshhuwontamah Cedaruhtugquash, Fi[rr]uhtugquash, kah Almuguhtugquash, wutch Lebanon (newutche n8wahteoh kittinneumog néhtóe tummethamwog timber ut Lebanon) kah kusseh, nuttinneumog pish weetomaog kittinneumoh.
E.2.8 Send me also cedar trees, fir trees, and algum trees, out of Lebanon: for I know that thy servants can skill to cut timber in Lebanon; and, behold, my servants shall be with thy servants,

α.2.9 Nukquagquashwehtamunkqunáoont m8[-]cheke timber, newutche wetu ne kodayim, pish missi kah monchanatamweyeu8.
E.2.9 Even to prepare me timber in abundance: for the house which I am about to build shall be wonderful great.

α.2.10 Kah kusseh, nuttinnumau kittinneumog wunagittahhôsuenuóg neg támetohhogig timber, nesnehchage muttannonganogkodt qutt8hwhosuash, sukquehthósu[e] wheatash: kah nesnehchage muttannonganogkodtu quttuhwhosuash barlyhash, kah nesnehchage muttannonanogkodtash wine bathsash: kah nesnehchage muttannonganogkodte pummée bathsash.
E.2.10 And, behold, I will give to thy servants, the hewers that cut timber, twenty thousand measures of beaten wheat, and twenty thousand measures of barley, and twenty thousand baths of wine, and twenty thousand baths of oil.

α.2.11 Neit Hyram Tyre ketass8t, wussukwhosue namp8ham, ne negonshhuadt en Solomonut, newutche Jehovah womonau ummissinninneumoh, na kuttit kutass8tamukonukqun.
E.2.11 Then Huram the king of Tyre answered in writing, which he sent to Solomon, Because the LORD hath loved his people, he hath made thee king over them.

α.2.12 Wonk Hyram n8wau, wunnanumunach Jehovah ummanitt8moh Israel, noh kesteunk kesuk kah ohke, noh anumauont Davidoh ketass8toh, waantamw[é] wunnaumoniinneuh, noh wahteunk wunnehtauunat, kah wohwohtam8onk, onk woh wekikauau Jehovahoh, kah ukketáss8tamukkomuk.
E.2.12 Huram said moreover, Blessed be the LORD God of Israel, that made heaven and earth, who hath given to David the king a wise son, endued with prudence and understanding, that might build an house for the LORD, and an house for his kingdom.

α.2.13 Kah yeuyeu nutann8n nehtuhtoenin, (wahteou wohwohtam8onk) noh wadchiit Huram n8shit.
E.2.13 And now I have sent a cunning man, endued with understanding, of Huram my father's,

α.2.14 Wunnaumonuh mittamwossis wutch Dane wuttauneunk, kah 8shoh wut-Tyre wosketomp, netuhto anakausuwontamun gold, kah Silver, kah brasse kah Iron, kah qussuk, kah timber kah purple, kah 8nóagk, kah wanegik hashabponagk, kah Crimson: wonk kogohkusohsinneah wame eiyane kogohksum8ongash, kah namehtinneat eiyane ussinnewonk, ne pish ponamauut, kenugke kenetuhtaeneumog, kah kenugke 8netuhtáeneumoh nussontimom David k8sh.
E.2.14 The son of a woman of the daughters of Dan, and his father was a man of Tyre, skilful to work in gold, and in silver, in brass, in iron, in stone, and in timber, in purple, in blue, and in fine linen, and in crimson; also to grave any manner of graving, and to find out every device which shall be put to him, with thy cunning men, and with the cunning men of my lord David thy father.

α.2.15 Newutche yeuyeu, wheatash kah barlyhash, kah pummee, kah wine, nish nussontimom keket8kontogish, negonshhuaj en wuttinneumehtu.
E.2.15 Now therefore the wheat, and the barley, the oil, and the wine, which my lord hath spoken of, let him send unto his servants:

α.2.16 Kah nenawun nuttummetahhamumun wuttuhqunash wutch Lebanon, ne woh teashe quenauwahikquean, kah kuppaudtauununan ut wutóhsuppahwuttauunat ut kehtahhannit en Joppa, k[á]h ken pish kutuss8tauun en Jerusalem.
E.2.16 And we will cut wood out of Lebanon, as much as thou shalt need: and we will bring it to thee in floats by sea to Joppa; and thou shalt carry it up to Jerusalem.

α.2.17 Kah Solomon ogkemau wame pen8wohteuh neh apinitcheh ut Israele ohkit, neanogkemoneup Davidoh 8shoh, kah naut nameheoneau, nequt pasuk8e kah napanna ta[h]hshinchage muttannonganog kussuog, kah nishwe muttannonganog kussuog, kah nequtta tahshe pasuk.
E.2.17 And Solomon numbered all the strangers that were in the land of Israel, after the numbering wherewith David his father had numbered them; and they were found an hundred and fifty thousand and three thousand and six hundred.

α.2.18 Kah weassumwaheau nesausuk tahshinchage muttannonganog kussuoh, kah wunnagehtahhamwenehheau shwosuk tahshinchage muttannonganog kussuoh, kah nishwe muttannonganog kussuoh nanawunnu[e]nuh, anakausheoncheg missinninnuh.
E.2.18 And he set threescore and ten thousand of them to be bearers of burdens, and fourscore thousand to be hewers in the mountain, and three thousand and six hundred overseers to set the people a work.

α.3.1 NEit Solomon n8che ayim wek Jehovah ut Jerusalem ut Moriahe wadchuut, uttoh adt Jehovah naehtauomp Davidoh 8shoh, ut ayeuonganit ne David quagquoshwehtogkup, ut ahhut tannuppoghog Ornan wutJebusit.
E.3.1 Then Solomon began to build the house of the LORD at Jerusalem in mount Moriah, where the Lord appeared unto David his father, in the place that David had prepared in the threshingfloor of Ornan the Jebusite.

α.3.2 Kah n8che weekitteau nahohtóeu kesukok ut nahohtoeu nepâuz, ut yaue kodtumwae ketass8tam8it.
E.3.2 And he began to build in the second day of the second month, in the fourth year of his reign.

α.3.3 Kah yeush Solomon netuhtauwaheonash, wutch ayimunat wek God, nisahteag nashpe ishquanogkodut, neane weske quttu[h]whosik, nequtta tahshinchage ishquanogkod, kah ne an8hque kishkag nesnehchag ishquanogkod.
E.3.3 Now these are the things wherein Solomon was instructed for the building of the house of God. The length by cubits after the first measure was threescore cubits, and the breadth twenty cubits.

α.3.4 Kah ahhut petutteamuk ne wohwussuhkomuk, nesahteag neaunag kishkag wetu, nesnehchag ishquanogkod, kah nesohkunkok nequt pasuk8e kah nesnehchag: kah woogquottumun ut anomut wanegik Gold.
E.3.4 And the porch that was in the front of the house, the length of it was according to the breadth of the house, twenty cubits, and the height was an hundred and twenty: and he overlaid it within with pure gold.

α.3.5 Kah mohsag wetu wutogquodtumun firuhtugquash, nish ogquodtukish wanegik Golde, kah na upponamun palmuhtugquash kah cháinsash.
E.3.5 And the greater house he cieled with fir tree, which he overlaid with fine gold, and set thereon palm trees and chains.

α.3.6 Kah ogquodtum wetu, mogkoadtikish qussukquanash wutché wunnegenit, kah ne gold, Parvaimme gold.
E.3.6 And he garnished the house with precious stones for beauty: and the gold was gold of Parvaim.

α.3.7 Kah wonk ogquodtum wetu, beamsash, postsash, kah nish sussipponkomukquash, kah ushquont gold kah kogohkswau cherubimsoh ut sussipponkkommuk.
E.3.7 He overlaid also the house, the beams, the posts, and the walls thereof, and the doors thereof, with gold; and graved cherubims on the walls.

α.3.8 Kah ayim waneetupanatamweyeu8g wetu: nesahteagk ne an8hque kishkag wetu nesnehchage ishquanogkod, kah neanukishkag nesnehchage ishquanogkod, káh wutogquodtumun wanegik Gold, nequtta tahshe pasuk8e talentsash.
E.3.8 And he made the most holy house, the length whereof was according to the breadth of the house, twenty cubits, and the breadth thereof twenty cubits: and he overlaid it with fine gold, amounting to six hundred talents.

α.3.9 Kah nean tuhkequog kenunkwhegash, napanna tahshinchagkodtash gole shekls[á]sh: kah ogquodtum gold waabe chambersash.
E.3.9 And the weight of the nails was fifty shekels of gold. And he overlaid the upper chambers with gold.

α.3.10 Kah ut anomut anue waneetupanatamweyeu8k, ayeuau nees8oh cherubimsoh, nunneukontunkane anakausuonk, kah wutogquonuh gold.
E.3.10 And in the most holy house he made two cherubims of image work, and overlaid them with gold.

α.3.11 Kah wunnuppihwhunouh cherubimsog nesnehchag ishquanogkod nesahteahettit pasuk wunnuppoh napanna tahshe isquanogkussu, missussin sussipponkomuk, kah onkatog wunnuppoh napanna tahshe isquanogkussu missuhkauau wunnuppohwhunoh onkatuk Cherub,
E.3.11 And the wings of the cherubims were twenty cubits long: one wing of the one cherub was five cubits, reaching to the wall of the house: and the other wing was likewise five cubits, reaching to the wing of the other cherub.

α.3.12 Kah pasuk wunnuppoh onkatuk cherub napanna tahshe ishquanogkussu, missussin sussipponkkomuk, kah onkatog wunnuppoh napanna tashishquânogkussu wonk mussussin onkatog Cherub wunnuppawhunit.
E.3.12 And one wing of the other cherub was five cubits, reaching to the wall of the house: and the other wing was five cubits also, joining to the wing of the other cherub.

α.3.13 Wunnuppuhwhun8uh yeug [C]erubimsog, sepageog nesnehchag isquanogkodtut: kah nag wesukkompóog wusset8oash, kah wuskesuk8ash anomiyeu.
E.3.13 The wings of these cherubims spread themselves forth twenty cubits: and they stood on their feet, and their faces were inward.

α.3.14 Kah ayim adtnikheg 8nóagk, kah purple, kah Crimson, kah wanegik hashabponagk kah ne wuttit wussukwhon cherubimsoh.
E.3.14 And he made the vail of blue, and purple, and crimson, and fine linen, and wrought cherubims thereon.

α.3.15 Wonk ayim anaquohtag wetu nesinásh pillersash, nishwinchage, kah napanna tahshe ishquanogkod nesohkunkquok, kah uppuhkuk ne woskeche naneeswe, napanna tashishquanogkod.
E.3.15 Also he made before the house two pillars of thirty and five cubits high, and the chapiter that was on the top of each of them was five cubits.

α.3.16 Kah ayim chainsash, onatuh ut oracle$ut, kah upponamunash pillarse uppuhkukquehtu kah ayim nequt pasuk88ash pomgranatsash, kah upponamunash chainsut.
E.3.16 And he made chains, as in the oracle, and put them on the heads of the pillars; and made an hundred pomegranates, and put them on the chains.

α.3.17 Kah neepattau pillersash anaquohtag Temple, pasuk muttinnonkôunit, onkatog menadcheanit, kah wutussowetamun ne muttinnukóuneiyeu Jachin, kah wuttissowetamun ne menadcheuneiyeu Boaz.
E.3.17 And he reared up the pillars before the temple, one on the right hand, and the other on the left; and called the name of that on the right hand Jachin, and the name of that on the left Boaz.

α.4.1 Nano, ayim brasse Altar, nesnehchage ishquanogkod nisahteagk, kah nesnehchag, ishquanogkod neanukkishkag, kah piogquish quanogkod ne sohkunkquok.
E.4.1 Moreover he made an altar of brass, twenty cubits the length thereof, and twenty cubits the breadth thereof, and ten cubits the height thereof.

α.4.2 Wonk ayim sabahsumwe keitoh, piogque ishquanogkod wutch wussadt onk yean wonk wussadt, papetukqui, kah napanna tashishquanogkod nesohkunkquok, kah shwinchage ishquanogkodte pemunneat weenisheau.
E.4.2 Also he made a molten sea of ten cubits from brim to brim, round in compass, and five cubits the height thereof; and a line of thirty cubits did compass it round about.

α.4.3 Kah ut agwu, oxinne nunneukontunkanog, neg ne wéinuhkunkeg: piukqussuog ut nequt ishquanogkod, wéenuhkomwog keitoh waéenu, neese pumikkompoog oxinog wunnupshanóog, wánuppashanit.
E.4.3 And under it was the similitude of oxen, which did compass it round about: ten in a cubit, compassing the sea round about. Two rows of oxen were cast, when it was cast.

α.4.4 Quenohteau nabo neese oxinit: nishuog unnuhquaeog nanummiyeu, kah nishuog unnuhquaeog wutcheksuiyeu kah nishuog unnuhquaeog sowaniyeu, kah nishuog unnuhquaeog wutchepwoiyeu: kah kehtoh wosketohtauuneau kah wame 8tamiyeumoash anomiyeu.
E.4.4 It stood upon twelve oxen, three looking toward the north, and three looking toward the west, and three looking toward the south, and three looking toward the east: and the sea was set above upon them, and all their hinder parts were inward.

α.4.5 Kah nean ukkuhpogkag pasuk menuhcheganit unnukkuhque kuppogki, kah wussadt onatuh wuttattamwaechue wus, nashpe lillee peshaónash, kah togqun nishwe muttannonganogkodtash bathsash.
E.4.5 And the thickness of it was an handbreadth, and the brim of it like the work of the brim of a cup, with flowers of lilies; and it received and held three thousand baths.

α.4.6 Kah wonk ayim piogquodtash ahhut kutchessumumukish, kah napanna tahshinash ponam unninohkôunit, kah napanna tahshinash menadcheanit, na ut kutchessittauinneat, nish maghetticheh wutche chikohtae mag8onk, na wuttit kutchissittauuneau, qut keitoh sephausuenuog wuttit kutchessumuneau.
E.4.6 He made also ten lavers, and put five on the right hand, and five on the left, to wash in them: such things as they offered for the burnt offering they washed in them; but the sea was for the priests to wash in.

α.4.7 Kah ayim piogquodtash golde wequananteganuhtugquash, n[é]anteomuk, kah nish uppondamunash temple, napanna tahshinash wuttinohkounit, kah napanna tahshinash menadcheanit.
E.4.7 And he made ten candlesticks of gold according to their form, and set them in the temple, five on the right hand, and five on the left.

α.4.8 Kah wonk ayim piogquadtash tablsash, kah upponamunash ut templeut, napanna tahshinash muttinnuhkôunit, kah napanna tahshinash menadcheanit: kah ayim nequt pasuk8ash golde wunnonganash.
E.4.8 He made also ten tables, and placed them in the temple, five on the right side, and five on the left. And he made an hundred basons of gold.

α.4.9 Kah wonk ayim wutchippineutunkan8 sephausuenúog, kah mohsag chippinneutunk, kah chippinneutungane squontash, kah kuppuhh8unash wutogquodtumunash brasse.
E.4.9 Furthermore he made the court of the priests, and the great court, and doors for the court, and overlaid the doors of them with brass.

α.4.10 Kah ponam keitoh muttinnuhkôuneiyeu wutchepwoiyeueiyeu, papiuhsuke sowaniyeu.
E.4.10 And he set the sea on the right side of the east end, over against the south.

α.4.11 Kah Huram ayim wishquash kah shovelsash, kah wunnonganash, kah Huram pakodjteo anakausuonk ne ayimauont Solomonoh, wutche wek God.
E.4.11 And Huram made the pots, and the shovels, and the basons. And Huram finished the work that he was to make for king Solomon for the house of God;

α.4.12 Neesinash pillarsash, kah pomelsash, kah uppuhkukquash nish woskeche neese pillarsut, kah neenash pepemsqunnum8ongash, unkhumunat neesinash uppuhkuk8e pummelsash, nish woskeche pillarsut.
E.4.12 To wit, the two pillars, and the pommels, and the chapiters which were on the top of the two pillars, and the two wreaths to cover the two pommels of the chapiters which were on the top of the pillars;

α.4.13 Kah yauut pasuk88ash pomgranatsash, ut neesinit pepemsqunnum8onganit, neese pomussinash pomgranatsash, na neese pepemsqunnum8onganit, onkhumunat chapiterse pummelsash, nish ohtagish pillarsut.
E.4.13 And four hundred pomegranates on the two wreaths; two rows of pomegranates on each wreath, to cover the two pommels of the chapiters which were upon the pillars.

α.4.14 Kah wonk ayimuk basesash, kah ahhut kutchessittomukish ut woskeche basesut.
E.4.14 He made also bases, and lavers made he upon the bases;

α.4.15 Pasuk keitoh, kah nabo nes8og oxenog agwe appuog.
E.4.15 One sea, and twelve oxen under it.

α.4.16 Wishquash wonk, kah shovelsash, kah weyause uhquonash, kah wame auwohteaongash, Huram 8shoh wutayimaúunápash Solomonoh ketass8toh, wutch wek Lord, wôhsepahtáe brasse.
E.4.16 The pots also, and the shovels, and the fleshhooks, and all their instruments, did Huram his father make to king Solomon for the house of the LORD of bright brass.

α.4.17 Ut Jordane mukoshquttaut, ketass8t nish 8nuppashadtauunash, ut man8nskohkit, nanashaue Succoth kah Zeredotha.
E.4.17 In the plain of Jordan did the king cast them, in the clay ground between Succoth and Zeredathah.

α.4.18 Yeu wuttin Solomon ayimun wame yeush auwohteaongash, monatash: newutche neantuhkequok brasse matta mishkom8un.
E.4.18 Thus Solomon made all these vessels in great abundance: for the weight of the brass could not be found out.

α.4.19 Kah Solomon ayim wame wishquash, nish wutch wek God, kah wonk golde altar, kah nahtitteáe petukqunnungane tablesash.
E.4.19 And Solomon made all the vessels that were for the house of God, the golden altar also, and the tables whereon the shewbread was set;

α.4.20 Wonk wequananteganuhtugquash, nashpe wul-lampsash, nish$noh chikohtauut ne woh ônag anaquohtag pahke golde oracle.
E.4.20 Moreover the candlesticks with their lamps, that they should burn after the manner before the oracle, of pure gold;

α.4.21 Kah uppeshauauash kah lampsash, kah golde tongsash, pannuppeyeue gold.
E.4.21 And the flowers, and the lamps, and the tongs, made he of gold, and that perfect gold;

α.4.22 Kah snuffersash, kah wunnongash, kah kenamóog, kah censersash, pahke goldeu8ash, kah ahhut petutteámuke wetu, anome ushquont, wutch anue wunnetupanatamwe kommukqut, kah ohkeiyeu ut temple wetuómut, goldeu8.
E.4.22 And the snuffers, and the basons, and the spoons, and the censers, of pure gold: and the entry of the house, the inner doors thereof for the most holy place, and the doors of the house of the temple, were of gold.

α.5.1 YEuin wame anakausuonk ne Solomon ayikup wutch wek Jehovah, pakodjteausu, kah Solomon petukodto wame teanteaquashinish, nish Davidoh 8shoh waneetupanatamwahteunkupash, kah silver kah g[o]ld, kah wame auwohteaongash ukkenukohtauunash wunnompak8unit ut wekit God.
E.5.1 Thus all the work that Solomon made for the house of the LORD was finished: and Solomon brought in all the things that David his father had dedicated; and the silver, and the gold, and all the instruments, put he among the treasures of the house of God.

α.5.2 Neit Solomon miyanau Israelle Eldersoh, kah wame chippan8e wabuhkuhk8utcheg, keihche wut8shinneunk ut wunnaumonat Israel, en Jerusalem, kuhkuhk8wuttauunat 8n8wae wut-arkum Jehovah, wutch wutotanat David ne Zion.
E.5.2 Then Solomon assembled the elders of Israel, and all the heads of the tribes, the chief of the fathers of the children of Israel, unto Jerusalem, to bring up the ark of the covenant of the LORD out of the city of David, which is Zion.

α.5.3 Ne waj wame Israelle wosketompaog, miyawéog en ketass8tamwut, ut mishadtupp8onganit, ne nesausuk adtahs8it nepauz.
E.5.3 Wherefore all the men of Israel assembled themselves unto the king in the feast which was in the seventh month.

α.5.4 Kah wame Israelle Eldersog peyaog, kah Levitsog nemunnumwog ark.
E.5.4 And all the elders of Israel came; and the Levites took up the ark.

α.5.5 Kah kuhkuhk8wuttóog ark, kah mukkinneae kommuk, kah wame wunnetupanatamwe auwohteaongash, nish ohtagish tabernakleut, yeush Levitsog kah sephausuenuog uppaudtauunáoash.
E.5.5 And they brought up the ark, and the tabernacle of the congregation, and all the holy vessels that were in the tabernacle, these did the priests and the Levites bring up.

α.5.6 Kah wonk ketass8t Solomon, kah wame Israelle mukkinnéonk, neg miyaécheg ut anaquohtag ark, sephausuog shepsoh kah oxenoh, neg matta woh wâogkemomukeg newutche muttaanwog.
E.5.6 Also king Solomon, and all the congregation of Israel that were assembled unto him before the ark, sacrificed sheep and oxen, which could not be told nor numbered for multitude.

α.5.7 Kah sephausuenuog petukodtóog 8n8wae wut-arkum Lord, en wutayeuonganit, en wetuóme Oracleut, en anue wunneetupanatamwe ayeuonganit, ut agwe wunnupp8whunn8wóu cherubimsog.
E.5.7 And the priests brought in the ark of the covenant of the LORD unto his place, to the oracle of the house, into the most holy place, even under the wings of the cherubims:

α.5.8 Newutche cherubimsog sepagin[á]og wunnupp8whun8uh, waábe arke aye[ú]onganit, kah cherubimsog nuhkuhkomwog ark, kah nish qunuhtukquash, waábe.
E.5.8 For the cherubims spread forth their wings over the place of the ark, and the cherubims covered the ark and the staves thereof above.

α.5.9 Kah kodtinnumwog arke qunuhtugquash ne waj uhquáe qunuhtugquash nogquodtash wutch arkut anaquohtag Oracle, qut matta poquadchit wutch nogquodtinn8wash, kah na ohteau pajeh yeu kesukok.
E.5.9 And they drew out the staves of the ark, that the ends of the staves were seen from the ark before the oracle; but they were not seen without. And there it is unto this day.

α.5.10 Wanne teag ohtano ut arkut, webe nesinash tablesash nish Moses petunkupash ut Horeb, Jehovah wann8wáhettit Israeloh wutch sohhamóhettit Egypt.
E.5.10 There was nothing in the ark save the two tables which Moses put therein at Horeb, when the LORD made a covenant with the children of Israel, when they came out of Egypt.

α.5.11 Kah n$niyeup, sephausuenúog sohhamwehettit wutch wunneetupanatamwe ayeuonganit, (newutche wame sephausuenúog neg na apitcheg, 8neetupánatamwa[h]eôog, neit matta wunashittue wowussummúwow8og.
E.5.11 And it came to pass, when the priests were come out of the holy place: (for all the priests that were present were sanctified, and did not then wait by course:

α.5.12 Kah wonk Levitsog, neg kodt8hómaenúutcheg, wame neg wadchiitcheg Asaph, Heman, Jeduthun, weeche wunnaumonáuh, kah wemat8oh, áhqhettit womponak, ohtauéhettit, cymbalsash, kah psalterisash, kah harpsash, neepóog wutchepwoiyeue altarut, kah nag weechayeumukquog nequt pas[u]k88oh, kah nesnehchagkussuoh sephausuénunnúh, puhpequohtóog nashpe monopuhpegquash.)
E.5.12 Also the Levites which were the singers, all of them of Asaph, of Heman, of Jeduthun, with their sons and their brethren, being arrayed in white linen, having cymbals and psalteries and harps, stood at the east end of the altar, and with them an hundred and twenty priests sounding with trumpets:)

α.5.13 Kah n$niyeup, puhpequaenúog kah ket8hamwáenuog, onatuh pasuk8hettit, nequttont8wahteauwahettit, wowenomónat k[á]h tabuttantamauónat Jehovah, káh mohtshont8wáhettit nashpe monopuhpegquonash, kah cymbalsash, kah wunnont8wae auwohteaongash, kah wowenomáhettit Jehovah, newutche wunneet8 newutche ummonaneteaong michemeyeu8, neit wetu numwohta matokqus, wek Jehovah.
E.5.13 It came even to pass, as the trumpeters and singers were as one, to make one sound to be heard in praising and thanking the LORD; and when they lifted up their voice with the trumpets and cymbals and instruments of musick, and praised the LORD, saying, For he is good; for his mercy endureth for ever: that then the house was filled with a cloud, even the house of the LORD;

α.5.14 Newaj sephausuenuog n8numhettit neepauun wowussummuónat, newutche mattokqs, newutche wussohsumóonk Jehovah numwohtau wekit God.
E.5.14 So that the priests could not stand to minister by reason of the cloud: for the glory of the LORD had filled the house of God.

α.6.1 NEit Solomon n8wau, Jehovah n8wop, nuttai$kuhpogke pohkenatu.
E.6.1 Then said Solomon, The LORD hath said that he would dwell in the thick darkness.

α.6.2 Qut kutayimoush kutayeuongane kommuk, kah micheme kutayeuonk.
E.6.2 But I have built an house of habitation for thee, and a place for thy dwelling for ever.

α.6.3 Kah ketass8t qunnuppenum wuskesuk, kah wunnanumau mamusse Israelle mukkinneonguh (kah wame Israelle mukkinnéonk neepóog.)
E.6.3 And the king turned his face, and blessed the whole congregation of Israel: and all the congregation of Israel stood.

α.6.4 Kah n8wau, wunnanumunach Jehovah Israel um-Manitt8moh, noh aseit nashpe wunnutcheg, ne anomp Davidoh n8shoh nashpe wutt8n, n8wop,
E.6.4 And he said, Blessed be the LORD God of Israel, who hath with his hands fulfilled that which he spake with his mouth to my father David, saying,

α.6.5 Nadteuh ne kesukok sohh8wunog nummissinninneumog wutch Egypte ohkeit, wanne nuppepenam8h keitotan, ut kenugke wame wutchippann8ongan8óut Israel, ne ut ayimunat wetu, n8wesuonk na ohtáut, asuh matta howae wosketomp wunnánauunonat Israelloh nummissinninneumoh.
E.6.5 Since the day that I brought forth my people out of the land of Egypt I chose no city among all the tribes of Israel to build an house in, that my name might be there; neither chose I any man to be a ruler over my people Israel:

α.6.6 Qut nuppepenum Jerusalem, na ohtáut n8wesuonk, kah nuppepenau David wunnánawunónat nummissinninneumoh Israeloh.
E.6.6 But I have chosen Jerusalem, that my name might be there; and have chosen David to be over my people Israel.

α.6.7 Kah ahtóp ut wuttahut David n8sh, wekuhkonat ut wesuonganit Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel.
E.6.7 Now it was in the heart of David my father to build an house for the name of the LORD God of Israel.

α.6.8 Qut Lord unnau n8shoh Davidoh: newutche kuttahut ohteau k8wekuhkonat ut n8wesuonganit, k8neseip newutche ne ohtóp ut kuttahut.
E.6.8 But the LORD said to David my father, Forasmuch as it was in thine heart to build an house for my name, thou didst well in that it was in thine heart:

α.6.9 Qut ken matta pish kutayimo wetu, qut kenaumon, noh woh sohhog wutch kusseganit, noh pish wekehteau ut n8wesuonganit.
E.6.9 Notwithstanding thou shalt not build the house; but thy son which shall come forth out of thy loins, he shall build the house for my name.

α.6.10 Newaj Jehovah pakodche usseuit yeu kutt8onk ne an8wop: newutche nunnompe waabéhtau David n8sh, kah nukquenap Israelle appuonganit, nean ukquoshóop, kah n8wekukkontam 8wesuonk Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel.
E.6.10 The LORD therefore hath performed his word that he hath spoken: for I am risen up in the room of David my father, and am set on the throne of Israel, as the LORD promised, and have built the house for the name of the LORD God of Israel.

α.6.11 Kah na nupponamun ark, ne ohtag 8n8waonk Jehovah, ne áyimwóhetteup wunnaumonuh Israel.
E.6.11 And in it have I put the ark, wherein is the covenant of the LORD, that he made with the children of Israel.

α.6.12 Kah nepau anaquohtag wut-altarum Jehovah, anaquabhettit wame Israelle mukkinneonk, kah sepáginitcháeu.
E.6.12 And he stood before the altar of the LORD in the presence of all the congregation of Israel, and spread forth his hands:

α.6.13 (Newutche Solomon ayimup brasse quésekompauonk, napanna tashishquonogkod nesahteagk, kah napanna tashishquanogkod neanukkishkag, kah nishweishquanogkod ne sohkunkquok, kah upponamunáh, ut noeu chippinneutunkanit, kah ne quesekompauin, uppésetukqussin ut ukkuttukqut ut anaquabhettit Israelle mukkinneonk, kah sepagenum wunnutchegash en kesukquieu.)
E.6.13 For Solomon had made a brasen scaffold of five cubits long, and five cubits broad, and three cubits high, and had set it in the midst of the court: and upon it he stood, and kneeled down upon his knees before all the congregation of Israel, and spread forth his hands toward heaven.

α.6.14 Kah n8wau, woi Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel wanne Manit kuttinnunk8, kesukqut asuh ohkeit, noh nanawehteunk 8n8waonk, kah kummonanum kittinneumog, neg paumushácheg anaquabean nashpe mamusse wuttahh8woash.
E.6.14 And said, O LORD God of Israel, there is no God like thee in the heaven, nor in the earth; which keepest covenant, and shewest mercy unto thy servants, that walk before thee with all their hearts:

α.6.15 Kén kenanawehteau kittinneum n8sh ne quoshomop: kah ne an8waop wutch kutt8nut, kah kutussen nashpe kenutcheg, neane yeu kesukok.
E.6.15 Thou which hast kept with thy servant David my father that which thou hast promised him; and spakest with thy mouth, and hast fulfilled it with thine hand, as it is this day.

α.6.16 Newutche yeuyeu, woi Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, nanawehteau David kittinneum n8sh, ne quoshomop, kussip, matta pish kuppanishodtauwahu wosketomp ut anaquabeh, apinneat Israelle appuonganit: qut tohneit keneechanog nunnukqussehettit, pomushaóunónat nuttinnaumatuonk, neane pomushaan anaquabeh.
E.6.16 Now therefore, O LORD God of Israel, keep with thy servant David my father that which thou hast promised him, saying, There shall not fail thee a man in my sight to sit upon the throne of Israel; yet so that thy children take heed to their way to walk in my law, as thou hast walked before me.

α.6.17 Neit yeuyeu woi Jehovah ummanitt8moh Israel, wunnomwaahteauunach, ne anomp kittinninneum David.
E.6.17 Now then, O LORD God of Israel, let thy word be verified, which thou hast spoken unto thy servant David.

α.6.18 (Qut wunnamuhkut sun God wetomau wosketompuh ut ohkeit: kussek kesuk, kah ukkesuk8m8 kesukquog, matta kuttapenuk8: uttoh en anue peásin yeu wetu ne ayim)
E.6.18 But will God in very deed dwell with men on the earth? behold, heaven and the heaven of heavens cannot contain thee; how much less this house which I have built!

α.6.19 Newutche wutt8wontash uppeantamóonk kittinneum, kah 8wehquetumóonk, woi Jehovah nummanitt8m n8tamunat mauonk kah peantamoonk, ne kittinneum an peantog ut anaquabean.
E.6.19 Have respect therefore to the prayer of thy servant, and to his supplication, O LORD my God, to hearken unto the cry and the prayer which thy servant prayeth before thee:

α.6.20 Kuskesukquash woh woshwem8it ut yeu wetuómut kesukodáeu kah nukonáeu, ut áyeuonanit ne papaume an8wáop, woh na kupponumunat k8wesuonk, n8tamunat peantamóonk, ne kittinneum ain peantog nogque en yeu ayéuonganit.
E.6.20 That thine eyes may be open upon this house day and night, upon the place whereof thou hast said that thou wouldest put thy name there; to hearken unto the prayer which thy servant prayeth toward this place.

α.6.21 Newutche n8tash 8wehquetum8onk kittinneum, kah kummissinninneumog Israel, ne woh áyimwéhettit yeu nogque in áyeuonganit: n8tash wutch kutayeuonganit, wutch kesukqut, kah n8taman ahquontash.
E.6.21 Hearken therefore unto the supplications of thy servant, and of thy people Israel, which they shall make toward this place: hear thou from thy dwelling place, even from heaven; and when thou hearest, forgive.

α.6.22 Howan matchenéheont wetahteamungoh, kah chadchekeyeuwáonk ponamauut, chadchekeyeuwáheonat; kah ne chadchekeyeuwáonk peyom8uk anaquohtag kut-altarumut ut yeu wetuómut.
E.6.22 If a man sin against his neighbour, and an oath be laid upon him to make him swear, and the oath come before thine altar in this house;

α.6.23 Neit n8tash wutch kesukqut, kah ussish, kah wussum kittinneumog, onkquatauónat mátchetou, nompenumauónat nehenwonche ummay ut nehenwonche upuhkukqut, kah sampweneheo[n]at sampweusseaenuog, aninnumauonat neaunak wussampweusseonk.
E.6.23 Then hear thou from heaven, and do, and judge thy servants, by requiting the wicked, by recompensing his way upon his own head; and by justifying the righteous, by giving him according to his righteousness.

α.6.24 Kah kummissinninneumog Israel togkomit ut anaquabenit ummatwóm8uh, newutche kummatchenehikquog, kah nag quinnuppehettit kah samp8waontamwéhettit k8wesuonk, kah peantamwehettit, kah wehquetumohettit ut anaquabean ut yeu wetuo[m]ut.
E.6.24 And if thy people Israel be put to the worse before the enemy, because they have sinned against thee; and shall return and confess thy name, and pray and make supplication before thee in this house;

α.6.25 Neit n8tash wutch kesukqut, kah ahquontamau ummatcheseongan8 kummissinninnumog Israel, kah wonk pas8h, en ohkeit ne anumauop, kah en 8sh8out.
E.6.25 Then hear thou from the heavens, and forgive the sin of thy people Israel, and bring them again unto the land which thou gavest to them and to their fathers.

α.6.26 Kesuk kuppuhhausik, kah matta sokanounun8g, newutche kummatchenehikquog: peantamwhettit yeu nogque in ayeuonganit, kah sampoantamwehettit k8wesuonk, kah quiñuppehettit wutch ummatcheseongan8out nag onkquanumweheadt.
E.6.26 When the heaven is shut up, and there is no rain, because they have sinned against thee; yet if they pray toward this place, and confess thy name, and turn from their sin, when thou dost afflict them;

α.6.27 Neit n8tash wutch kesukqut, kah ahquontamau ummatcheseongan8 kittinneumog, kah kummissinninneumog Israel; mahche kuhk8tomauadt wunne may, ne woh áahettit, kah sokanonteash en ohkeit, ne anumauadt kummissinninneumog 8tahtauonganinneaóont.
E.6.27 Then hear thou from heaven, and forgive the sin of thy servants, and of thy people Israel, when thou hast taught them the good way, wherein they should walk; and send rain upon thy land, which thou hast given unto thy people for an inheritance.

α.6.28 Mashagquok ut ohkeit eninneaonganù88k, ohp8htag, asuh mildew88k, chonsomspsu88k, asuh m8pó88k: ummatwom8oh wéenuhkongkhéttit, en ohkee keitotanahtu: ne teage kehkechiyeu8k, asuh ne teague matchinnaonganu8k.
E.6.28 If there be dearth in the land, if there be pestilence, if there be blasting, or mildew, locusts, or caterpillers; if their enemies besiege them in the cities of their land; whatsoever sore or whatsoever sickness there be:

α.6.29 Ne teagwe peantamoonk, asuh ne teague wehquetum8onk, ne woh howan ayik, asuh wame kummissinninneumog Israel, nish$noh pasuk wahteunk nehenwonche ukkéhkechesuonk kah nehenwonche wutonkquomom8onk, kah sepágenuk wunnutcheganash yeu en wetuómut.
E.6.29 Then what prayer or what supplication soever shall be made of any man, or of all thy people Israel, when every one shall know his own sore and his own grief, and shall spread forth his hands in this house:

α.6.30 Neit n8tash wutch kesukqut kutayeuonganit, kah ahquontash, kah onkquatau nishnoh wosketomp neaunak wame ummayash, noh wuttah wahteauan (newutche webe ken k8wahteoh wuttahh8óash wunnaumonáuh wosketompaog.)
E.6.30 Then hear thou from heaven thy dwelling place, and forgive, and render unto every man according unto all his ways, whose heart thou knowest; (for thou only knowest the hearts of the children of men:)

α.6.31 Onk woh nag kukqushhukquog, pomushonat kumm[à]yikontu, nisáhke pomantamwehettit ut ohkeit, ne anumauop k8shinónoh.
E.6.31 That they may fear thee, to walk in thy ways, so long as they live in the land which thou gavest unto our fathers.

α.6.32 Wonk papaume pen8wot, noh matta wadchiegk kummissinninneumog Israel, qut 8m88 nôadtit wutohtimóneat, newutche kummishe wesuonk, kah kumménuhkinnutcheg, kah kussummogkinnum8e kuhpit: nag peyahettit, kah peantamwehettit yeuut wetuómut.
E.6.32 Moreover concerning the stranger, which is not of thy people Israel, but is come from a far country for thy great name's sake, and thy mighty hand, and thy stretched out arm; if they come and pray in this house;

α.6.33 Neit n8tash wutch kesukqut, wutch kutayeuongane áyeuonganit, kah ussish neaunak wame, ne pen8wot wehquetumunkquean: onk woh wame ohke wahteauog k8wesuonk, kah woh kuhqushhukquog, ne aséhettit Israelle kummissinninneumog, kah woh wahteauog, yeu wetu ne ayim, ne ussowetamun k8wesuonganit.
E.6.33 Then hear thou from the heavens, even from thy dwelling place, and do according to all that the stranger calleth to thee for; that all people of the earth may know thy name, and fear thee, as doth thy people Israel, and may know that this house which I have built is called by thy name.

α.6.34 Kummissinninnúmwog sohhamwehettit ayeuuhkonónat ummatwom8oh, nashpe may, ne woh ann8taman; kah peantamwehettit en nogque yeu keitotanat, ne pepenamau, kah yeu wetu, ne ayim wutche k8wesuonk.
E.6.34 If thy people go out to war against their enemies by the way that thou shalt send them, and they pray unto thee toward this city which thou hast chosen, and the house which I have built for thy name;

α.6.35 Neit ken n8tash wutch kesukqut, uppeantam8ongán8, kah 8wehquetum8ongan8, kah menuhketeaush wuttinniyeuongan8.
E.6.35 Then hear thou from the heavens their prayer and their supplication, and maintain their cause.

α.6.36 Matchenehikquéan, (newutche wanne howan noh matta matcheásik) kah nag musquanumadt, kah nag mag8an en anaquabhettit ummatwom8oh, nag missinnóhteáhettit, en nóadt wutohtimóneat asuh pas8che.
E.6.36 If they sin against thee, (for there is no man which sinneth not,) and thou be angry with them, and deliver them over before their enemies, and they carry them away captives unto a land far off or near;

α.6.37 Qut onch qushkeâeahettit ut wuttahh8óut, ut ne ohkeit ottoh adt missinohteamuk, nag quinnuppéhettit, kah peantamunkquean ut en ummissinóe ohkeyeuóont n8wahettit, nummatchesemun, nuppanneussemun, numm8cheke matchesemun.
E.6.37 Yet if they bethink themselves in the land whither they are carried captive, and turn and pray unto thee in the land of their captivity, saying, We have sinned, we have done amiss, and have dealt wickedly;

α.6.38 Nag qushkehettit en kuhhogkat nashpe mamusse kuttahou, kah nashpe mamusse ukketeahogkounoh, en ummissináe ohkeyeuóut, uttoh as8wunáhettit missinuh, peantamwehettit nogque en ohkeit ne anumauop 8sh8oh, kah nogque en keitotanat ne pepenaman, kah nogque en wetuómut ne ayim ut k8wesuonganit.
E.6.38 If they return to thee with all their heart and with all their soul in the land of their captivity, whither they have carried them captives, and pray toward their land, which thou gavest unto their fathers, and toward the city which thou hast chosen, and toward the house which I have built for thy name:

α.6.39 Neit n8tash wutch kesukqut, wutch kutayeuongane ayeuonganit, uppeantam8ongan8óash, kah 8wehquetum8ongash, kah menehketeaush wuttinniyeuonk, kah ahquontamau kummissinninneumog, neg matchenehikqueaneg.
E.6.39 Then hear thou from the heavens, even from thy dwelling place, their prayer and their supplications, and maintain their cause, and forgive thy people which have sinned against thee.

α.6.40 Yeuyeu num-Manitt8m, k8wehquetumoush, kuskesukquash wôshwohtaj, kah kuhtauogash ahchúsittamóm8utch peantam8onk yeu ut ayeuonganit.
E.6.40 Now, my God, let, I beseech thee, thine eyes be open, and let thine ears be attent unto the prayer that is made in this place.

α.6.41 Newutche yeuyeu omohkish woi Lord God, en kutanwósinne ayeuonganit, ken, kah kummenuhkesue ark; kussephausueneumog woi Jehovah, hogk8m8utch wadchanittuonk, kah k8neetupanatam8mog, wekontam8m8utch en wunnet8onganit.
E.6.41 Now therefore arise, O LORD God, into thy resting place, thou, and the ark of thy strength: let thy priests, O LORD God, be clothed with salvation, and let thy saints rejoice in goodness.

α.6.42 Woi Jehovah Manit, ahque amáe quinnupinish wuskesuk sasequnadt: mehquontash ummonaneteaongash David kittinneum.
E.6.42 O LORD God, turn not away the face of thine anointed: remember the mercies of David thy servant.

α.7.1 KAh Solomon mahche peantog, n8tau n8kem8 wutch kesukqut, kah mahchuhkussum chikohtae mag8ongash, kah sephausuongash, kah wussohsumóonk Jehovah numwohteau wetuómut.
E.7.1 Now when Solomon had made an end of praying, the fire came down from heaven, and consumed the burnt offering and the sacrifices; and the glory of the LORD filled the house.

α.7.2 Kah sephausuenuoh n8nanumóog petukon wekit Jehovah, newutche wussohsumóonk Jehovah numwohteau Jehovah wekit.
E.7.2 And the priests could not enter into the house of the LORD, because the glory of the LORD had filled the LORD's house.

α.7.3 Kah wame wunnaumonuh Israel naumohettit uttoh án n8tau n8kem8uk, kah wussohsum8onk Jehovah ut wetuómut, nauwaéog, nashpe wuskesukk88ash en ohkekontu, ut wunnomskinausuut, wowussummuwáog kah woweenomáog Jehovaoh, newutche wunneetou, newutche ummonanitteaonk michemohteau.
E.7.3 And when all the children of Israel saw how the fire came down, and the glory of the LORD upon the house, they bowed themselves with their faces to the ground upon the pavement, and worshipped, and praised the LORD, saying, For he is good; for his mercy endureth for ever.

α.7.4 Neit ketass8t, kah wame missinninnuog, mag8og sephausuongash ut anaquabit Jehovah.
E.7.4 Then the king and all the people offered sacrifices before the LORD.

α.7.5 Kah ketass8t Solomon sephausuonk mag8, nesnehchage kah neese muttannongkussuog oxenog, kah nequtpasuk8e, kah nesnehchage muttannonganogkussuog shepsog, neit ketass8t kah wame missinninnúog wunneetupanatamwéhteauog wek God.
E.7.5 And king Solomon offered a sacrifice of twenty and two thousand oxen, and an hundred and twenty thousand sheep: so the king and all the people dedicated the house of God.

α.7.6 Kah sephausuenúog usseog wutannohsuongan8: kah wonk Levitsog nashpe wunnont8wáe wutauwohteaongash Jehovah, nish David ketass8t ayikupash wowenumonat Jehovah, newutche ummonàneteaongash michemohtáash; David wáeenomuadt nashpe nag wunnutchegan8oash: kah sephausuenuog wunnont8watauog monopuhpegqunash ut anaquabhettit, kah wame Israel neepóog.
E.7.6 And the priests waited on their offices: the Levites also with instruments of musick of the LORD, which David the king had made to praise the LORD, because his mercy endureth for ever, when David praised by their ministry; and the priests sounded trumpets before them, and all Israel stood.

α.7.7 Nano, Solomon wunneetupanatamwáteo nasháue chippinneutunk, ne anaquohtag wek Jehovah: newutche na wuttit magun chikohtae mag8ongash, kah wunnohteáe mag8ongane wees; newutche brasse altar ne Solomon ayeuompoh, matta tapenum8 attumunumunat, chikohtae mag8ongash, kah meetsue mag8ongash kah wees.
E.7.7 Moreover Solomon hallowed the middle of the court that was before the house of the LORD: for there he offered burnt offerings, and the fat of the peace offerings, because the brasen altar which Solomon had made was not able to receive the burnt offerings, and the meat offerings, and the fat.

α.7.8 Kah wonk ne ahquompak nesausuk tahshikquinne mishadtupp8, kah wame weeche Israel, ahche mishe mukkinneonk, wutch ahhut petutteamuk Hamath, wehque Egypte sepuut.
E.7.8 Also at the same time Solomon kept the feast seven days, and all Israel with him, a very great congregation, from the entering in of Hamath unto the river of Egypt.

α.7.9 Kah shwosuk adtahshikquinogkok, ayimwog wunnetupanatamwe moéonk: newutche nanawehteauog wunneetupanatamwahteóonk altar, nesausuk tahshikquinne, kah mishadtupp8onk nesausuk tahshikquinne.
E.7.9 And in the eighth day they made a solemn assembly: for they kept the dedication of the altar seven days, and the feast seven days.

α.7.10 Kah nesnehchadtequnhog kah nish, nesausuk adtahs8it nepauz, moncheaheau missinninnúh en wekuómut, wekontamwog, kah muskouánatamwúhteahâog wutch wanegig ne nahtinont Davidoh kah Solomonoh, kah Israeloh ummissinninneumoh.
E.7.10 And on the three and twentieth day of the seventh month he sent the people away into their tents, glad and merry in heart for the goodness that the LORD had shewed unto David, and to Solomon, and to Israel his people.

α.7.11 Yeu wuttin Solomon kesteauun wek Jehovah, kah ketass8t wek, kah wame nish paom8ukish Solomon wuttahhut ayimunat ut wekit Jehovah, kah ut nehenwonche wekit, 8niyeue ussen.
E.7.11 Thus Solomon finished the house of the LORD, and the king's house: and all that came into Solomon's heart to make in the house of the LORD, and in his own house, he prosperously effected.

α.7.12 Kah Jehovah naéhtauau Solomonoh nukkonáeu, kah wuttinuh, nunn8tam kuppeantamóonk, kah yeu ayeuonk nuppepènamwaushun nuhhog, wutche sephausúkomuk.
E.7.12 And the LORD appeared to Solomon by night, and said unto him, I have heard thy prayer, and have chosen this place to myself for an house of sacrifice.

α.7.13 Yânunnúmon kesuk matta sokanon8ut, asuh ann8nog chansompsog ummatchteauunnaóont ohke; asuh enninneáonk ann8nog, en nummissinninnúmut.
E.7.13 If I shut up heaven that there be no rain, or if I command the locusts to devour the land, or if I send pestilence among my people;

α.7.14 Nummissinninnúmog, neg as8wesitcheg nashpe n8wesuonk, nag hohpaheáhettit wuhhogkauh, kah peantamwehettit, kah natinnehamohettit nuskesuk, kah qushkehettit wutch ummatche mayeuwóut: neit pish nunn8tam wutch kesukqut, kah pish nutahquontam ummatcheseongan8, kah pish nunneetskehteo wutohkéyeu.
E.7.14 If my people, which are called by my name, shall humble themselves, and pray, and seek my face, and turn from their wicked ways; then will I hear from heaven, and will forgive their sin, and will heal their land.

α.7.15 Yeuyeu nuskesukquash pish woshwem8ash, kah nehtauogash pish ahchúsittam8m8ash peantamóonk yeuut ayeuonganit.
E.7.15 Now mine eyes shall be open, and mine ears attent unto the prayer that is made in this place.

α.7.16 New[ú]tche yeuyeu nuppepenam, kah n8neetupanatamwahteo yeu wetu, n8wesuonk na woh michemohtea, kah nuskesukquash kah nuttah na pish nagwutteohteau.
E.7.16 For now have I chosen and sanctified this house, that my name may be there for ever: and mine eyes and mine heart shall be there perpetually.

α.7.17 Kah papaume ken, pomush[â]an anaquabeh neane David k8sh pomushop: kah ussean wame neanann8nun, kah kuhkinneaséan nukkuhk8waongash kah nosittum8ongash.
E.7.17 And as for thee, if thou wilt walk before me, as David thy father walked, and do according to all that I have commanded thee, and shalt observe my statutes and my judgments;

α.7.18 Neit pish nummenuhkehteoh ketass8tamwe appuonk, neane wunn8waogkup David k8sh, nussip, matta pish pannushano w[ò]sketomp wutche ken wunnánawunnúaennúunneat ut Israel.
E.7.18 Then will I stablish the throne of thy kingdom, according as I have covenanted with David thy father, saying, There shall not fail thee a man to be ruler in Israel.

α.7.19 Qut qushkeóg, kah nukkodtumóg nukkuhk8waongash, kah nutann8team8ongash nish ponamonish anaquabeóg; kah moncheóg kah wuttinneumuhkauóg kah wowussumóg onkatogig manitt8og:
E.7.19 But if ye turn away, and forsake my statutes and my commandments, which I have set before you, and shall go and serve other gods, and worship them;

α.7.20 Neit pish nukkodtahchabpúhkonóog wutch nutohkit, ne anúmauog, kah yeu wetu ne wunneetupanatamwáhteau, wutche n8wesuonk, pish nuppogketamun wutch anaquabeh, kah pish núnnukkummuwóhtauun, kah nutóiontogkodtauwahteauun ut kenugke wame wutohtimóneat.
E.7.20 Then will I pluck them up by the roots out of my land which I have given them; and this house, which I have sanctified for my name, will I cast out of my sight, and will make it to be a proverb and a byword among all nations.

α.7.21 Kah yeu wetu, ne mahsh[à]numukquok, pish wutchepshàadtamun nish$noh howan noh pamwushâadtog, newaj pish n8wadt, tohwutch yeu unnéhteunk Jehovah yeu ohkée, kah yeu wetu?
E.7.21 And this house, which is high, shall be an astonishment to every one that passeth by it; so that he shall say, Why hath the LORD done thus unto this land, and unto this house?

α.7.22 Kah pish en namp8hamwontamun, newutche nukkonáog Jehovahoh um-Manitt8m8uh 8sh8oh, noh sohh8wunont wutch Egypte ohkeit, kah menuhkenáog onkatogeh manitt8h, kah wowussumáog, kah 8tinninneumuhkauóuh, newaj nukúhkauwáheont wame yeu machuk.
E.7.22 And it shall be answered, Because they forsook the LORD God of their fathers, which brought them forth out of the land of Egypt, and laid hold on other gods, and worshipped them, and served them: therefore hath he brought all this evil upon them.

α.8.1 KAh nniyeup (mahche nesnechage kodtum8k ne adt kesteunk Solomon, wek Jehovah, kah nehenwonche wek.)
E.8.1 And it came to pass at the end of twenty years, wherein Solomon had built the house of the LORD, and his own house,

α.8.2 Keitotanash nish Huram nompenumauonche Solomonoh: Solomon nish wutayimunash, kah nó wutáyeuwaheon wunnaumonuh Israel.
E.8.2 That the cities which Huram had restored to Solomon, Solomon built them, and caused the children of Israel to dwell there.

α.8.3 Kah Solomon au Hamoth$Zobah, kah wússohkomun.
E.8.3 And Solomon went to Hamathzobah, and prevailed against it.

α.8.4 Kah ayim Tadmor ut touohkomukqut, kah wame ogqunniikkomukque keitotanash, nish ayikish ut Hamath.
E.8.4 And he built Tadmor in the wilderness, and all the store cities, which he built in Hamath.

α.8.5 Kah wonk ayim Bethhoron, koduhkôageiyeu, kah Bethhoron 8muhkoiageiyeu, pummeneutausu otanash, nashpe pummeneutungash, ushquontamash, kah bársash.
E.8.5 Also he built Bethhoron the upper, and Bethhoron the nether, fenced cities, with walls, gates, and bars;

α.8.6 Kah Baalath, kah wame wadchanumwe keitotanash, nish Solomon ohtunk, kah wame chariotse keitotanash, kah Horsesoh na8mukqutcheg ukkeitotanash, kah wamu ne Solomon kodtantog ayimunat ut Jerusalem, kah ut Lebanon, kah papannuppe wame wunnanawunumwe ohkeit.
E.8.6 And Baalath, and all the store cities that Solomon had, and all the chariot cities, and the cities of the horsemen, and all that Solomon desired to build in Jerusalem, and in Lebanon, and throughout all the land of his dominion.

α.8.7 Papaume wame missinninnuog neg sequttawhutcheg wut-Hittitsog, kah wut$Amoritsog, kah up-Perizitsog, kah wut-Hivitsog, kah wutJebusitsog, neg matta wadchiegig Israel.
E.8.7 As for all the people that were left of the Hittites, and the Amorites, and the Perizzites, and the Hivites, and the Jebusites, which were not of Israel,

α.8.8 Qut wunneechan8oh, neg asquttawhutcheg asuhkaue ut ohkeit, neh wunnaumonuh Israel matta mohtupanahettegeh: neh Solomon wutompweteaheuh pajeh yeu kesukok.
E.8.8 But of their children, who were left after them in the land, whom the children of Israel consumed not, them did Solomon make to pay tribute until this day.

α.8.9 Qut wutch wunnaumonat Israel, Solomon matta 8tinninneumehteaunuh wutche wutanakausuonk, qut nag ayeuhteaenuog, 8kehchemugquompominneuh, wut$chariotse Mugq[ú]ompomoh, kah horsesoh na8mukqutcheg.
E.8.9 But of the children of Israel did Solomon make no servants for his work; but they were men of war, and chief of his captains, and captains of his chariots and horsemen.

α.8.10 Kah yeug megonneyeuutcheg wutannohsueneumoh ketass8t Solomon, neese pasuk88og kah napanna tahshinchag, neg nánawunoncheg missinninnuh.
E.8.10 And these were the chief of king Solomon's officers, even two hundred and fifty, that bare rule over the people.

α.8.11 Kah Solomon kuhkuhk8unau wuttaunoh Pharoh wutch wutotanat David, en wetuomut ne ayimauont, newutche n8wau, nummittamwos matta pish ayéeu wekit David Israelle ketass8t, newutche ayeuongash wunneetupanat[à]mweyeu8ash uttoh adt peyaum8uk wut-Arkum Jehovah.
E.8.11 And Solomon brought up the daughter of Pharaoh out of the city of David unto the house that he had built for her: for he said, My wife shall not dwell in the house of David king of Israel, because the places are holy, whereunto the ark of the LORD hath come.

α.8.12 Neit Solomon mag8 chikohtae sephausuongash en Jehovahut, ut wut-Altarumut Jehovah, ne ayik ut anaquohtag porch.
E.8.12 Then Solomon offered burnt offerings unto the LORD on the altar of the LORD, which he had built before the porch,

α.8.13 Kukquttum8e tahshe asekesukokish, maguk neaunak wuttinnaumatuonk Moses, Sasaboth$dayeu, kay ut wuske nepauzsahtu, kah ut mishe mishadtupp8onganehtu, nishwudt nish$noh podtumm8, mat seanne petukquenongane mishadtupp8onkanit, kah wekse mishadtupp8onkanit, kah Tabernaklee mishadtupp8onganit.
E.8.13 Even after a certain rate every day, offering according to the commandment of Moses, on the sabbaths, and on the new moons, and on the solemn feasts, three times in the year, even in the feast of unleavened bread, and in the feast of weeks, and in the feast of tabernacles.

α.8.14 Kah kuhquttum, neaunak 8nohtóonk 8shoh Davidoh, sephausuenue 8nappuongash, ut 8tinninneumuhkausuongan8óut, kah Levitsog ut ummeechumuhkonaonganit, woweenomuwonat, kah wuttinneumuhkausinneat ut anaquabhettit sephausuenuog, neane nishnoh kesukodtae wuttiñeumuka[u]simuk: kah wonk nanausquontamenuog ut 8nappuongan8out ut nish$noh asquontamut, newutche ne wuttinne Manittowomp David ann8teamwunneah.
E.8.14 And he appointed, according to the order of David his father, the courses of the priests to their service, and the Levites to their charges, to praise and minister before the priests, as the duty of every day required: the porters also by their courses at every gate: for so had David the man of God commanded.

α.8.15 Kah nag matta nukkodtum8og wutann8team8onk ketass8t, neanann8nont sephausuenuog, kah Levitsog, papume ne teaguas, asuh papaume nompak8unash.
E.8.15 And they departed not from the commandment of the king unto the priests and Levites concerning any matter, or concerning the treasures.

α.8.16 Kah wame wutanakausuonk Solomon, quagquoshwunumun wutche ne kesukok wanahtauhettit quenohtag wetu J[e]hovah, kah nô pajeh kestauunat: neit wek God pannuppeteauun.
E.8.16 Now all the work of Solomon was prepared unto the day of the foundation of the house of the LORD, and until it was finished. So the house of the LORD was perfected.

α.8.17 Neit Solomon au Ezion$Geber, kah en Elith ut kishke ketahhannit ut Edome ohkit.
E.8.17 Then went Solomon to Eziongeber, and to Eloth, at the sea side in the land of Edom.

α.8.18 Kah Huram na en negonshhuau kuht8nogwash nashpe wunnutchegan8out wuttinneumoh, kah wuttinneumuneunk neg wahteunkig keitoh, kah nag weechaauog wuttinneumoh Solomon en Ophir, kah na 8tinnumuneau yauut pasuk8e, kah napanna tahshinchage golde talentsash, kah uppaudtauunaoash ketass8toh Solomonoh.
E.8.18 And Huram sent him by the hands of his servants ships, and servants that had knowledge of the sea; and they went with the servants of Solomon to Ophir, and took thence four hundred and fifty talents of gold, and brought them to king Solomon.

α.9.1 KAh Shebae sonkusq n8tog 8wenomaonk Solomon peyau, qutcheheonat Solomonoh nashpe siogke nat8tomwehteaongash, ut Jerusalem, nashpe muttaán8e chipwushaog, kah Camelsog neg nayeutogig, spicesash kah Gold m8cheke, kah magôadtikish qussukquanash: kah paohonont Solomonoh, ukkeket8kauau papaume wame ne wuttahhut.
E.9.1 And when the queen of Sheba heard of the fame of Solomon, she came to prove Solomon with hard questions at Jerusalem, with a very great company, and camels that bare spices, and gold in abundance, and precious stones: and when she was come to Solomon, she communed with him of all that was in her heart.

α.9.2 Kah Solomon wuttinnonash wame wunnat8tomwehteaongash, kah monteag adtuhtôsin8 wutch Solomon ne matta anunk.
E.9.2 And Solomon told her all her questions: and there was nothing hid from Solomon which he told her not.

α.9.3 Kah Shebae sonksq nag* 8wáantamóonk Solomon kah wetu ne kesteunk.
E.9.3 And when the queen of Sheba had seen the wisdom of Solomon, and the house that he had built,

α.9.4 Kah meetsuonk ut wuttableumut, kah ne apinit wuttinneumoh: kah nean wuttinneumit wuttinneumoh, kah wuthogk8un8oash, & wonk 8tattamwaitch kôunnumunutcheg, kah wuthogk8n8ash, kah ukkuhkuhqueonk nean kuhkuhqueit en wekit Jehovah, wanne wonk wunnashaonganeu.
E.9.4 And the meat of his table, and the sitting of his servants, and the attendance of his ministers, and their apparel; his cupbearers also, and their apparel; and his ascent by which he went up into the house of the LORD; there was no more spirit in her.

α.9.5 Kah unnau ketass8tóh, wunnamuhkuteyeu8 unnehtunkquodt ne n8tam ut nehenwonche nutohkit papaume kutusseong[â]sh, kah papaume k8waantamóonk.
E.9.5 And she said to the king, It was a true report which I heard in mine own land of thine acts, and of thy wisdom:

α.9.6 Qut matta n8namptam8 ukkutt8ongan8oash, nó pajeh nuppeyonat, kah nuskesukqutash wunnaumun, kah kusseh pohshe mátanunkquok k8wáantamoonk matta nuttitteaan, newutche kummishteoh wowenodtuonk ne n8tamomp.
E.9.6 Howbeit I believed not their words, until I came, and mine eyes had seen it: and, behold, the one half of the greatness of thy wisdom was not told me: for thou exceedest the fame that I heard.

α.9.7 Wunniyeuog k8wosketompaog, kah wunniyeuog yeug kuttinneumog, neg nagwutteagkompauitcheg anaquabean, kah n8togig k8waantam8onk.
E.9.7 Happy are thy men, and happy are these thy servants, which stand continually before thee, and hear thy wisdom.

α.9.8 Wunnanumunach Jehovah kum$Manitt8m, noh tapeneunkquean, kupponukqunat yeu appuonganit, ketass8tam8ineat wutche Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, newutche kum-Manitt8m womonau Israeloh nah um̃enuhkeheonat micheme, newaje naut kutass8tam̃ukkônukqueā, ussēat wussittūóonk & sampwagk
E.9.8 Blessed be the LORD thy God, which delighted in thee to set thee on his throne, to be king for the LORD thy God: because thy God loved Israel, to establish them for ever, therefore made he thee king over them, to do judgment and justice.

α.9.9 Kah aninnumauau ketass8toh nequt pasuk8e kah nesnehchage golde talentsash, kah spicash monatash, kah magôadtikish qussukquanash, kah ne matta nano spicash, nish Shebae sonksq anúmauonche ketass8toh Solomonoh.
E.9.9 And she gave the king an hundred and twenty talents of gold, and of spices great abundance, and precious stones: neither was there any such spice as the queen of Sheba gave king Solomon.

α.9.10 Kah wonk wuttinneumoh Huram, kah wuttinneumoh Solomon, neg paudtunkig gold wutch Ophir, paudtóog almuhtukquash, kah magôadtikish qussukquanash.
E.9.10 And the servants also of Huram, and the servants of Solomon, which brought gold from Ophir, brought algum trees and precious stones.

α.9.11 Kah ketass8t nashpe almuhtukquash wut-stairsuhkónash ut wekit Jehovah, kah ut ketass8t wekit, kah harpsash, kah ps[á]lterisash wutche ket8hamwaenúog, kah matta wonk nein negonne naum8unah ut ohkeit Judah.
E.9.11 And the king made of the algum trees terraces to the house of the LORD, and to the king's palace, and harps and psalteries for singers: and there were none such seen before in the land of Judah.

α.9.12 Kah ketass8t Solomon aninnumauau Shebae sonksquau wame ukkodtanatam8onk, uttoh an wehquetuk, chaubok ne paudtauont ketass8toh: neit qushkeu, kah monchu nehenwonche wutohkeit, nagum kah wuttinneumoh.
E.9.12 And king Solomon gave to the queen of Sheba all her desire, whatsoever she asked, beside that which she had brought unto the king. So she turned, and went away to her own land, she and her servants.

α.9.13 Kah nean tuhkequok gold, ne paógqut Solomon nequt kodtumwáe, ne nequtta tahshe pasuk8e, kah nequtta tahshinchage, kah nequtta tahshe golde talentsash.
E.9.13 Now the weight of gold that came to Solomon in one year was six hundred and threescore and six talents of gold;

α.9.14 Chaubok ne adtoáenuog kah anaqushaenúog paudtauéhettit, kah wame Arabiáe ketass8tamwog, kah wutohtimóinne nanauwunnuenúog, paudtauáog gold Solomonoh.
E.9.14 Beside that which chapmen and merchants brought. And all the kings of Arabia and governors of the country brought gold and silver to Solomon.

α.9.15 Kah ketass8t Solomon ayim nesepasuk8e sukquehthamwe golde targetsash, nequtta tahshe pasuk88ash sukquehthamwe golde shekelsash, pasukqunnú8 target.
E.9.15 And king Solomon made two hundred targets of beaten gold: six hundred shekels of beaten gold went to one target.

α.9.16 Kah nishwudt pasuk88ash sugquehthamwe golde ogqunnegash, nishwudt pasuk88ash golde shekelsash pasukqunnú8 ogqunneg, kah ketass8t nash upponamunash ut Lebanone tauohkomukque wetuómut.
E.9.16 And three hundred shields made he of beaten gold: three hundred shekels of gold went to one shield. And the king put them in the house of the forest of Lebanon.

α.9.17 Wonk ketass8t ayim Ivorie mishe appuonk, kah wutogquodtumun wanegik gold.
E.9.17 Moreover the king made a great throne of ivory, and overlaid it with pure gold.

α.9.18 Kah nequtta tashanéhtuonganu8 en appuonganit, nashpe golde quenannéhtuonk, nish manuhkohtagish appuonganit: kah aninnuhk8unash, aéetaue ne ahapimuk, kah nesuog qunnónúog, kehchekompóog, aninúhk8unit.
E.9.18 And there were six steps to the throne, with a footstool of gold, which were fastened to the throne, and stays on each side of the sitting place, and two lions standing by the stays:

α.9.19 Kah nabo nees8og qunnon8og na wunneepauunneau aéetaue, ut nequtta adtahshánittuonganogkok: matta neanteausin8 woh toh ut ass8tam8onganit.
E.9.19 And twelve lions stood there on the one side and on the other upon the six steps. There was not the like made in any kingdom.

α.9.20 Kah wame wuttattamwaitchuash ketass8t Solomon goldeu8ash, kah wame auwohteaongash ut Lebanone touohkomukque wetuómut pahke goldeu8ash: wanne silvereu8ash, matta toh ogquantam8un, pâmontog Solomon.
E.9.20 And all the drinking vessels of king Solomon were of gold, and all the vessels of the house of the forest of Lebanon were of pure gold: none were of silver; it was not any thing accounted of in the days of Solomon.

α.9.21 Newutche ketass8t kuht8nogquash aum8ash Tarshish, weche wuttinneumoh Huram: nishnoh nishwe kodtumwáe pasukqut peyaum8ash kuht8nogquash wutch Tarshish, paudtóog gold kah silver, Ivory, kah Apes, kah Peacocks.
E.9.21 For the king's ships went to Tarshish with the servants of Huram: every three years once came the ships of Tarshish bringing gold, and silver, ivory, and apes, and peacocks.

α.9.22 Kah ketass8t Solomon aneúauau wame muttaohke ketass8tamwoh, ut weenauwetuonganit, kah waantam8onganit.
E.9.22 And king Solomon passed all the kings of the earth in riches and wisdom.

α.9.23 Kah wame ketass8tamwog ohkeit, natinnehamwog wuttinnuhquábuonk Solomon n8tamunat 8waantamóonk, ne God ponamauont wuttahut.
E.9.23 And all the kings of the earth sought the presence of Solomon, to hear his wisdom, that God had put in his heart.

α.9.24 Kah nag paudtóog nish$noh ummag8onk, silvere wishquash, kah golde wishquash, kah hogk8ongash, kenauwameongash, kah spicash, horsesog kah mulsog, kuhquttumwe âadtehteáonk nish$noh kodtumm8.
E.9.24 And they brought every man his present, vessels of silver, and vessels of gold, and raiment, harness, and spices, horses, and mules, a rate year by year.

α.9.25 Kah Solomon ohtóou yauut pasuk88ash horsese stalsash, kah chariotsash, kah nabo neese muttannonganogkussuog horsesoh na8mukqutcheg, neh pononcheh ut chariotte keitotanahtu, kah weeche ketass8t ut Jerusalem.
E.9.25 And Solomon had four thousand stalls for horses and chariots, and twelve thousand horsemen; whom he bestowed in the chariot cities, and with the king at Jerusalem.

α.9.26 Kah piahtimau wame ketass8tamwoh wutch sepuut, wehque Philistianse ohkeit, kah wehque Egypte sussippoiyeuut.
E.9.26 And he reigned over all the kings from the river even unto the land of the Philistines, and to the border of Egypt.

α.9.27 Kah ketass8t ogquehteau silver qussukquanit, kah Cedaruhtugquash ogquehteau Sycamoruhtugqut, nish monakish ut mukoshqutuhtu.
E.9.27 And the king made silver in Jerusalem as stones, and cedar trees made he as the sycomore trees that are in the low plains in abundance.

α.9.28 Kah paudtauáog Solomonoh, horsesoh wutch Egypt, kah wutch wame ohkeit.
E.9.28 And they brought unto Solomon horses out of Egypt, and out of all lands.

α.9.29 Kah onkatogish wutusseongash Solomon, negonneyeu8gish kah maumachishú8gish, sunnummatta wussukwhosinash ut 8sukuhwhonganit Nathan quoshodtumwaen, kah ut ukquoshodtum8ongonit Ahijah wus-Shilonit, kah ut wunnaumoonganit Iddo naumwaenin, ayeuuhkonittue Jeroboam wunnaumonuh Nebat.
E.9.29 Now the rest of the acts of Solomon, first and last, are they not written in the book of Nathan the prophet, and in the prophecy of Ahijah the Shilonite, and in the visions of Iddo the seer against Jeroboam the son of Nebat?

α.9.30 Kah Solomon ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem, ut wame Israel, yauunchage kodtumwae.
E.9.30 And Solomon reigned in Jerusalem over all Israel forty years.

α.9.31 Kah Solomon weesequom8mau 8shoh, kah posekinau ukkeitotanat 8shoh Davidoh, kah Rehoboamoh wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tam8mukquoh.
E.9.31 And Solomon slept with his fathers, and he was buried in the city of David his father: and Rehoboam his son reigned in his stead.

α.10.1 KAh Rehoboam au Shechem, newutche wame Israel peyaog Shechem ukketass8tamuhkonaóont.
E.10.1 And Rehoboam went to Shechem: for to Shechem were all Israel come to make him king.

α.10.2 Kah n$niyeup, Jeroboam wunnaumonuh Nebat (noh apit Egypt, uttoh ashph8op wutch anaquabit Solomon ketass8t) n8tog, Jeroboam qushkeu wutch Egypt.
E.10.2 And it came to pass, when Jeroboam the son of Nebat, who was in Egypt, whither he fled from the presence of Solomon the king, heard it, that Jeroboam returned out of Egypt.

α.10.3 Kah ann8team8og kah 8wehkomóuh, neit Jeroboam kah wame Israel peyaog, kah ken8naog Rehoboamoh, n8waog,
E.10.3 And they sent and called him. So Jeroboam and all Israel came and spake to Rehoboam, saying,

α.10.4 K8sh, unkquéheop neyoakumùnonoh, yowutche nompunkitteaush ogguhse, nutunkque wuttiñeumuhkauwaonganun k8sh, kah wuttuhkéque yoakumoh, ne ponamunkqueog, kah k8tinninneumuhkauunumun.
E.10.4 Thy father made our yoke grievous: now therefore ease thou somewhat the grievous servitude of thy father, and his heavy yoke that he put upon us, and we will serve thee.

α.10.5 Kah nah wuttinuh, wonk peyaausek, mahche nishikquinogkok, kah missinninnúog moncheog.
E.10.5 And he said unto them, Come again unto me after three days. And the people departed.

α.10.6 Kah ketass8t Rehoboam ken8nau kehchisoh, neh neepauunitcheh anaquabenit Solomonoh 8shoh, ash pâmontog, n8wau, toh kittin ken8simw8 namp8hamauónat yeug missinninn[u]og?
E.10.6 And king Rehoboam took counsel with the old men that had stood before Solomon his father while he yet lived, saying, What counsel give ye me to return answer to this people?

α.10.7 Kah ukken8nóuh, n8waog, womonadt yeug missinninnúog, kah wussikkitteaheadt, kah wunne kén8nadt, nag pish micheme kittinneumog.
E.10.7 And they spake unto him, saying, If thou be kind to this people, and please them, and speak good words to them, they will be thy servants for ever.

α.10.8 Qut nukkodtum ken8nittuonk, ne kechisog án ken8nahettit: kah ken8nau wuskenúh, neh weecheteumukqutcheh, neh nepauunitcheh, anaquabit.
E.10.8 But he forsook the counsel which the old men gave him, and took counsel with the young men that were brought up with him, that stood before him.

α.10.9 Kah nah wuttinuh, toh kittin ken8s8wam8, onk woh kenamp8hamauómun yeug missinninnúog, neg kôn8sitcheg n8waog, ogguhse nunkeh, ne yoak k8sh ponamunkqueogkup.
E.10.9 And he said unto them, What advice give ye that we may return answer to this people, which have spoken to me, saying, Ease somewhat the yoke that thy father did put upon us?

α.10.10 Kah wuskenúog neh weechetumukqutcheh, ukken8nóuh, n8waog, yeu woh kittin namp8hamauon missinninnúog, neg kôn8nukqueaneg, n8waog, k8sh tuhkekqheóp keyoakumunónuh, qut ken ogguhse nunkeáteainnean; yeu woh nag kittinnóneau, nummattassonitch pish ánue kuhpogki, onk ne n8sh wusseganit.
E.10.10 And the young men that were brought up with him spake unto him, saying, Thus shalt thou answer the people that spake unto thee, saying, Thy father made our yoke heavy, but make thou it somewhat lighter for us; thus shalt thou say unto them, My little finger shall be thicker than my father's loins.

α.10.11 Newutche n8sh takequeteunkqueóg keyoakumóuh; nen kukk8tnehteauunumw8 keyoakumw8: n8sh kussasametóhuk8óp whipsash, qut nen scorpionsog.
E.10.11 For whereas my father put a heavy yoke upon you, I will put more to your yoke: my father chastised you with whips, but I will chastise you with scorpions.

α.10.12 Neit Jeroboam kah wame missinninnuog peyaonáog Rehoboamoh nashikquinogok, ne ánont ketass8t, n8wop, peyaausek wonk nashikquinogkok.
E.10.12 So Jeroboam and all the people came to Rehoboam on the third day, as the king bade, saying, Come again to me on the third day.

α.10.13 Kah ketass8t nah ummusquanittamwe namp8hamauoh, kah ketass8t Rehoboam nukkodtum kehchisog ukken8s8waongan8.
E.10.13 And the king answered them roughly; and king Rehoboam forsook the counsel of the old men,

α.10.14 Kah nag wuttinnamp8hamauoh neaunak ukken8s8waongan8 wuskenuog, n8wau, n8sh kutt[ù]hkequéhteunk8óp keyoakum8uh, qut nen nukk8tneh, n8sh kussasamatuhhuk8 whipsash, qut nen scorpionsog.
E.10.14 And answered them after the advice of the young men, saying, My father made your yoke heavy, but I will add thereto: my father chastised you with whips, but I will chastise you with scorpions.

α.10.15 Neit ketass8t matta kuhkehtauóou missinninnúh, newutche ne 8m88 Godut, onk woh Jehovah ussenat wuttinn8waonk ne án8wop, nashpe wunnutcheg Ahijah wus-Shilonit, en Jeroboamut wunnaumonuh Nebat.
E.10.15 So the king hearkened not unto the people: for the cause was of God, that the LORD might perform his word, which he spake by the hand of Ahijah the Shilonite to Jeroboam the son of Nebat.

α.10.16 Kah wame Israel namohettit matta ketass8t ukkeiketauoh, namp8hamauáog ketass8toh n8waog, teaguas kutchippôiyeumun ut David? kah matta k8tohtoonganeúmun[na]t wunnaumonat Jesse, nishnoh pasuk en wekit woi Israel: kah yeuyeu David nanawehteaush nehenwonche kek: neit wame Israel auog wekuóont.
E.10.16 And when all Israel saw that the king would not hearken unto them, the people answered the king, saying, What portion have we in David?  and we have none inheritance in the son of Jesse: every man to your tents, O Israel: and now, David, see to thine own house. So all Israel went to their tents.

α.10.17 Qut yeug wunnaumonuh Israel, apitcheg Judae keitotanahtu, Rehoboam nah uppiahtimuh.
E.10.17 But as for the children of Israel that dwelt in the cities of Judah, Rehoboam reigned over them.

α.10.18 Neit Rehoboam ann8nau Adoramoh, noh nanawunuk ompweteaonk, kah wunnaumonuh Israel, ukqussukquantahwhóuh, ne waj nuppuk: qut ketass8t Rehoboam kenuppe kuhkuhqueu wut-chariotumut, ushpuhh8wonat Jerusalem.
E.10.18 Then king Rehoboam sent Hadoram that was over the tribute; and the children of Israel stoned him with stones, that he died. But king Rehoboam made speed to get him up to his chariot, to flee to Jerusalem.

α.10.19 Kah Israel ayeuuhkonittue cheketamwog wek David pajeh yeu kesukok.
E.10.19 And Israel rebelled against the house of David unto this day.

α.11.1 KAh Rehoboam paont Jerusalem, miyanau, wutch wekit Judah, kah Benjamin, nequt pasuk8e, kah shwosuk tahshinchage muttannonganog kussuoh, pepenauutcheg, neg ayeuwéhteaenuitcheg, ayeuhkononat Israel, woh wonk uppaudtauunat wutass8tamóonk Rehoboam.
E.11.1 And when Rehoboam was come to Jerusalem, he gathered of the house of Judah and Benjamin an hundred and fourscore thousand chosen men, which were warriors, to fight against Israel, that he might bring the kingdom again to Rehoboam.

α.11.2 Qut wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Shemajah Manittowomp, n8wau,
E.11.2 But the word of the LORD came to Shemaiah the man of God, saying,

α.11.3 Ken8s Rehoboam wunnaumonuh Solomon ketass8t ut Judah, kah wame Israel ut Judah kah Benjamin, n8wash.
E.11.3 Speak unto Rehoboam the son of Solomon, king of Judah, and to all Israel in Judah and Benjamin, saying,

α.11.4 Yeu wussin Jehovah matta pish kukkuhk8mw8, asuh kutayeuuhkonomw8 keematt8oog: qushkek nish$noh wosketomp en wekit newutche yeu nutussen: kah nag n8swehtamwog wutinn8waongash Jehovah kah qushkeog wutch n8swetahwhonat Jeroboam.
E.11.4 Thus saith the LORD, Ye shall not go up, nor fight against your brethren: return every man to his house: for this thing is done of me. And they obeyed the words of the LORD, and returned from going against Jeroboam.

α.11.5 Kah Rehoboam ayeu Jerusalem, kah ayim pummeneutausue keitotanash ut Judah.
E.11.5 And Rehoboam dwelt in Jerusalem, and built cities for defence in Judah.

α.11.6 Ayim Bethlehem, kah Etam, kah Tekoa.
E.11.6 He built even Bethlehem, and Etam, and Tekoa,

α.11.7 Kah Bethzur, kah Shoco, kah Adullam.
E.11.7 And Bethzur, and Shoco, and Adullam,

α.11.8 Kah Gath, kah Mareshah, kah Ziph.
E.11.8 And Gath, and Mareshah, and Ziph,

α.11.9 
E.11.9 And Adoraim, and Lachish, and Azekah,

α.11.10 Kah Zorah, kah Ajalon, kah Hebron, nish ohtagish ut Judah kah Benjamin: pummeneutausue keitotanash.
E.11.10 And Zorah, and Aijalon, and Hebron, which are in Judah and in Benjamin fenced cities.

α.11.11 Kah men[o]hketeou menuhkonogquash, kah na upponon mugquompuh kah mummishkod meechum kah pummee, kah wine.
E.11.11 And he fortified the strong holds, and put captains in them, and store of victual, and of oil and wine.
