α.11.12 Kah nish$noh ut pasuk keitotan, na$ut ponamun ogqunnegash, kah qunuhtugquash, kah ahche menuhkehteauunash, Judahoh kah Benjaminoh weech8humuk.
E.11.12 And in every several city he put shields and spears, and made them exceeding strong, having Judah and Benjamin on his side.

α.11.13 Kah sephausuenuog Kah Levitsog, u[t] wame Israel, uppeyaounouh wutch wame wutayeuongan8out.
E.11.13 And the priests and the Levites that were in all Israel resorted to him out of all their coasts.

α.11.14 Newutche Levitsog, nukkodtumwog 8wonkôiyeum8ash, kah wutohtoonganóoash, kah peyaog Judah, kah Jerusalem: newutche Jeroboam kah wunnaumonuh, uppogkenouh wutch wussephausue anninnohsuenuunneat en Jehovah$ut.
E.11.14 For the Levites left their suburbs and their possession, and came to Judah and Jerusalem: for Jeroboam and his sons had cast them off from executing the priest's office unto the LORD:

α.11.15 Kah wussephausuenuheuh ut qunuhqui ayeuonganit, kah ut mattannit8uhtu, kah ut Calfsut neh kezheoncheh.
E.11.15 And he ordained him priests for the high places, and for the devils, and for the calves which he had made.

α.11.16 Kah nag asuhkaue, wutch wame Israelle chippan8onganehtu neg ponukeg wuttahh8oash wowussumonat Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, peyaog Jerusalem, sepha[m]auonat, Jehovah, ummanitt8m8uh 8sh8uh.
E.11.16 And after them out of all the tribes of Israel such as set their hearts to seek the LORD God of Israel came to Jerusalem, to sacrifice unto the LORD God of their fathers.

α.11.17 Neit menehketeauog Judae ketass8tamóonk, kah menehkheaog Rehoboamoh wunnaumonuh Solomon, nishwe kodtumwae, newutche nishwe kodtumwae pomushaog ummayut David Kah Solomon.
E.11.17 So they strengthened the kingdom of Judah, and made Rehoboam the son of Solomon strong, three years: for three years they walked in the way of David and Solomon.

α.11.18 Kah Rehoboam ummittamwussu Mahalath wuttaunoh Jerimoth, wunnaumonuh David, kah Abihail, wuttaunoh Eliab wunnaumonuh Jesse.
E.11.18 And Rehoboam took him Mahalath the daughter of Jerimoth the son of David to wife, and Abihail the daughter of Eliab the son of Jesse;

α.11.19 Noh nekitteauont, Joash kah Shamariah, kah Zaham.
E.11.19 Which bare him children; Jeush, and Shamariah, and Zaham.

α.11.20 Kah noh asuhkaue ummittamwussu Maachah, wuttaunoh Absolom, noh wunnekitteauoh Abijah, kah Attai, kah Ziza, kah Shelomith
E.11.20 And after her he took Maachah the daughter of Absalom; which bare him Abijah, and Attai, and Ziza, and Shelomith.

α.11.21 Kah Rehoboam womonau Maachah wuttaunoh Absolom, anue onk wame ummittamwussoh, kah 8skappeumoh, newutche nabo shwosuk tahsh8hkauau, kah nequtta tahshinchag kussuoh 8skappeumoh, kah wunnaumonieu nesnehchagkodtoh kah shwosuk tahsuoh wunnaumonuh, kah nequtta tahshinchagkodtoh wuttaunoh.
E.11.21 And Rehoboam loved Maachah the daughter of Absalom above all his wives and his concubines: (for he took eighteen wives, and threescore concubines; and begat twenty and eight sons, and threescore daughters.)

α.11.22 Kah Rehoboam negonneaheau Abijah wunnaumonuh Maachah, wunnanawunnuaenuunneat ut kenugke wematut, newutche ukkodketass8tamuhkonuh.
E.11.22 And Rehoboam made Abijah the son of Maachah the chief, to be ruler among his brethren: for he thought to make him king.

α.11.23 Kah waantamwe ussu, sepagehheau wunneechanoh, pannuppe wame Judae kah Benjamine ohkeit, ut nish pummeneutausue otanat kah umm8cheke assamuh, kah kodtanumau m8naoh ummittamwussoh.
E.11.23 And he dealt wisely, and dispersed of all his children throughout all the countries of Judah and Benjamin, unto every fenced city: and he gave them victual in abundance. And he desired many wives.

α.12.1 KAh nniyeup, Rehoboam manuhkehteunk ketass8tamóonk kah nanuhketeunk wunnogkuh, ohquontam wuttinnaumatuonk Jehovah, kah wame weeche Israel.
E.12.1 And it came to pass, when Rehoboam had established the kingdom, and had strengthened himself, he forsook the law of the LORD, and all Israel with him.

α.12.2 Kah nniyeup, napanna wutteashe kodtum8mit Rehoboam, Shishak Egypte ketass8t ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhqueontam Jerusalem (newutche matcheneheaog Jehovahoh.)
E.12.2 And it came to pass, that in the fifth year of king Rehoboam Shishak king of Egypt came up against Jerusalem, because they had transgressed against the LORD,

α.12.3 Nashpe naboneese pasuk88ash chariotsash, kah nequtta tahshinchage muttannonganog kussuog horsesoh na8mukqutcheg: kah missinninnuog matta waogkem8og neg weechogqutcheg wutch Egypt Labimsog kah Sukkimsog, kah Ethiopiansog.
E.12.3 With twelve hundred chariots, and threescore thousand horsemen: and the people were without number that came with him out of Egypt; the Lubims, the Sukkiims, and the Ethiopians.

α.12.4 Kah sohkom pummeneutausue keitotanash nish ut Judah, kah peyaog Jerusalem.
E.12.4 And he took the fenced cities which pertained to Judah, and came to Jerusalem.

α.12.5 Neit Shemajah quoshodtumwaen peyaonau Rehoboamoh, kah Judae sontimuh, neg miyaecheg ut Jerusalem newutche Shishak, kah na wuttinuh yeu wussin Jehovah: kenaau kutohquanumimw8, kah newaj nukonunog ut wunnutcheganit Shishak.
E.12.5 Then came Shemaiah the prophet to Rehoboam, and to the princes of Judah, that were gathered together to Jerusalem because of Shishak, and said unto them, Thus saith the LORD, Ye have forsaken me, and therefore have I also left you in the hand of Shishak.

α.12.6 Newaj Israelle sontimóog kah ketass8t, hohpaheahettit, kah n8waog, Jehovah sampweusseaen.
E.12.6 Whereupon the princes of Israel and the king humbled themselves; and they said, The LORD is righteous.

α.12.7 Kah Jehovah nag* hohpáheáog wuhhogkauh wuttiñ8waonk Jehovah peyaónuk Shemajah n8wau: nag hohaheáog wuhhogkauh matta nuppaguanóog, qut nuttinnumauaog ne teagwe tomhettuonk, kah nummasquantam8onk matta pish sohkemun8, ut Jerusalem, nashpe wunnutcheg Shishak.
E.12.7 And when the LORD saw that they humbled themselves, the word of the LORD came to Shemaiah, saying, They have humbled themselves; therefore I will not destroy them, but I will grant them some deliverance; and my wrath shall not be poured out upon Jerusalem by the hand of Shishak.

α.12.8 Qut nah pish 8tinninneumuneuh, onk woh wahteauog n8tinninneumuhko[n]teaonk, kah wuttinneumuhkontamoonk wutohtimoinne ketass8tam8ongash.
E.12.8 Nevertheless they shall be his servants; that they may know my service, and the service of the kingdoms of the countries.

α.12.9 Neit Shishak Egypte ketass8t ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquehtam Jerusalem, kah amaunum nompak8ansh ut wekit Jehovah, kah nompakouunash ut ketass8t wekit, 8wame maumunash: kah wonk amaunum golde ogquñeg[á]sh, nish Solomon ayikupash.
E.12.9 So Shishak king of Egypt came up against Jerusalem, and took away the treasures of the house of the LORD, and the treasures of the king's house; he took all: he carried away also the shields of gold which Solomon had made.

α.12.10 Nompe nish, ketass8t Rehoboam ayim brasse ogqunegash: kah wutahtashonash en wunnutcheganit, negonneyeuit ut wadchanonganit, noh nanawehteunk ahhut petutteamuk ketass8t wek.
E.12.10 Instead of which king Rehoboam made shields of brass, and committed them to the hands of the chief of the guard, that kept the entrance of the king's house.

α.12.11 Kah ketass8t petutteadt wekit Jehovah, wadchanuacheg peyaog, kah wunneemskomunaoash kah wonk uppaudtamunaoash wadchanuae chamberut.
E.12.11 And when the king entered into the house of the LORD, the guard came and fetched them, and brought them again into the guard chamber.

α.12.12 Kah ohhohpaheont wuhhogkuh ummusquanitteaonk Jehovah qushkehtunk, kah matta pannuppe uppaguanuh, kah wonk ut Judah wunniyeuog.
E.12.12 And when he humbled himself, the wrath of the LORD turned from him, that he would not destroy him altogether: and also in Judah things went well.

α.12.13 Neit ketass8t Rehoboam menehkheau wuhhogkuh ut Jerusalem, kah ketass8tam88: newutche Rehoboam yauunchage kah nequtta kodtumwohkomup n8che ketass8tam8it, kah nabo nesausuk tahshe kodtumwae ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem, ut keitotanat, ne Jehovah pepenog, wutch wame wutchippan8onganit Israel[,] na upponamunat 8wesuonk: kah ohkasoh ussowesuoh Naamah, wut-Ammonitesse.
E.12.13 So king Rehoboam strengthened himself in Jerusalem, and reigned: for Rehoboam was one and forty years old when he began to reign, and he reigned seventeen years in Jerusalem, the city which the LORD had chosen out of all the tribes of Israel, to put his name there. And his mother's name was Naamah an Ammonitess.

α.12.14 Kah matchesu newutche matta quagquashwunnum8 wuttah natinneawhonat Jehovah.
E.12.14 And he did evil, because he prepared not his heart to seek the LORD.

α.12.15 Kah wutusseongash Rehoboam, negonneyeuukish kah maumachisheu8gish, sunnummatta wussukwhosinash ut wussukwhonganit Shemajah quoshodtumwaen, kah Iddo naumwaen, papaume wutontseongash? kah ayeuwuttuonganu8 nagwutteaeu nashaue ut Rehoboam kah Jeroboam.
E.12.15 Now the acts of Rehoboam, first and last, are they not written in the book of Shemaiah the prophet, and of Iddo the seer concerning genealogies? And there were wars between Rehoboam and Jeroboam continually.

α.12.16 Kah Rehoboam weesequom8mau 8shoh, kah posekinau ut ukkeitotanat David, kah Abijahoh wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tam8mukquoh.
E.12.16 And Rehoboam slept with his fathers, and was buried in the city of David: and Abijah his son reigned in his stead.

α.13.1 KAh nabo shwosuk wutteashe kodtum8mit Jeroboam, Abijah n8che ketass8tam88 ut Judah.
E.13.1 Now in the eighteenth year of king Jeroboam began Abijah to reign over Judah.

α.13.2 Ketass8tam88 nishwe kodtumwae ut Jerusalem: (kah wonk ohkasoh ussowesu Micajah wuttaunoh Uzziel wutch Gibeah) kah na ayeuwuttuonganu8, nashaue Abijah Kah Jeroboam.
E.13.2 He reigned three years in Jerusalem. His mother's name also was Michaiah the daughter of Uriel of Gibeah. And there was war between Abijah and Jeroboam.

α.13.3 Kah Abijah wunohto ayeuwuttuonk, nashpe menuhkoshektomp kenauwameonk yauut pasuk88e muttannonganog kussuog, pepenauutcheg, kah wonk Jeroboam wutayeuuhkonittue wunohtauoh, shwosuk táhshe pasuk8e muttannonganog kussuog wosketompaog, menuhkesuenuog.
E.13.3 And Abijah set the battle in array with an army of valiant men of war, even four hundred thousand chosen men: Jeroboam also set the battle in array against him with eight hundred thousand chosen men, being mighty men of valour.

α.13.4 Kah Abijah neepau ut Zemaraimme wadchuut, ne Ephraimme wadchuut, kah n8wau, n8tah ken Jeroboam, & wame Israel.
E.13.4 And Abijah stood up upon mount Zemaraim, which is in mount Ephraim, and said, Hear me, thou Jeroboam, and all Israel;

α.13.5 Sunnummatta woh kutahche wahteau8mw8, Lord um-Manitt8moh Israel aninnumauau Davidoh wutass8tamonk Israel micheme, en wuhhogkat, kah en wunnaumonat, nashpe salte wunn8waonk?
E.13.5 Ought ye not to know that the LORD God of Israel gave the kingdom over Israel to David for ever, even to him and to his sons by a covenant of salt?

α.13.6 Qut Jeroboam wunnaumonuh Nebat, wuttinneumoh Solomon, wunnaumonuh David, waábu, kah ayeuuhkonittue cheketauau wussontimom.
E.13.6 Yet Jeroboam the son of Nebat, the servant of Solomon the son of David, is risen up, and hath rebelled against his lord.

α.13.7 Kah noh wuttit miyánumauon tohn8cheyeuunitche, wunnaumonuh Belial, kah menehkheáog wuhhogkauh, ayeuuhkonittue Rehoboamoh wunnaumonuh Solomon, Rehoboam peississit, kah n8chumweteáhont, kah n8nannum8 wuttapenonat.
E.13.7 And there are gathered unto him vain men, the children of Belial, and have strengthened themselves against Rehoboam the son of Solomon, when Rehoboam was young and tenderhearted, and could not withstand them.

α.13.8 Kah yeuyeu kuttenantamw8 wuttammehteauunat wutass8tamóonk Jehovah, ut wunnutcheganit wunnaumonuh David, kah kummuttaánumw8, kah k8wetomukumw8 golde Calvesog, neh Jeroboam ayeuompuh wutch kum-manitt8m8óog.
E.13.8 And now ye think to withstand the kingdom of the LORD in the hand of the sons of David; and ye be a great multitude, and there are with your golden calves, which Jeroboam made you for gods.

α.13.9 Sunnummatta kuppogkenomw8 wussephausuéneumoh Jehovah, wunnaumonuh Aaron, kah Levitsog, kah kussephausuewennu[à]heamw8 kuhhogkaóog, ne aséhettit wutohtimoneash ut ohkeit? newutche wuttinniin howan peyont, 8neetupanatamwaheonat wuhhogkuh, nashpe wushkoshim ox, kah nesausuk tahsuog ramsog: onk noh woh sephausuenu8 ut nag matta wamanitt8mogig?
E.13.9 Have ye not cast out the priests of the LORD, the sons of Aaron, and the Levites, and have made you priests after the manner of the nations of other lands? so that whosoever cometh to consecrate himself with a young bullock and seven rams, the same may be a priest of them that are no gods.

α.13.10 Qut neenawun, Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, kah matta nutohquan[u]móun, kah sephausuenuog neg wowussumoncheg Jehovahoh neh wunnaumonuh Aaron, kah Levitsog usseog wutusseongan8.
E.13.10 But as for us, the LORD is our God, and we have not forsaken him; and the priests, which minister unto the LORD, are the sons of Aaron, and the Levites wait upon their business:

α.13.11 Kah nag chikohsumauáog Jehovahoh nishnoh mohtomp[à]eu nishnoh wunnonkquaeu chikohsumóe sephausuongash, kah wetemungquok, kah wonk nahtitteáe petukqunnunk wunohtóog ut pahke tableut, kah golde wequananteganuhtug nashpe wul$lampsash, chikohsumunat nishnoh wunnonk8, newutche nanawehteómun ummeechumuhkausuáonk Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, qut kenaau kutohquanumau.
E.13.11 And they burn unto the LORD every morning and every evening burnt sacrifices and sweet incense: the shewbread also set they in order upon the pure table; and the candlestick of gold with the lamps thereof, to burn every evening: for we keep the charge of the LORD our God; but ye have forsaken him.

α.13.12 Kah kusseh, God k8wetomukqun, mugquomp, kah wussephausueneumoh, nashpe mishont8wáe monopuhpegquash, ayeuuhkonittue kenaau ummishont8wáe puhpequonat, woi wunnaumonuh Israel, ayeukonúhteogk Lord um-Manitt8moh k8sh8óog, newutche matta pish koniyeum8.
E.13.12 And, behold, God himself is with us for our captain, and his priests with sounding trumpets to cry alarm against you. O children of Israel, fight ye not against the LORD God of your fathers; for ye shall not prosper.

α.13.13 Qut Jeroboam adhôsuonk quinnuppeá[h] au ut uppusquan8óut, newaj nag negonuhk[a]uâhettit Judah, & adhausuonk uppushquan8óont.
E.13.13 But Jeroboam caused an ambushment to come about behind them: so they were before Judah, and the ambushment was behind them.

α.13.14 Kah Judah ompámuhquait, kusseh ayeuwuttuonk anaquabit, kah uppusquanit; kah nag mauunnitteaog Jehovahoh, kah sephausuenúog puhpequaog.
E.13.14 And when Judah looked back, behold, the battle was before and behind: and they cried unto the LORD, and the priests sounded with the trumpets.

α.13.15 Neit Judae wosketompaog mishont8waog: kah mashant8wáhettit wosketompaog Judah, n$niyeup, God togkomau Jeroboamoh, kah wame Israeloh, anaquabhettit Abijah, kah Judah.
E.13.15 Then the men of Judah gave a shout: and as the men of Judah shouted, it came to pass, that God smote Jeroboam and all Israel before Abijah and Judah.

α.13.16 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel wusseemoog wutch anaquabhettit Judah: kah God nah upponuh wunnutchegan8óut.
E.13.16 And the children of Israel fled before Judah: and God delivered them into their hand.

α.13.17 Kah Abijah kah ummissinninneumoh nah wunnushóuh nashpe mishe paguanittùonk: neit na wuttit nushóe penushóneau, napaña tahshit pasuk88e muttañonganogkussuog pepenauutcheg Israelle wosketompaog.
E.13.17 And Abijah and his people slew them with a great slaughter: so there fell down slain of Israel five hundred thousand chosen men.

α.13.18 Yeu in wunnaumonuh Israel sohkauóneau, na ahquompak: kah wunnaumonuh Judah sohkóhsuoh, newutche pabuhtanumáog Jehovahoh, um-Manitt8m8uh 8sh8oh.
E.13.18 Thus the children of Israel were brought under at that time, and the children of Judah prevailed, because they relied upon the LORD God of their fathers.

α.13.19 Kah Abijah n8swetahwau Jeroboamoh, kah wunnemanumauoh keitotanash, Bethel kah nish otanash, kah Jeshanah, kah nish otanash, kah Ephron, kah nish otanash.
E.13.19 And Abijah pursued after Jeroboam, and took cities from him, Bethel with the towns thereof, and Jeshanah with the towns thereof, and Ephraim with the towns thereof.

α.13.20 Kah Jeroboam matta wonk nompenuhkésu, ut ukkesukodtumut Abijah, kah Jehovah wuttogkomuh, kah nupp8.
E.13.20 Neither did Jeroboam recover strength again in the days of Abijah: and the LORD struck him, and he died.

α.13.21 Kah Abijah nano menuhkesu, kah nabo yau8kauau, kah nesnehchag kenaumóniau kah nees8oh, kah nabo nequtta tahsuoh wuttaunoh.
E.13.21 But Abijah waxed mighty, and married fourteen wives, and begat twenty and two sons, and sixteen daughters.

α.13.22 Kah onkatogish wutusseongash Abijah, kah ummayash, kah wunnupwóaongash, nish wussukwhosuash, ut 8wohtamwáhuónat Iddo quoshodtumwáen.
E.13.22 And the rest of the acts of Abijah, and his ways, and his sayings, are written in the story of the prophet Iddo.

α.14.1 NEit Abijah weesequom8mau 8shoh, kah upposekinóuh ut ukkeitotanat David, kah Asahoh wunnaumonuh, wunnompass8tamomukquoh: ut ukkesukodtumut, ohke chequnohteau piogque kodtumwae,
E.14.1 So Abijah slept with his fathers, and they buried him in the city of David: and Asa his son reigned in his stead. In his days the land was quiet ten years.

α.14.2 Kah Asa ussu ne wanegik, kah ne sampwagk ut wuskesukqut Jehovahoh um-Manitt8moh.
E.14.2 And Asa did that which was good and right in the eyes of the LORD his God:

α.14.3 Newutche amaunau wut-altarumóuh penóe manittóog, kah qunuhqui ayeuongash, kah sohquetahwhau nunneukontunkoh, kah m8setahham kuppiyeuash.
E.14.3 For he took away the altars of the strange gods, and the high places, and brake down the images, and cut down the groves:

α.14.4 Kah ann8nau Judahoh wunnatineahwhonat Jehovaoh um-Manitt8m8oh 8sh8oh, kah ussenat wuttinnaumatuonk, kah ann8team8onk.
E.14.4 And commanded Judah to seek the LORD God of their fathers, and to do the law and the commandment.

α.14.5 Wonk amaunum wutch Judae keitotanahtu, qunuhqui ayeuongash, kah nunneukontunkoh: kah an8tamóonk nanowóhteau ut anaquabit.
E.14.5 Also he took away out of all the cities of Judah the high places and the images: and the kingdom was quiet before him.

α.14.6 Kah ayim pummeneutausue otanash ut Judah, newutche ohke anwôshshin, kah matta ayeuwuttéin yeush ut kodtum8ash, newutche Jehovah wutanwôhsum8wáheuh.
E.14.6 And he built fenced cities in Judah: for the land had rest, and he had no war in those years; because the LORD had given him rest.

α.14.7 Newaj unnont Judahoh, ayimuttuh yeush otanash, kah nash quinnuppeneutauuttuh, kah qunuhqui wonkonôsuash, squontamash, kah barsash, ohke ash anaquabeog áohtagkup: newutche kenatinneawhómun kum-Manitt8mun, kenátinneawhóunnônup, kah kutanwohsumwáhikqun waéenu: neit wekitteáog kah wunniyeuog.
E.14.7 Therefore he said unto Judah, Let us build these cities, and make about them walls, and towers, gates, and bars, while the land is yet before us; because we have sought the LORD our God, we have sought him, and he hath given us rest on every side. So they built and prospered.

α.14.8 Kah Asa wutáyeuwehteómw8 neg ohtunkeg ogqunnegash kah qunnuhtukquash, wutch Judah, nishwudt pasuk8e muttannonganogkussuog, kah wutch Benjamin, neg kôunukeg ogqunegash, kah wadohtompéitcheg, neese pasuk8e kah shwosuk tahshinchage muttannonganogkussuog, wame yeug menuhkesuénuog.
E.14.8 And Asa had an army of men that bare targets and spears, out of Judah three hundred thousand; and out of Benjamin, that bare shields and drew bows, two hundred and fourscore thousand: all these were mighty men of valour.

α.14.9 Kah wutayeuuhkonittue sohwehtau Zerah wut$Ethiopian, nashpe muttannongane muttannonganogkussuog ayeuteáog, kah nishwudt pasuk88ash chariotsash, kah peyaog Mareshah.
E.14.9 And there came out against them Zerah the Ethiopian with an host of a thousand thousand, and three hundred chariots; and came unto Mareshah.

α.14.10 Neit Asa ayeuwehkonittue s[ô]hwehtau, kah wunohto ayeuwuttuonk ut Zephathae 8nouhkoiyeuut, ut Mareshah.
E.14.10 Then Asa went out against him, and they set the battle in array in the valley of Zephathah at Mareshah.

α.14.11 Kah Asa mauunnitteauau Jehovaoh um-Manitt8moh, kah n8wau, Woi Jehovah peamesau teaguas kutanumaiinneanónut, asuh nashpe m8náog, asuh nashpe neg matta wâmenuhkésuo[n]ganegig: aninnumaiinnean woi Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, newutche kutanwôhsinn8wóunumun, kah ut k8wesuonganit nutayeukôunómun yeug mattaánukeg: woi Jehovah, ken num$Manitt8mun; howae wosketomp sohkunk8hkan.
E.14.11 And Asa cried unto the LORD his God, and said, LORD, it is nothing with thee to help, whether with many, or with them that have no power: help us, O LORD our God; for we rest on thee, and in thy name we go against this multitude. O LORD, thou art our God; let no man prevail against thee.

α.14.12 Neit Jehovah togkomau Ethiopiansoh ut anaquabit Asa, kah anaquabhettit Judah, kah Ethiopiansog wussem8og.
E.14.12 So the LORD smote the Ethiopians before Asa, and before Judah; and the Ethiopians fled.

α.14.13 Kah Asa, kah missinninnuog neg wetomoncheg, wunn8suttahwhouh en Gerar: kah Ethiopiansog, kepuhkonunk, kah matta wonk menuhkeséog, newutche nag ushkoméhheôog ut anaquabit Jehovah, kah ut anaquabenit wutáyeuwehteomuh, kah monchatauog m8cheke sequttahham8onk.
E.14.13 And Asa and the people that were with him pursued them unto Gerar: and the Ethiopians were overthrown, that they could not recover themselves; for they were destroyed before the LORD, and before his host; and they carried away very much spoil.

α.14.14 Kah nag togkodtamwog wame keitotanash waéenu Gerar, newutche qushaonk Jehovah nuhkuhkongquog: kah sequttahhamwontamwog wame keitotanash, newutche na$ut m8cheke sequttahhamóonk.
E.14.14 And they smote all the cities round about Gerar; for the fear of the LORD came upon them: and they spoiled all the cities; for there was exceeding much spoil in them.

α.14.15 Kah wonk togkodtamwog puppinashimwe wetuómash, kah monchanáog shepsoh kah camelsoh m8cheke, kah qushkeog en Jerusalem.
E.14.15 They smote also the tents of cattle, and carried away sheep and camels in abundance, and returned to Jerusalem.

α.15.1 KAh wunnashauanitt8moh God nuhkuhkauau Azariahoh wunnaumonuh Oded
E.15.1 And the Spirit of God came upon Azariah the son of Oded:

α.15.2 Kah sohham wunnogskauónat Asahoh, kah wuttinuh, n8tiegk Asa, kah wame Judah, kah Benjamin, Jehovah k8wetomuk8, ash weetomog; kah noh natinneáhwhóog, noh woh naméheau wutche kenaau: qut nukkonóg, noh pish kutóhquanumukou.
E.15.2 And he went out to meet Asa, and said unto him, Hear ye me, Asa, and all Judah and Benjamin; The LORD is with you, while ye be with him; and if ye seek him, he will be found of you; but if ye forsake him, he will forsake you.

α.15.3 Yeuyeu sepe, Israel matta sampwe um-Manitt8mu, kah wannekuhk8tomuhteáe sephausuenúmeu, kah matta wuttinnaumatuonganu.
E.15.3 Now for a long season Israel hath been without the true God, and without a teaching priest, and without law.

α.15.4 Qut nag wadtamehpunahettit, quinnuppehettit en Jehovahut um-Manitt8moh Israel, kah natinnewháhettit, noh nah wunn[a]mhikquoh.
E.15.4 But when they in their trouble did turn unto the LORD God of Israel, and sought him, he was found of them.

α.15.5 Kah nish ahquompagish wanne 8nohteaonganu noh sohhog, asuh noh petutteadt, qut mishe wuttammehpunnaonganúog wame ne wadohkitcheg ne wutohtimóneat.
E.15.5 And in those times there was no peace to him that went out, nor to him that came in, but great vexations were upon all the inhabitants of the countries.

α.15.6 Kah wutohtimóin ôshkommehtóhuk wutohtimóin, kah keitotan keitotan: newutche God 8taméhpunáheuh nashpe wame wuttaméhpunnaongash.
E.15.6 And nation was destroyed of nation, and city of city: for God did vex them with all adversity.

α.15.7 Newutche menuhkesek, kah kenutchegan8ash n8chumwahkitch: newutche kutanakausuonganu pish onkquatantamun.
E.15.7 Be ye strong therefore, and let not your hands be weak: for your work shall be rewarded.

α.15.8 Kah Asa n8tog yeush kutt8wongash, kah ukquoshodtumóonk Oded quoshodtumwáen wutt8antam, kah amaunau wame unkquanumwe nunneukontunkoh, wutch wame Judae ohkeit, kah Benjamin, kah wutch keitotanash nish neemunukish wutch Ephraime wadchuut, kah wushkeheau Jehovah wut-altarumoh, ne anaquohtag Jehovah up-porchum.
E.15.8 And when Asa heard these words, and the prophecy of Oded the prophet, he took courage, and put away the abominable idols out of all the land of Judah and Benjamin, and out of the cities which he had taken from mount Ephraim, and renewed the altar of the LORD, that was before the porch of the LORD.

α.15.9 Kah miyanau wame Judahoh, kah Benjaminoh, kah penuwohteuh neh wetomukquehetticheh wutch Ephraim, kah wutch Manasseh, kah wutch Simeon: (newutche na 8ch 8weech8whin Israelut m8naoh, namohettit Jehovahoh um-Manitt8moh weetomuk)
E.15.9 And he gathered all Judah and Benjamin, and the strangers with them out of Ephraim and Manasseh, and out of Simeon: for they fell to him out of Israel in abundance, when they saw that the LORD his God was with him.

α.15.10 Neit miyawéog ut Jerusalem, ut nash8unitcheh nepâuzsoh, nabo napanna tahshe kodtumwae ketass8tam8it Asa.
E.15.10 So they gathered themselves together at Jerusalem in the third month, in the fifteenth year of the reign of Asa.

α.15.11 Kah nag sephamauáog Jehovaoh, ne kesukok, nawhutch sequttahham8onk ne paudtauahettit, nesausuk tahshe pasuk88og oxenog, kah nesausuk tahshe muttannonganogkussuog shepsog.
E.15.11 And they offered unto the LORD the same time, of the spoil which they had brought, seven hundred oxen and seven thousand sheep.

α.15.12 Kah wunn8wáog natinneawhonat Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh 8sh8oh, nashpe mamusse wuttahh8óash, kah nashpe mamusse ukketeahogkôunuh.
E.15.12 And they entered into a covenant to seek the LORD God of their fathers with all their heart and with all their soul;

α.15.13 Kah noh howan matta natinneáwhonk Jehovahoh um$Manitt8moh Israel, pish nushau, uttoh en peississit asuh masugkenit, uttoh en wosketomp asuh mittumwossis.
E.15.13 That whosoever would not seek the LORD God of Israel should be put to death, whether small or great, whether man or woman.

α.15.14 Kah nag chadchekeimaog Jehovahoh nashpe mishont8waonk, kah nashpe kussont8waonk, kah nashpe monopuhpequonash, kah nashpe Cornetsash.
E.15.14 And they sware unto the LORD with a loud voice, and with shouting, and with trumpets, and with cornets.

α.15.15 Kah wame Judah wekontamwog ut chadchekeyeuwaonganit, newutche nag chadchekeyeuwaog nashpe mamusse wuttahhou, kah wunnatinneawhouh nashpe mamusse ukkodtantam8ongan8, kah noh nah wunnamhukquoh: kah Jehovah wutanwohsumwaheuh waeenu.
E.15.15 And all Judah rejoiced at the oath: for they had sworn with all their heart, and sought him with their whole desire; and he was found of them: and the LORD gave them rest round about.

α.15.16 Kah wonk papaume Maacha, ohkasoh Asa ketass8t, wutontashuh wutch wussonksquauninneat, newutche nunneukontunkanehteau ut kuppahtu, kah Asa wuttummetahhamauoh wuttiñeukontunkoh, & wuttogwhuh, kah wutchikoss8h ut Kidrone sepuut.
E.15.16 And also concerning Maachah the mother of Asa the king, he removed her from being queen, because she had made an idol in a grove: and Asa cut down her idol, and stamped it, and burnt it at the brook Kidron.

α.15.17 Qut qunuhqui ayeuongash matta amaunum8unash wutch Israel: qut wuttah Asa pannuppeyeu8 nisohke pomantog.
E.15.17 But the high places were not taken away out of Israel: nevertheless the heart of Asa was perfect all his days.

α.15.18 Kah uppaudtauunash wekit God, nish 8shoh waneetupanatamwateunkupash, silver kah Gold kah auwohteaongash.
E.15.18 And he brought into the house of God the things that his father had dedicated, and that he himself had dedicated, silver, and gold, and vessels.

α.15.19 Kah matta wonk ayeuwuttuonganinno, nô pajeh nishwinchage kah napannah kohtass8tam8it Asa:
E.15.19 And there was no more war unto the five and thirtieth year of the reign of Asa.

α.16.1 NIshwinchage kah nequtta kehtass8tam8it Asah Baasha Israelle ketass8t, ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquehtam Judah, kah ayim Ramah, yeu wutche, matta woh howan wussohham8unat, asuh petutteaonat Asa ketass8t ut Judah.
E.16.1 In the six and thirtieth year of the reign of Asa Baasha king of Israel came up against Judah, and built Ramah, to the intent that he might let none go out or come in to Asa king of Judah.

α.16.2 Neit Asa sohh8wuttau gold, kah nompakouunash wutch wekit Jehovah, kah wutch wekit ketass8t, kah wunnegonshhuon en Benhadadut Syriae ketass8t, noh wadohkit Damascus, n8wau.
E.16.2 Then Asa brought out silver and gold out of the treasures of the house of the LORD and of the king's house, and sent to Benhadad king of Syria, that dwelt at Damascus, saying,

α.16.3 Wunn8waonganu8 nashaue ut nen kah ken, neane ut nashaue ut n8sh kah k8sh: kusseh negonshhuam en kuhhogkat s[i]ver kah gold, monchish, pohquenush k8n8waongan8 Baashah Israelle ketass8t, onk woh nutamaehtunk.
E.16.3 There is a league between me and thee, as there was between my father and thy father: behold, I have sent thee silver and gold; go, break thy league with Baasha king of Israel, that he may depart from me.

α.16.4 Kah Benhadad n8tauau ketass8t Asa, kah ayeuuhkonittue ann8nau, en Israelle keitotanat wutayeuwuhteae ummugquompomoh kah togkodtamwog Jion, kah Dan, kah Abel$maim, kah wame 8wadchanumwe otanash Naphthali.
E.16.4 And Benhadad hearkened unto king Asa, and sent the captains of his armies against the cities of Israel; and they smote Ijon, and Dan, and Abelmaim, and all the store cities of Naphtali.

α.16.5 Kah niyeup, Baasha n8tog, ahque weekitteau ut Ramah, kah wutanakausuonk netahshinnu8.
E.16.5 And it came to pass, when Baasha heard it, that he left off building of Ramah, and let his work cease.

α.16.6 Neit ketass8t Asa, nemunau wame Judahoh, kah nag uss8wuttauog qussukquanash Ramah, kah ne Timber, ne nashp[é] Baasha weekitteaop, kah ne wunnashpe wekukon Geba, kah Mizpah.
E.16.6 Then Asa the king took all Judah; and they carried away the stones of Ramah, and the timber thereof, wherewith Baasha was building; and he built therewith Geba and Mizpah.

α.16.7 Kah na ahquompak Hanani naumwaen peyau Asa Judae ketass8tam8ut, kah wuttinuh, newutche kuppabahtanum Syriae keta[a]ss8t, kah matta kuppabahtanumóh Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, newaj wutáyeuwéhteomoh Syriae ke[t]ss8t; pohquohham wutch kenutcheganit.
E.16.7 And at that time Hanani the seer came to Asa king of Judah, and said unto him, Because thou hast relied on the king of Syria, and not relied on the LORD thy God, therefore is the host of the king of Syria escaped out of thine hand.

α.16.8 Sunnummatta Ethiopiansog, kah Lubimsog missi wutayeuwehteongan8, weeche monatash chariotsash kah horsesoh na8mukqutcheh? qut newutche kuppabohtanumomp Jehovah, upponah ut kenutcheganit.
E.16.8 Were not the Ethiopians and the Lubims a huge host, with very many chariots and horsemen? yet, because thou didst rely on the LORD, he delivered them into thine hand.

α.16.9 Newutche wuskesukquash Jehovah papannupushaash mamusse ohkeit, ummenuhkeeu weech8hamonat nah wuttahh8óash pannuppeyeu8gish nogque en wuhhogkat, yeu kuttit mattammagwe ussen, newutche, yeu wutch pish k8matompag8m.
E.16.9 For the eyes of the LORD run to and fro throughout the whole earth, to shew himself strong in the behalf of them whose heart is perfect toward him. Herein thou hast done foolishly: therefore from henceforth thou shalt have wars.

α.16.10 Neit Asa musquanumau naumwaenuh kah ukkupshagkinuh, newutche ummishe musquanumuh, newutche yeu, kah Asa sunukohwau nawhutch missinninnuh ne nan ahquompag.
E.16.10 Then Asa was wroth with the seer, and put him in a prison house; for he was in a rage with him because of this thing. And Asa oppressed some of the people the same time.

α.16.11 Kah kusséh wutusseongash Asa negonne kah maumachish, kusseh, wussukwhosuash, ut 8sukuhwhongan8out Judae, kah Israelle ketass8tamwog.
E.16.11 And, behold, the acts of Asa, first and last, lo, they are written in the book of the kings of Judah and Israel.

α.16.12 Kah Asa nishwinchage kah pasuk8gun tahshe kodtumwae ketass8tam8it, mahchinau ut wusseetut, nô pajeh ummahchinnáonk missiyeuit: qut onch ut wunn8chumwesuonganit matta natinneawhoou Jehovahoh, qut ponaskehtuaenuh.
E.16.12 And Asa in the thirty and ninth year of his reign was diseased in his feet, until his disease was exceeding great: yet in his disease he sought not to the LORD, but to the physicians.

α.16.13 Kah Asa weesequom8mau 8shoh, kah nupp8 yauunnehchage kah nahen nequt kodtumwae kohtass8tam8it.
E.16.13 And Asa slept with his fathers, and died in the one and fortieth year of his reign.

α.16.14 Kah upposekinouh nehenwonche wenohkeit, ne ayimauont wuhhogkuh, ut wut8tanat David, kah wussepsumouh appinneat, ne nomwohtag wetemungquokish, kah eiyane spicash; quagquashwehtogish nashpe wunnetuhtauonk Apothecary: kah ummishe chikohsumwontamauouh.
E.16.14 And they buried him in his own sepulchres, which he had made for himself in the city of David, and laid him in the bed which was filled with sweet odours and divers kinds of spices prepared by the apothecaries' art: and they made a very great burning for him.

α.17.1 KAh Jehosaphatoh wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tamomukquoh, kah ayeuuhkonittue menehkheau wuhhogkuh Israeloh.
E.17.1 And Jehoshaphat his son reigned in his stead, and strengthened himself against Israel.

α.17.2 Kah wunohto wadchanuaongash, ut wame pummeneutausue keitotanash ut Judah, kah ut Ephraime keitotanash, nish Asaoh 8shoh neemunuhpash.
E.17.2 And he placed forces in all the fenced cities of Judah, and set garrisons in the land of Judah, and in the cities of Ephraim, which Asa his father had taken.

α.17.3 Kah Jehovah wetômau Jehosophatoh, newutche pomushau negonne ummayash 8shoh Davidoh, kah matta natinneawhau Baalimoh.
E.17.3 And the LORD was with Jehoshaphat, because he walked in the first ways of his father David, and sought not unto Baalim;

α.17.4 Qut natinneawhau Lord um$Manitt8m8uh 8shoh, kah pomushauoh wutann8team8onganit, kah matta asuhkaue wutusseongash Israel.
E.17.4 But sought to the Lord God of his father, and walked in his commandments, and not after the doings of Israel.

α.17.5 Newaj Jehovah menehketeunk ketass8tamóonk ut wunnutcheganit, kah wame Judah mag8og wenauwetuonk kah quttianittuonk m8cheke.
E.17.5 Therefore the LORD stablished the kingdom in his hand; and all Judah brought to Jehoshaphat presents; and he had riches and honour in abundance.

α.17.6 Kah wuttah tahshinausu ut ummayut Jehovah: kah wonk amaunum qunuhqui ayeuongash, kah kuppiyeuash wutch Judah.
E.17.6 And his heart was lifted up in the ways of the LORD: moreover he took away the high places and groves out of Judah.

α.17.7 Wonk ut nashwe kodtumwae kohtass8tam8it, negont8au, wussontimausimoh, Benhailoh, kah Obadiahoh, kah Zechariahoh kah Nathaneeloh, kah Micajatoh, kuhk8tomuhkonat ut keitotanahtu Judah.
E.17.7 Also in the third year of his reign he sent to his princes, even to Benhail, and to Obadiah, and to Zechariah, and to Nethaneel, and to Michaiah, to teach in the cities of Judah.

α.17.8 Kah nag weechayeumukquog Levitsoh, Shemajah, & Nathaniah, & Zebadiah, & Asahel, kah Shemiramoth, kah Jehonathan, kah Adonijah, kah Tobijah, kah Tob-Adonijah, Levitsog, kah nag weechayeumukquog Elishama, kah Jehoram sephausuenuog.
E.17.8 And with them he sent Levites, even Shemaiah, and Nethaniah, and Zebadiah, and Asahel, and Shemiramoth, and Jehonathan, and Adonijah, and Tobijah, and Tobadonijah, Levites; and with them Elishama and Jehoram, priests.

α.17.9 Kah kuhk8tomwehteaog ut Judah, kah weeche kenunnumwog wuttinnaumatue Jehovah b8k, kah pannupwushaog wame Judae keitotanash, kah kuhk8tomauaog missinninnuh.
E.17.9 And they taught in Judah, and had the book of the law of the LORD with them, and went about throughout all the cities of Judah, and taught the people.

α.17.10 Kah qushaonk Jehovah nuhkuhkom wame, wutohtimoine ketass8tam8ongash, nish weenohtagish Judah, newaj matta ayeuuhkonahetteg Jehosophatoh.
E.17.10 And the fear of the LORD fell upon all the kingdoms of the lands that were round about Judah, so that they made no war against Jehoshaphat.

α.17.11 Wonk nawhutch Philistiansog pau[à]tauaog mag8ongash Jehosophatoh, kah ompweteae silver, kah Arabiansog uppaudtauouh floksog, nesausuk tahṣhe muttannonganog kussuog ramsog, kah nesausuk tahṣhe muttannonganog kussuog nomposhimwe goatsog.
E.17.11 Also some of the Philistines brought Jehoshaphat presents, and tribute silver; and the Arabians brought him flocks, seven thousand and seven hundred rams, and seven thousand and seven hundred he goats.

α.17.12 Kah Jehoshaphat nano missugken m8cheke, kah ayim ut Judah wonkon8sinash, kah wadchanumwae otanash.
E.17.12 And Jehoshaphat waxed great exceedingly; and he built in Judah castles, and cities of store.

α.17.13 Kah missi wutusseongash ut Judae keitotanahtu, kah ayeuteaenuog, menuhkesuenuog ut Jerusalem.
E.17.13 And he had much business in the cities of Judah: and the men of war, mighty men of valour, were in Jerusalem.

α.17.14 Kah yeu wutteas8unneau, neaunak 8sh8oh week8oash ut Judah muttannongane mugquompuh, Adnah negonneyeu8, kah weechayeumuk menuhkesuenuh nishwudt pasuk8e muttannonganog kussuoh.
E.17.14 And these are the numbers of them according to the house of their fathers: Of Judah, the captains of thousands; Adnah the chief, and with him mighty men of valour three hundred thousand.

α.17.15 Kah asukunkqutcheh, Jehohanan mugquomp, kah weechayeumok neese pasuk8e kah shwosuk tahshinchage muttannonganog kussuoh.
E.17.15 And next to him was Jehohanan the captain, and with him two hundred and fourscore thousand.

α.17.16 Kah asuhkonk Amasiah wunnaumonuh Zichri, noh weekontamwe maguk wuhhogkuh en Jehovah$ut, kah weechayeumuk neese pasuk8e muttannonganogkussuoh menuhkesuenuog.
E.17.16 And next him was Amasiah the son of Zichri, who willingly offered himself unto the LORD; and with him two hundred thousand mighty men of valour.

α.17.17 Kah wutch Benjaminit Eliada menuhkesuen, kah weechay[e]umuk, kenauwameenuh nashpe ahtompeh kah ogqunneganash, neese pasuk8e muttannonganog kussuoh.
E.17.17 And of Benjamin; Eliada a mighty man of valour, and with him armed men with bow and shield two hundred thousand.

α.17.18 Kah asuhkunk Jehosabadoh, kah weechayeumuk nequt pasuk8e & shwosuk tahshinchag muttannonganog kussuoh, pakodche quashweog wutch ayeuwuttuonk.
E.17.18 And next him was Jehozabad, and with him an hundred and fourscore thousand ready prepared for the war.

α.17.19 Yeu kenompamaog ketass8toh chabussinitcheh yeuh ketass8t pononcheh ut pummeneutausue otanashtu pannuppe wame Judah.
E.17.19 These waited on the king, beside those whom the king put in the fenced cities throughout all Judah.

α.18.1 KAh Jehosaphat wenaneetuongash kah quttianittuonk ohtóu m8cheke, kah weetauadtue nongk8tuog Ahaboh.
E.18.1 Now Jehoshaphat had riches and honour in abundance, and joined affinity with Ahab.

α.18.2 Kah mahtshunk nawhutche kodtum8ash, w8msu en Ahabut en Samaria, kah wunnehtauoh m8cheke shepsoh kah oxenoh, kah wutch missinninnúh neh weechógqutcheh, kah wunnupwéshanuh 8weeche kuhkuhk8mukqunat en Ramoth-Gilead.
E.18.2 And after certain years he went down to Ahab to Samaria. And Ahab killed sheep and oxen for him in abundance, and for the people that he had with him, and persuaded him to go up with him to Ramothgilead.

α.18.3 Kah Ahab Israelle ketass8t unnau Jehosaphat Judae ketass8toh, woh k8weecháeh en Ramoth-Gilead? kah wunnamp8hamauoh, nen netatupe ken, kah nummissinninnumog netatuppe kummissinninnúmog, kah k8weetomunnumun ut ayeuwuttinneat.
E.18.3 And Ahab king of Israel said unto Jehoshaphat king of Judah, Wilt thou go with me to Ramothgilead? And he answered him, I am as thou art, and my people as thy people; and we will be with thee in the war.

α.18.4 Kah Jehosaphat unnau Israelle ketass8toh, nat8tamwéhteash, k8wehquetumoush, wuttinn8wáonk Jehovah yeu kesukok.
E.18.4 And Jehoshaphat said unto the king of Israel, Enquire, I pray thee, at the word of the LORD to day.

α.18.5 Newaj Israelle ketass8t miyanau quoshodtumwaénuh yauut pasuk88oh wosketompuh, kah wuttinuh, sun woh nutaumun Ramoth-Gilead en ayeuwuttinneat, asuh sun nukkehchetuhhómu? kah nag n8waog, kuhkuhquish, newutche God pish upponamun ketass8t wunnutcheganit.
E.18.5 Therefore the king of Israel gathered together of prophets four hundred men, and said unto them, Shall we go to Ramothgilead to battle, or shall I forbear? And they said, Go up; for God will deliver it into the king's hand.

α.18.6 Qut Jehosaphat n8wau, sunnummatta yeu wutappein chippe ukquoshodtumwaéneumoh Jehovah, onk woh noh kenat8tomauóun?
E.18.6 But Jehoshaphat said, Is there not here a prophet of the LORD besides, that we might enquire of him?

α.18.7 Kah ketass8t unnau Jehosaphatoh, na onkatuk wosketomp, noh woh n[à]shpe nat8tomauogkut Jehovah: qut nussekeneau, newutche matta n8wáunne quoshodtumwanshik8, qut nagwutteáe machuk: ne nan Micajah wunnaumonuh Iimla: kah Jehosaphat n8wau, ketass8t ahque ne n8waj.
E.18.7 And the king of Israel said unto Jehoshaphat, There is yet one man, by whom we may enquire of the LORD: but I hate him; for he never prophesied good unto me, but always evil: the same is Micaiah the son of Imla. And Jehoshaphat said, Let not the king say so.

α.18.8 Kah Israelle ketass8t wehkomau pasuk8h wuttannohsuéneumoh, kah n8wau, teanuk nós8k Micajah wunnaumonuh Iimla.
E.18.8 And the king of Israel called for one of his officers, and said, Fetch quickly Micaiah the son of Imla.

α.18.9 Kah Israelle ketass8t, kah Jehosaphat Judae ketass8t appuog naneeswe ut wutappuongan8óut hogk8og ketass8tamwe hogk8ongash; kah appuog, chippe appuonganit ahhut petutteamuk Samarie squont, kah wame quoshodtumwaenúog, quoshodtumwog ut anaquabenit.
E.18.9 And the king of Israel and Jehoshaphat king of Judah sat either of them on his throne, clothed in their robes, and they sat in a void place at the entering in of the gate of Samaria; and all the prophets prophesied before them.

α.18.10 Neit Zedekiah wunnaumonuh Chenaanah, umm8ohshog quoshkonuhkauópuh, kah n8wau, yeu wussin Jehovah, nashpe yeug pish kukkonnukkéhtau Syria nô pajeh ummohtupaénaóont.
E.18.10 And Zedekiah the son of Chenaanah had made him horns of iron, and said, Thus saith the LORD, With these thou shalt push Syria until they be consumed.

α.18.11 Kah wame quoshodtumwaenuog ne wuttin quoshodtumuneau, n8waog, kuhkuhquish en Ramoth-Gilead, kah wunniish: newutche Jehovah pish ummagun en wunnutcheganit ketass8t.
E.18.11 And all the prophets prophesied so, saying, Go up to Ramothgilead, and prosper: for the LORD shall deliver it into the hand of the king.

α.18.12 Kah ann8naen noh wehkomont Micajahoh, ukken8nuh wuttinuh, kusseh, ukkutt8ongan8oash quoshodtumwaénuog wunnegenash ut ketass8tamut, nashpe nequtt8wáonk: yowutche, k8wehquetumoush, kuttinn8wáonk netatuppeyeuitch, ukkutt8wongan8out, kah n8w[a]sh wanegik.
E.18.12 And the messenger that went to call Micaiah spake to him, saying, Behold, the words of the prophets declare good to the king with one assent; let thy word therefore, I pray thee, be like one of their's, and speak thou good.

α.18.13 Kah Micaj[a]h n8wau, nean uppomantog Jehovah, uttoh num-Manitt8m an8adt ne nussin.
E.18.13 And Micaiah said, As the LORD liveth, even what my God saith, that will I speak.

α.18.14 Kah paont ketass8tamut, ketass8t wuttinuh, Micajah, sun woh nutaumun en Ramoth-Gilead, ayeuwuttinneat, asuh woh nukkehchetahhun? kah n8wau, kuhkuhquish kah wunniish, kah nag pish magununk en kenutcheganit.
E.18.14 And when he was come to the king, the king said unto him, Micaiah, shall we go to Ramothgilead to battle, or shall I forbear? And he said, Go ye up, and prosper, and they shall be delivered into your hand.

α.18.15 Kah ketass8t wuttinuh, toh woh kutteashish chadchekéeuwáhesh, matta teag kusséinadt qut ne wanumuhkuteyeuonk ut 8wesuonganit Jehovah?
E.18.15 And the king said to him, How many times shall I adjure thee that thou say nothing but the truth to me in the name of the LORD?

α.18.16 Neit n8wau nunnau wame Israel naswáiyeuog ut wadchuuhkontu, onatuh shepsog neg matta wananaushepsomégig, kah Jehovah n8wau, yeug matta wussontimó[8]éog, qushkehettich nish$noh pasuk en wekit, wunohteáe.
E.18.16 Then he said, I did see all Israel scattered upon the mountains, as sheep that have no shepherd: and the LORD said, These have no master; let them return therefore every man to his house in peace.

α.18.17 (Kah Israelle ketass8t unnau Jehosophatoh, sunnummatta kuttinnonop, matta noh n8nequoshodtumwanshik8, qut machuk)
E.18.17 And the king of Israel said to Jehoshaphat, Did I not tell thee that he would not prophesy good unto me, but evil?

α.18.18 Wonk n8wau, newutche n8tash wuttinn8waonk Jehovah: nunnau Lord, appu wutappuonganit kah wame kesukque kenauwameonk nepóoh wuttinuhkôunit, kah ummenadcheanit.
E.18.18 Again he said, Therefore hear the word of the LORD; I saw the LORD sitting upon his throne, and all the host of heaven standing on his right hand and on his left.

α.18.19 Kah Jehovah n8wau, howan woh napweshanont Ahaboh Israelle ketass8toh, onk woh kuhkuhqueu, kah woh penushau, ut Ramoth$Gilead? kah pasuk ket8kau, n8wau, yeu enneu, onkatuk ket8kau, n8wau, naunneu.
E.18.19 And the LORD said, Who shall entice Ahab king of Israel, that he may go up and fall at Ramothgilead? And one spake saying after this manner, and another saying after that manner.

α.18.20 Neit nashauonk sohham, kah neepau anaquabit Lord, kah n8wau, nen nupweshon, kah Jehovah wuttinuh, uttoh ut?
E.18.20 Then there came out a spirit, and stood before the LORD, and said, I will entice him. And the LORD said unto him, Wherewith?

α.18.21 Kah n8wau, nussohham, kah nuppann8wáeu nashauonganu, ut wutt8n8wóut wame ukquoshodtumwaéneumoh, kah Jehovah n8wau, pish kenupshan, kah pish kussohkau: sohhash kah ne ussish.
E.18.21 And he said, I will go out, and be a lying spirit in the mouth of all his prophets. And the Lord said, Thou shalt entice him, and thou shalt also prevail: go out, and do even so.

α.18.22 Newutche yeuyeu, Jehovah ponau pann8wae nashauonguh wutt8n8out, yeuh kukquoshodtumwaéneumoh: kah Jehovah kutayeuuhkonittue matche ken8nuk.
E.18.22 Now therefore, behold, the LORD hath put a lying spirit in the mouth of these thy prophets, and the LORD hath spoken evil against thee.

α.18.23 Neit Zedechiah wunnaumonuh Chenaanah pas8tshau, kah togkomau Micajahoh ut wann8nauut, kah n8wau, toh nogque wutónás nogkussit wunnashauanitt8moh Jehovah, kukken8nukqunat:
E.18.23 Then Zedekiah the son of Chenaanah came near, and smote Micaiah upon the cheek, and said, Which way went the Spirit of the LORD from me to speak unto thee?

α.18.24 Kah Micajah n8wau, kusseh, pish kenaumun ne kesukok, petutteaan keme chamberut puttogquean.
E.18.24 And Micaiah said, Behold, thou shalt see on that day when thou shalt go into an inner chamber to hide thyself.

α.18.25 Neit Israelle ketass8t n8wau, nemunuk Micajah, quehch8on8k en Amonut nanánuáen keitotanat, kah en Joashut ketass8t wunnaumonuh:
E.18.25 Then the king of Israel said, Take ye Micaiah, and carry him back to Amon the governor of the city, and to Joash the king's son;

α.18.26 Kah n8wagk yeu wussin ketass8t, yeuoh kuppishagkinok, kah assam8k unkquanumóe petukqunnunk, kah unkquanumóe nippe, nô pajeh n8nohteáe qushkenadt.
E.18.26 And say, Thus saith the king, Put this fellow in the prison, and feed him with bread of affliction and with water of affliction, until I return in peace.

α.18.27 Kah Micajah n8wau, wunnamuhkut wunohteáe qushkean, neit Jehovah matta ket8kóou nashpe nen, kah n8wau, n8tiegk wame missinninnúog.
E.18.27 And Micaiah said, If thou certainly return in peace, then hath not the LORD spoken by me. And he said, Hearken, all ye people.

α.18.28 Neit Israelle ketass8t, kah Jehosaphat Judae ketass8t, kuhkuhqueog en Ramoth-Gilead.
E.18.28 So the king of Israel and Jehoshaphat the king of Judah went up to Ramothgilead.

α.18.29 Kah Israelle ketass8t, unnau Jehosaphatoh, nuppen8wauwóhós, kah nuttom ayeuwuttinneat, qut hogqush kuppetwoshqushaongash, neit Israelle ketass8t penuwauuhwhósu, kah au ayeuwuttuonganit.
E.18.29 And the king of Israel said unto Jehoshaphat, I will disguise myself, and I will go to the battle; but put thou on thy robes. So the king of Israel disguised himself; and they went to the battle.

α.18.30 Kah Syriae ketass8t ann8nop wut-chariotse ummugquompuh, neh weetomukqutcheh, n8wau, ayeuhkonuhteok papeississitcheg asuh matikenukeg, webe Israelle ketass8t.
E.18.30 Now the king of Syria had commanded the captains of the chariots that were with him, saying, Fight ye not with small or great, save only with the king of Israel.

α.18.31 Kah niyeup chariotse mugquompaog nauahettit Jehosaphatoh, n8waog, noh Israelle ketass8t, newaj wéenuhkauwáhettit wutáyeuwuttinneaóont, qut Jehosaphat mishont8wau, kah Lord wuttannumauoh, kah God neh wutamáeáheuh.
E.18.31 And it came to pass, when the captains of the chariots saw Jehoshaphat, that they said, It is the king of Israel. Therefore they compassed about him to fight: but Jehoshaphat cried out, and the LORD helped him; and God moved them to depart from him.

α.18.32 Newutch n$niyeup, chariotse mugquompaog, wahteauhettit noh matta Israelle ketass8t, qushkeog wutch wunn8swehtahwhonaóont.
E.18.32 For it came to pass, that, when the captains of the chariots perceived that it was not the king of Israel, they turned back again from pursuing him.

α.18.33 Kah howae wosketomp nanwohtau, kah muswau Israelle ketass8toh ut nashaue adt wâadjishunk kenauwameonk, newaj unnont wutchariotse woksetompomoh, quinnupinish kenutcheg, onk woh kussohh8wuneh wutch ayeuhteáut, newutche nunn8chumwetáwhut.
E.18.33 And a certain man drew a bow at a venture, and smote the king of Israel between the joints of the harness: therefore he said to his chariot man, Turn thine hand, that thou mayest carry me out of the host; for I am wounded.

α.18.34 Kah nano missi ayeuwuttuonk ne kesukok: qut Israelle ketass8t, chetanunau ut wutchariotumut, ayeukonittue Syriansoh nô pajeh wunnonk8ut: kah papaume wayont nupp8.
E.18.34 And the battle increased that day: howbeit the king of Israel stayed himself up in his chariot against the Syrians until the even: and about the time of the sun going down he died.

α.19.1 KAh Jehosaphat Judae ketass8t, wunohteáe qushkeu en wekit en Jerusalem.
E.19.1 And Jehoshaphat the king of Judah returned to his house in peace to Jerusalem.

α.19.2 Kah Jehu wunnaumonuh Hanani naumwaenin sohham wunnogskauónat, kah unnau ketass8toh Jehosaphatoh, sun woh kutanninnumau matcheseaen, kah sun woh k8womun neg sekeneauoncheg Lordoh: newutche musquanittuonk kenuhkukunk wutch anaquabit Lord.
E.19.2 And Jehu the son of Hanani the seer went out to meet him, and said to king Jehoshaphat, Shouldest thou help the ungodly, and love them that hate the LORD? therefore is wrath upon thee from before the LORD.

α.19.3 Qut wanegugish kenamheunt, newutche kutamaunum kuppiyeuash wutch ohkeit, kah k8quagquashwunum kuttah kenatinneawhonat God.
E.19.3 Nevertheless there are good things found in thee, in that thou hast taken away the groves out of the land, and hast prepared thine heart to seek God.

α.19.4 Kah Jehosaphat ayeu Jerusalem, kah wonk sohham pañuppe missiñinnúhtu, wutch Beersheba, wehque Ephraime wadchuut, kah quehchuunau en Jehovahut um-Manitt8m8oh 8sh8oh.
E.19.4 And Jehoshaphat dwelt at Jerusalem: and he went out again through the people from Beersheba to mount Ephraim, and brought them back unto the LORD God of their fathers.

α.19.5 Kah ponau wussittumwaénúh ohkeit, pannuppe wame pummeneutausue keitotanáhtu ut Judah, kukkeitotanáeu.
E.19.5 And he set judges in the land throughout all the fenced cities of Judah, city by city,

α.19.6 Kah unnau wussittumwaénùh, nunnukqussek toh aséog, newutche matta k8sittumwanshomw8 wosketomp, qut Jehovah, noh wetomukqueóg ut wussittum8onganit.
E.19.6 And said to the judges, Take heed what ye do: for ye judge not for man, but for the LORD, who is with you in the judgment.

α.19.7 Newutche yeuyeu qusháonk Jehovah appehtunk8k, nunnukqussek, kah ussek, newutche na mo matcheseonganinno Jehovahut kum-Manitt8mun, asuh papenauánumóou howane, asuh mat neemunnum8 mag8onk.
E.19.7 Wherefore now let the fear of the LORD be upon you; take heed and do it: for there is no iniquity with the LORD our God, nor respect of persons, nor taking of gifts.

α.19.8 Kah wonk, ut Jerusalem, Jehosaphat ponau nawhutch Levitsoh, kah nawhutch sephausuéninnúh, kah nawhutch kehche wut8shinneunk ut Israel, wutche 8sittumóonk Jehovah, kah chann8waongash, nag quashkehettit en Jerusalem.
E.19.8 Moreover in Jerusalem did Jehoshaphat set of the Levites, and of the priests, and of the chief of the fathers of Israel, for the judgment of the LORD, and for controversies, when they returned to Jerusalem.

α.19.9 Kah noh ummeechumuhkonuh wuttinuh, yeu pish kuppabuhtanumwe usseneau, ut qushaonganit Jehovah, kah nashpe pannuppée metah.
E.19.9 And he charged them, saying, Thus shall ye do in the fear of the LORD, faithfully, and with a perfect heart.

α.19.10 Kah ne teag peyaonukqueóg wutch kematt8óut neg wadohkitcheg u[h]keitotanaóont, nashaue wasqueheonganit, nashaue naumatuonganit kah ann8team8onganit, kuhk8waongash kah wussittum8ongash, nag pish kutamoóog matta uppaneussehtauónaóont Jehovah: kah newaj musquanittuonk nuhkuhkongqueog, kah kematt8óog: yeu ussek, kah matta pish kuppanneusseumw8.
E.19.10 And what cause soever shall come to you of your brethren that dwell in your cities, between blood and blood, between law and commandment, statutes and judgments, ye shall even warn them that they trespass not against the LORD, and so wrath come upon you, and upon your brethren: this do, and ye shall not trespass.

α.19.11 Kah kusseh, Amariah negonne sephausuaen noh kenánawunukou, ut wame wuttinniyeuonganit Jehovah: kah Zebadiah wunnaumonuh Ishmael, nanaúnnuénin ut wekit Judah, wutche wame ketass8t wuttinniyeuognash; kah wonk Levitsog neg aninnohsuénuog ut anaquabeóg, wutt8anatamwe ussek, kah Jehovah wetomau wunneet8oh.
E.19.11 And, behold, Amariah the chief priest is over you in all matters of the LORD; and Zebadiah the son of Ishmael, the ruler of the house of Judah, for all the king's matters: also the Levites shall be officers before you. Deal courageously, and the LORD shall be with the good.

α.20.1 Kah n$nih yeu mahche n$nag, wunnaumonuh Moab, kah wunnaumonuh Ammon, kah nag weech ayeumukquog onkatogeh chabesitcheg Ammonitsoh, ayeuhkonôog Jehosophatoh.
E.20.1 It came to pass after this also, that the children of Moab, and the children of Ammon, and with them other beside the Ammonites, came against Jehoshaphat to battle.

α.20.2 Neit nawhutch peyaog anoncheg Jehosaphatoh, n8wáog, kutayeuuhkonittue peyaonuk mattaánukeg, wutch ongkoue kehtahhannit, wutuhshame Syria, kah kusseh, nag appuog Hazazon-Tamar ne Engedi.
E.20.2 Then there came some that told Jehoshaphat, saying, There cometh a great multitude against thee from beyond the sea on this side Syria; and, behold, they be in Hazazontamar, which is Engedi.

α.20.3 Kah Jehosaphat wabesu, kah ponau wuhhog natinneawhónat Jehovah, kah wahteauwáhuau mat meetseonk papashpe wame Judah.
E.20.3 And Jehoshaphat feared, and set himself to seek the LORD, and proclaimed a fast throughout all Judah.

α.20.4 Kah Judah miyaéog, 8wehquetumauónaóont Jehovah wutannumunkqunanóont, wutch wame Judae keitotanahtu, nag peyaog wunnatinneawhonaóont Jehovah.
E.20.4 And Judah gathered themselves together, to ask help of the LORD: even out of all the cities of Judah they came to seek the LORD.

α.20.5 Kah Jehosaphat neepau ut Judae, kah Jerusaleme mukkinneonganit, ut wekit Jehovah, anaquohtag wuske chippinneutunk.
E.20.5 And Jehoshaphat stood in the congregation of Judah and Jerusalem, in the house of the LORD, before the new court,

α.20.6 Kah n8wau, woi Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh n8shunónog, sunnummatta ken God ut kesukqut? kah sunnummatta kenanawunnum8 wame wutass8tam8ongash pen8wohteaog? kah ut kenutcheganit menuhkesuonk kah missugkenuonk, newaj matta howan tapenum8k kutayeuuhkonittue keneepauwehtunkqunat.
E.20.6 And said, O LORD God of our fathers, art not thou God in heaven? and rulest not thou over all the kingdoms of the heathen? and in thine hand is there not power and might, so that none is able to withstand thee?

α.20.7 Sunnummatta ken num-Manitt8mun, nph ama8hkauomp wadohkinitcheh yeu ohkeit wutch anaquabhettit kummissinninnumog Israel, jah kittinnumauónap 8skanneumuneuh Abraham ketomp, micheme.
E.20.7 Art not thou our God, who didst drive out the inhabitants of this land before thy people Israel, and gavest it to the seed of Abraham thy friend for ever?

α.20.8 Kah na wutaiinneau, kah na kuttit ayimunkquneau Sanctuarium wutche k8wesuonk, n8waog,
E.20.8 And they dwelt therein, and have built thee a sanctuary therein for thy name, saying,

α.20.9 Machuk nuhkuhkongqueog, togkodteg, wussittumóonk, asuh eninneáonk, asuh mahshagquodt, neepauéóog anaquohtag yeu wetu, ut anaquabean, (newutche k8wesuonk ohteau yeu wetuómut) kah mauunnitteauunóg ut nutuhquanum8onganunónut, neit pish ken8tam, kah kutannunos.
E.20.9 If, when evil cometh upon us, as the sword, judgment, or pestilence, or famine, we stand before this house, and in thy presence, (for thy name is in this house,) and cry unto thee in our affliction, then thou wilt hear and help.

α.20.10 Kah yeuyeu kusseh, wunnaumonuh Ammon, kah Moab, kah Seire wadchu, neh matta Israel ânánumóadcheh sohkok, sohhamwehettit wutch ohkeit Egypt, qut ukqushkehtauóuh, kah matta uppaguanóuh.
E.20.10 And now, behold, the children of Ammon and Moab and mount Seir, whom thou wouldest not let Israel invade, when they came out of the land of Egypt, but they turned from them, and destroyed them not;

α.20.11 Kusseh, uttoh nuttinunkquottunkqunan, uppeyonaóont nussohwhokónukqunnanónut wutch kutohtóonganit, ne anumiéog nutohtauunnanónut.
E.20.11 Behold, I say, how they reward us, to come to cast us out of thy possession, which thou hast given us to inherit.

α.20.12 Woi num-Manitt8mun sunnummatta woh k8sumóog? newutche matta n8menuhkesuonganeumun, ayeuuhkonittue yeug mattaánukeg, neg ayeuuhkonittue peyaonukqueagig, asuh matta n8wahteomun uttoh woh aséog, qut nuskesukqunnónash kuhkogkaeiyeu.
E.20.12 O our God, wilt thou not judge them? for we have no might against this great company that cometh against us; neither know we what to do: but our eyes are upon thee.

α.20.13 Kah wame Judah neepóog anaquabit Lord, nashpe ummukkiesum8uh kah ummittamwussúm8uh, kah wunneechan8uh.
E.20.13 And all Judah stood before the LORD, with their little ones, their wives, and their children.

α.20.14 Neit wunnashauanitt8moh Jehovah nuhkuhkunk Jahaziel, wunnaumonuh Zechariah, wunnaumonuh Benajah, wunnaumonuh Jehiel, wunnaumonuh Mattaniah, wul-Levit wutch wunnaumonat Asaph, ut nashaue mukkinneonganit.
E.20.14 Then upon Jahaziel the son of Zechariah, the son of Benaiah, the son of Jeiel, the son of Mattaniah, a Levite of the sons of Asaph, came the Spirit of the LORD in the midst of the congregation;

α.20.15 Kah n8wau, n8tam8k wame Judah, kah wadohkeógish Jerusalem, kah ken ketass8t Jehosaphat, yeu kuttukqun Jehovah, wabesehteógk, asuh chepsúhteóg, newutche yeug mataánukeg, newutche ayeuwuttuonk matta kuttaiheyeu, qut Jehovah.
E.20.15 And he said, Hearken ye, all Judah, and ye inhabitants of Jerusalem, and thou king Jehoshaphat, Thus saith the LORD unto you, Be not afraid nor dismayed by reason of this great multitude; for the battle is not yours, but God's.

α.20.16 Saup ayeuhkonittue w8mséhtok, kusseh, nag kuhkuhqueog, kishke w8msuonganit Ziz, kah nag pish kummishkôôog wéhqshik sepueṣus, anaquohtag Jeruelle touohkomuk.
E.20.16 To morrow go ye down against them: behold, they come up by the cliff of Ziz; and ye shall find them at the end of the brook, before the wilderness of Jeruel.

α.20.17 Ayeuteáteogk, 8nappek, neepo8k, kah naum8k 8wadchanuaonk Jehovah ut kuhhogkaóut, woi Judah kah Jerusalem, wabesehteogk, asuh chepsehteogk, saup nag ayeuuhkonittue sohwetók, newutche Jehovah k8wetomukou.
E.20.17 Ye shall not need to fight in this battle: set yourselves, stand ye still, and see the salvation of the LORD with you, O Judah and Jerusalem: fear not, nor be dismayed; to morrow go out against them: for the LORD will be with you.

α.20.18 Kah Jehosaphat nauwánum uppuhkuk, wuskesuk en ohkekontu, kah wame Judah, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, penusháog ut anaquabit Jehovah wowussumàog Jehovahoh.
E.20.18 And Jehoshaphat bowed his head with his face to the ground: and all Judah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem fell before the LORD, worshipping the LORD.

α.20.19 Kah Levitsog wunnaumonuh Kohathitsog, kah wunnaumonuh Korhitsog, neepoog woweenomonat Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, nashpe mishont8waonk, qunuhque.
E.20.19 And the Levites, of the children of the Kohathites, and of the children of the Korhites, stood up to praise the LORD God of Israel with a loud voice on high.

α.20.20 Kah nag nompoae omohkéog, k[a]h sohhamwog en Tekoae touohkomukqut, kah ne en sohhamwehettit, Jehosophat neepau kah n8wau, n8tiek woi Judah, kah kenaau wadohkeogish Jerusalem, wunnamptog Lord kum-Manitt8mw8, neit woh kuttinne menehkhetteaneau: wunnamptok ukquoshodtumwaeneumoh, neit pish k8niimw8.
E.20.20 And they rose early in the morning, and went forth into the wilderness of Tekoa: and as they went forth, Jehoshaphat stood and said, Hear me, O Judah, and ye inhabitants of Jerusalem; Believe in the LORD your God, so shall ye be established; believe his prophets, so shall ye prosper.

α.20.21 Kah keket8kauont missinninnuh, kehtimau ket8hamaenuh en Lordut, neg woh waeenodtukeg, wunneetupanatamwe wunneetuonk, nean sohhamohettit negonuhkauut ayeuhteáog, kah n8wonat, woweenomuk Jehovah newutche ummonanitteaonk michemohteau.
E.20.21 And when he had consulted with the people, he appointed singers unto the LORD, and that should praise the beauty of holiness, as they went out before the army, and to say, Praise the LORD; for his mercy endureth for ever.

α.20.22 Kah n8che ket8hamahettit, kah woween[ô]muonat, Jehovah wunnashau adhósuoh ayeuuhkonittue wunnaumonuh Ammon, Moab, kah Seire wadchu, neg ayeuuhkontogig Judah, kah nag togkom[o]og.
E.20.22 And when they began to sing and to praise, the LORD set ambushments against the children of Ammon, Moab, and mount Seir, which were come against Judah; and they were smitten.

α.20.23 Newutche wunnaumonuh Ammon, kah Moab, neg ayeuhkonittue neepauwehtauaog neh wadohkinitche wadchuut Seir, uppápaquanne nushonat, kah paguanonat, kah nag mahche paguanahettit wadohkinitche Seir, nag wame paguanittuog.
E.20.23 For the children of Ammon and Moab stood up against the inhabitants of mount Seir, utterly to slay and destroy them: and when they had made an end of the inhabitants of Seir, every one helped to destroy another.

α.20.24 Kah Judah pas8sukamohettit touohkomukque askuhwheteae kommuk, moninneauáog mataánutcheh, kah kusseh nag nuppee muhtogkuk penushaog en ohkekontu, kah wanne howan uppohquohham8.
E.20.24 And when Judah came toward the watch tower in the wilderness, they looked unto the multitude, and, behold, they were dead bodies fallen to the earth, and none escaped.

α.20.25 Kah Jehosophat kah ummissinninneumoh, paahettit wunneemunnumáoont, sequttahhamauaongánoash, nah wunnamehteauouh monatash wenauwetuongash kenugke nuppoe muhhogkuhtu, kah môgoadtue nompakouunash (nish amaunumauwahettiche wuhhogkauh) anue onk ne woh adtahshe monchadtauhettit: kah nishikkesukquae mukkinnumwog sequttahham8ongash, newutche monat.
E.20.25 And when Jehoshaphat and his people came to take away the spoil of them, they found among them in abundance both riches with the dead bodies, and precious jewels, which they stripped off for themselves, more than they could carry away: and they were three days in gathering of the spoil, it was so much.

α.20.26 Kah yauquinogkok, nag miyaeog ut Berachae 8nohkoiyeuut, newutche na wuttit wunnaumoneau Jehovahoh, newaj ne ayeuonk hettamuk Berachae 8nôuhkoi pajeh yeu kesukok.
E.20.26 And on the fourth day they assembled themselves in the valley of Berachah; for there they blessed the LORD: therefore the name of the same place was called, The valley of Berachah, unto this day.

α.20.27 Neit nag qushkeog nish$noh pasuk Judae & Jerusalem wosketomp, kah Jehoshaphat wunnegonuhkauuh wonk weekontamwe onat Jerusalem: newutche Jehovah 8wekontamwáheuh ut ummatwom8óut:
E.20.27 Then they returned, every man of Judah and Jerusalem, and Jehoshaphat in the forefront of them, to go again to Jerusalem with joy; for the LORD had made them to rejoice over their enemies.

α.20.28 Kah nag peyaog Jerusalem nashpe psalterisash kah harps[à]sh, kah monopuhpeguanash, en wekit Jehovah.
E.20.28 And they came to Jerusalem with psalteries and harps and trumpets unto the house of the LORD.

α.20.29 Kah qushaonk God nuhkuhkau wame wutohtimóine ketass8tam8ongash, n8tamwehettit Jehovah ayeuuhkonau ummatwom8oh Israel.
E.20.29 And the fear of God was on all the kingdoms of those countries, when they had heard that the LORD fought against the enemies of Israel.

α.20.30 Neit wutass8tamóonk Jehosaphat chequnohteau, newutche um-Manitt8moh anwôhsumwáhik waéenu.
E.20.30 So the realm of Jehoshaphat was quiet: for his God gave him rest round about.

α.20.31 Kah Jehoshaphat ketass8tam88 ut Judah: noh nishwinchage kah napanna tahshe kodtumwohkom n8che ketass8tam8it, kah nesnehchage kah napanna tahshe kodtumwae ut Jerusalem, kah ohkasoh ussowesu Azubah, wuttaunoh Shilhi.
E.20.31 And Jehoshaphat reigned over Judah: he was thirty and five years old when he began to reign, and he reigned twenty and five years in Jerusalem. And his mother's name was Azubah the daughter of Shilhi.

α.20.32 Kah pomushau ummayit Asa 8shoh, kah matta wunnukkodtum8un; usseup ne sampwagk ut anaquabit Jehovah.
E.20.32 And he walked in the way of Asa his father, and departed not from it, doing that which was right in the sight of the LORD.

α.20.33 Qut qunuhqui ayeuongash matta amaunum8unash: newutche missiñinnúog asquam quoshwehtamóog wuttahh8óash, en um-Manitt8m8óut 8sh8óuh.
E.20.33 Howbeit the high places were not taken away: for as yet the people had not prepared their hearts unto the God of their fathers.

α.20.34 Kah onkatogish wutusseongash Jehoshaphat, negonne kah maumachish, kusseh wussukwhósuash ut 8sukuhwhonganit Jehu, wunnaumonuh Hanani, noh mâsohwhut ut 8sukuhwhongan8úut, ISraelle ketass8tamwog.
E.20.34 Now the rest of the acts of Jehoshaphat, first and last, behold, they are written in the book of Jehu the son of Hanani, who is mentioned in the book of the kings of Israel.

α.20.35 Kah mahche yeu n$nag, Jehosophat Judae ketass8t, weech8hamau Ahaziahoh Israelle ketass8t, noh ahche macheseit.
E.20.35 And after this did Jehoshaphat king of Judah join himself with Ahaziah king of Israel, who did very wickedly:

α.20.36 Kah 8weech8humuh ayimunat keiht8nogquash ônat Tarshish, kah ayimwog keiht8nogquash ut Ezion$Geber.
E.20.36 And he joined himself with him to make ships to go to Tarshish: and they made the ships in Eziongaber.

α.20.37 Neit Eliezer wunnaumonuh Dodavah wutch Mareshah, ayeuuhkonittue quoshodtumomau Jehoshaphatoh, n8wau, newutche k8weech8hum Ahaziah, Jehovah pohquenum kutanakausuongash, kah keit8nogquash pokshaash, newaj n8nanumwéhettit onat Tarshish.
E.20.37 Then Eliezer the son of Dodavah of Mareshah prophesied against Jehoshaphat, saying, Because thou hast joined thyself with Ahaziah, the LORD hath broken thy works. And the ships were broken, that they were not able to go to Tarshish.

α.21.1 NEit Jehoshaphat weesequom8mau 8shoh kah posekinau weeche 8sh ut ukkeitotanat David: kah Jehoramoh wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tamomukquoh.
E.21.1 Now Jehoshaphat slept with his fathers, and was buried with his fathers in the city of David. And Jehoram his son reigned in his stead.

α.21.2 Kah wematoh wunnaumonuh Jehoshaphat, Azariah, kah Jehiel, kah Zechariah, kah Azáriah, kah Michael, kah Shephatiah, wame yeuh wunnaumonuh Jehosophat, Israelle ketass8t.
E.21.2 And he had brethren the sons of Jehoshaphat, Azariah, and Jehiel, and Zechariah, and Azariah, and Michael, and Shephatiah: all these were the sons of Jehoshaphat king of Israel.

α.21.3 Kah 8sh8uh aninnumunkquog mishe silvere kah Golde mag8ongash, kah mâgoadtikish, nashpe pummeneutausue keitotanash ut Judah: qut ass8tamóonk aninnumauau Jehoramoh, newutche mohtamétu.
E.21.3 And their father gave them great gifts of silver, and of gold, and of precious things, with fenced cities in Judah: but the kingdom gave he to Jehoram; because he was the firstborn.

α.21.4 Kah Jehoram waábit ut wutass8tam8onganit 8shoh, menehkheau wuhhogkuh, kah nushau wame wematuh nashpe togkodteg kah wonk nawhutche Israelle sontimóog,
E.21.4 Now when Jehoram was risen up to the kingdom of his father, he strengthened himself, and slew all his brethren with the sword, and divers also of the princes of Israel.

α.21.5 Jehoram nishwinchage k[u]h neeswe kodtumwohkom n8che ketass8tam8it, kah shwosuk tahshe kodtumwae ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem.
E.21.5 Jehoram was thirty and two years old when he began to reign, and he reigned eight years in Jerusalem.

α.21.6 Kah pomushau ummayeuout Israelle ketass8tamwog onatuh wek8 Ahab, newutche ummittamwussu wuttaunoh Ahab, kah ussu ne machuk ut anaquabit Jehovah.
E.21.6 And he walked in the way of the kings of Israel, like as did the house of Ahab: for he had the daughter of Ahab to wife: and he wrought that which was evil in the eyes of the LORD.

α.21.7 Qut Jehovah matta paguodtoou wek David, newu[t]che wunn8waonk ne ayimauomp Davidoh, kah neane quoshomomp, wuttinnumauonat, wequananteg, kah wunnaumonuh micheme.
E.21.7 Howbeit the LORD would not destroy the house of David, because of the covenant that he had made with David, and as he promised to give a light to him and to his sons for ever.

α.21.8 Ut ukkesukodtumut Edomitsog amaéog wutch agwe wunnutcheganit Judah: kah ketass8tamuhkonaog wuhhogkauh.
E.21.8 In his days the Edomites revolted from under the dominion of Judah, and made themselves a king.

α.21.9 Neit Jehoram sohham wutch wussontimosumuh, kah wame wutchariotsumash, kah neepau nukonaeu, kah togkomau Edomitsoh neh weenuhkunkqutcheh, kah chariotse Mugquompaog.
E.21.9 Then Jehoram went forth with his princes, and all his chariots with him: and he rose up by night, and smote the Edomites which compassed him in, and the captains of the chariots.

α.21.10 Nemehkuh Edomitsog amaeog wutch agwe wunnutcheganit Judah pajeh yeu kesukok, nenan wonk ahquompak Libnah amaeu wutch agwe wunn[u]tcheganit, newutche ohquanumau 8shoh um-Manitt8moh.
E.21.10 So the Edomites revolted from under the hand of Judah unto this day. The same time also did Libnah revolt from under his hand; because he had forsaken the LORD God of his fathers.

α.21.11 Nano, ayim qunuhqui ayeuongash ut Judae wadchuuhkontu, kah nanwun8dsuasuaheau wadohkinitcheh Jerusalem, kah chetimau Judahoh.
E.21.11 Moreover he made high places in the mountains of Judah and caused the inhabitants of Jerusalem to commit fornication, and compelled Judah thereto.

α.21.12 Kah na wuttit peyaonukqun wussukwhonk wutch Elijah quoshodumwaen, n8wom8, yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh David k8sh, newutche matta kuppomshoh ut ummayit Jehoshaphat k8sh, asuh matta en ummayut Asa Judae ketass8t.
E.21.12 And there came a writing to him from Elijah the prophet, saying, Thus saith the LORD God of David thy father, Because thou hast not walked in the ways of Jehoshaphat thy father, nor in the ways of Asa king of Judah,

α.21.13 Qut kuppomusham ummayeuout Israelle ketass8tamwog kah Judah, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, kenanwun8dsquaáusuaheóog, netatupe nanwun8dsquaausuongash wek Ahab, kah wonk kenush kematog wutch k8sh wekit, neg aneúkunkqueaneg.
E.21.13 But hast walked in the way of the kings of Israel, and hast made Judah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem to go a whoring, like to the whoredoms of the house of Ahab, and also hast slain thy brethren of thy father's house, which were better than thyself:

α.21.14 Kusseh, nashpe mishe togkodtuonk, Jehovah pish togkomau kummissinninneumoh, kah keneechanog, kah kummittamwussog kah wame kummaumachiyeumash.
E.21.14 Behold, with a great plague will the LORD smite thy people, and thy children, and thy wives, and all thy goods:

α.21.15 Kah ken pish kummishe mahchinam, nashpe taninneáonk menugkussit, nô pajeh kenogkus penushont wutche mahchináonk asekesukokish,
E.21.15 And thou shalt have great sickness by disease of thy bowels, until thy bowels fall out by reason of the sickness day by day.

α.21.16 Nano, Jehovah ayeuuhkonittue wogkouinau wunnashauongan8ooh Philistiansog Jehoramoh, kah Arabiansog kishke Ethiopiansog.
E.21.16 Moreover the LORD stirred up against Jehoram the spirit of the Philistines, and of the Arabians, that were near the Ethiopians:

α.21.17 Kah nag kuhkuhqueog en Judah kah uppohkuppúnauúnau, kah amáunumwog maumachiyeuash nish nampteomukish ut ketass8t wekit, kah wonk wunnaumonuh kah ummittamwussoh: newaj matta pasuk8 wunnaumonuh ushqunumauau webe Jehoahaz ummuttasonsuh.
E.21.17 And they came up into Judah, and brake into it, and carried away all the substance that was found in the king's house, and his sons also, and his wives; so that there was never a son left him, save Jehoahaz, the youngest of his sons.

α.21.18 Kah mahche wame yeu n$nag Jehovah wuttogkomuh ut wunnogkussit nashpe matta na neetskeseumuk mahchinaonk.
E.21.18 And after all this the LORD smote him in his bowels with an incurable disease.

α.21.19 Kah n$niyeup, chekeyeu8k, mahche neese kodtum8uk, wunnogkus penusheau nashpe ummahchinaonk: neit nupp8 nashpe mishe mahchinaongash kah ummissinninneumoh matta wutchikkusumwanshik8oh, neane wutchikohsum8ongash 8sh8oh.
E.21.19 And it came to pass, that in process of time, after the end of two years, his bowels fell out by reason of his sickness: so he died of sore diseases. And his people made no burning for him, like the burning of his fathers.

α.21.20 Nishwinchage kah neese kodtumwohkom n8che ketass8tam8mit, kah ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem shwosuk tahshe kodtumwae, kah amaeu wanne kodtanum[ó]ont: qut upposekinouh ut ukkeitotanat David qut matta 8weenohkeóonk ketass8tamwog.
E.21.20 Thirty and two years old was he when he began to reign, and he reigned in Jerusalem eight years, and departed without being desired. Howbeit they buried him in the city of David, but not in the sepulchres of the kings.

α.22.1 KAh wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, Ahaziah ummuttasonsoh wunnompe ketass8tamuhkonauh: newutche kenauwameénuog neg weeche peyomoncheg Arabiansoh en tuppuksinn8wonganit nushaog wame mohtomeginitcheh, neit Ahaziah wunnaumonuh Jehoram Judae ketass8t ketass8tam88.
E.22.1 And the inhabitants of Jerusalem made Ahaziah his youngest son king in his stead: for the band of men that came with the Arabians to the camp had slain all the eldest. So Ahaziah the son of Jehoram king of Judah reigned.

α.22.2 Ahazia yauunchage kah neese kodtumwohkom, n8che ketass8tam8it, kah neese kodtumwae ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem, kah ohkasoh ussowesuoh Athaliah wuttaunoh Omri.
E.22.2 Forty and two years old was Ahaziah when he began to reign, and he reigned one year in Jerusalem. His mother's name also was Athaliah the daughter of Omri.

α.22.3 Noh wonk pomushau ummayit wek Ahab: newutche ohkasoh neh ukken8nuaeneumoh, matchesenat.
E.22.3 He also walked in the ways of the house of Ahab: for his mother was his counsellor to do wickedly.

α.22.4 Newaj matcheseit ut anaquabit Jehovah netatuppé wek Ahab: newutche nah ukken8nuaeneumoh, mahche nupinit 8shoh, en wunnuppoonganit.
E.22.4 Wherefore he did evil in the sight of the LORD like the house of Ahab: for they were his counsellors after the death of his father to his destruction.

α.22.5 Kah wonk noh n8swuhkom nag ukken8s8waongan8, kah weechau Jehoramoh wunnaumonuh Ahab, Israelle ketass8t ayeuuhkononat Hazael Syriae ketass8t, ut Ramoth$Gilead, kah Syriansog togkomaog Joramoh.
E.22.5 He walked also after their counsel, and went with Jehoram the son of Ahab king of Israel to war against Hazael king of Syria at Ramothgilead: and the Syrians smote Joram.

α.22.6 Kah qushkeu netskeheonat ut Jezreel, newutche nish ain n8chumwetahwutche ut Ramah ayeuuhkonont Hazaeloh Syriae ketass8toh, kah Azariah wunnaumonuh Jehoram, Judae ketass8t, w8msu nauonat Jehoram wunnaumonuh Ahab ut Jezreel, newutche mahchinau.
E.22.6 And he returned to be healed in Jezreel because of the wounds which were given him at Ramah, when he fought with Hazael king of Syria. And Azariah the son of Jehoram king of Judah went down to see Jehoram the son of Ahab at Jezreel, because he was sick.

α.22.7 Kah wuttinineaonk Ahaziah wutch ayeu8 Godut, nashpe uppeyaononat Joramoh, newutche paont, ayeuuhkonittue Jehuoh wunnaumonuh Nimshi weeche sohham8mau Jehoramoh, noh Jehovah sussequnop tummethamunat wek Ahab.
E.22.7 And the destruction of Ahaziah was of God by coming to Joram: for when he was come, he went out with Jehoram against Jehu the son of Nimshi, whom the LORD had anointed to cut off the house of Ahab.

α.22.8 Kah nniyeup, Jehu asit wussittumóonk ut wekit Ahab, kah namheont Judae sontimoh, kah wunnaumonauh wematoh Ahaziah, neg wadtiñinneumuhkauoncheg Ahazioh.
E.22.8 And it came to pass, that, when Jehu was executing judgment upon the house of Ahab, and found the princes of Judah, and the sons of the brethren of Ahaziah, that ministered to Ahaziah, he slew them.

α.22.9 Kah natinnewhau Ahaziahoh, kah wuttohqunouh (Newutche puttogqueu ut Samaria) kah uppaudtauonauh Jehuoh, kah nushahettit upposekinouh n8waog, newutche yeuh wunnaumonuh Jehosophat noh natinneawhont Jehovahoh nashpe mámusse metah, neit wek Ahaziah matta umménuhkesuonganu ashpumme ohtauunat ass8tamóonk.
E.22.9 And he sought Ahaziah: and they caught him, (for he was hid in Samaria,) and brought him to Jehu: and when they had slain him, they buried him: Because, said they, he is the son of Jehoshaphat, who sought the LORD with all his heart. So the house of Ahaziah had no power to keep still the kingdom.

α.22.10 Qut Athaliah ohkasoh Ahaziah, nag* wunnaumoniuh nupp8i neepau,
E.22.10 But when Athaliah the mother of Ahaziah saw that her son was dead, she arose and destroyed all the seed royal of the house of Judah.

α.22.11 Qut Jehoshabeath wuttaunoh ketass8t nemunau Joashoh wunnaumonuh Ahaziah, kah komm8tinuh wutch kenugke wunnaumonat ketass8t neg nashomukeg, kah upponuh, kah neh nanukkehikqutcheh, appinneáe chamberut, nemehkuh Jehoshabeath wuttaunoh ketass8t Jehoram, ummittamwussoh Jehojada sephausuwaen (newutche neh weetompasu Ahaziah) wutattashuh wutch Athaliahut, newaj matta nushunk.
E.22.11 But Jehoshabeath, the daughter of the king, took Joash the son of Ahaziah, and stole him from among the king's sons that were slain, and put him and his nurse in a bedchamber. So Jehoshabeath, the daughter of king Jehoram, the wife of Jehoiada the priest, (for she was the sister of Ahaziah,) hid him from Athaliah, so that she slew him not.

α.22.12 Kah nah 8wetomuh attahshau ut God wekit nequtta tahshe kodtumwáe, kah Athaliah keichesonksquoou ut ohkeit.
E.22.12 And he was with them hid in the house of God six years: and Athaliah reigned over the land.

α.23.1 KAh nesausuk adtahshe kodtum8k, Jehojada menehkheau wuhhogkuh, kah neumunau pasuk8e mugquompuh, Azariah wunnaumonuh Jeroham, Ishmael wunnaumonuh Jehohanan, kah Azariah wunnaumonuh Obed, kah Maasiah wunnaumonuh Adajah, kah Elishaphat wunnaumonuh Zichri, 8n8wonáuh.
E.23.1 And in the seventh year Jehoiada strengthened himself, and took the captains of hundreds, Azariah the son of Jeroham, and Ishmael the son of Jehohanan, and Azariah the son of Obed, and Maaseiah the son of Adaiah, and Elishaphat the son of Zichri, into covenant with him.
