α.23.2 Kah papaumshaog Judah, kah miyanáog Levitsoh wutch wame wut8tanaôont Judah, kah kehche wut8shinneunk ut Israel, kah nag peyaog Jerusalem.
E.23.2 And they went about in Judah, and gathered the Levites out of all the cities of Judah, and the chief of the fathers of Israel, and they came to Jerusalem.

α.23.3 Kah wame mukkinnéonk wunn8wáog ketass8toh ut wekit God, kah nah wuttinuh, kusseh, ketass8t wunnaumonuh pish ketass8tam88, nean8wop Jehovah papaume wunnaumonuh David.
E.23.3 And all the congregation made a covenant with the king in the house of God. And he said unto them, Behold, the king's son shall reign, as the LORD hath said of the sons of David.

α.23.4 Yeu woh kutusseneau, kenaau nashwe chippeógish petutteaog ut Sabath$dayut, sephausuénuog, kah Levitsog, nanausquontamagk.
E.23.4 This is the thing that ye shall do; A third part of you entering on the sabbath, of the priests and of the Levites, shall be porters of the doors;

α.23.5 Kah nashwe chippissitcheg appek ketass8t wekit, kah nashwe chippissitcheg ut quenohtage squont, kah wame missinninnuog appehettich chippinnutonganehtu wekit Jehovah.
E.23.5 And a third part shall be at the king's house; and a third part at the gate of the foundation: and all the people shall be in the courts of the house of the LORD.

α.23.6 Qut howan peyunkitch wekit Jehovah, webe sephausuénuog, kah neg Levitsog wadtinninneumuhkausitcheg, nag pish petutteaog newutche[,] nag wunneetupanatamweyeu8og: uqt wame missinninnúog nanawehteauhettich wutuskuhwheteaonk Jehovah. 
E.23.6 But let none come into the house of the LORD, save the priests, and they that minister of the Levites; they shall go in, for they are holy: but all the people shall keep the watch of the LORD.

α.23.7 Kah Levitsog pish wéenuhkauwaog ketass8toh nish$noh wosketomp wutauwohteaonk wunnutcheganit, kah howan onkatuk petutteadt wetuómut, pish nushau: qut kenaau wetom8k ketass8t petutteadt, kah sohhog.
E.23.7 And the Levites shall compass the king round about, every man with his weapons in his hand; and whosoever else cometh into the house, he shall be put to death: but be ye with the king when he cometh in, and when he goeth out.

α.23.8 Neit Levitsog kah wame Judah usseog neaunak wame ne Jehojada sephausuen ann8teamwit: kah nag neemunáog nishnoh pasuk, 8wosketomp8moh, neg woh petutteacheg Sabath$dayeu, keeche nag woh sohhogig Sabath$dayeu, newutche Jehojada sephausuen, matta moncheahtóou wunohtóongash.
E.23.8 So the Levites and all Judah did according to all things that Jehoiada the priest had commanded, and took every man his men that were to come in on the sabbath, with them that were to go out on the sabbath: for Jehoiada the priest dismissed not the courses.

α.23.9 Wonk Jehojada sephausuen aninnumauau pasuk8e mugquompuh, qunuhtugquash kah buklersash kah ogqunegash, nish wadtiehépash ketass8t David, nish ohtagish wekit God.
E.23.9 Moreover Jehoiada the priest delivered to the captains of hundreds spears, and bucklers, and shields, that had been king David's, which were in the house of God.

α.23.10 Kah wunnashau wame missinninnúh (nishnoh pasuk wutauwohteaonk ut wunnutcheganit) wutch muttinuhkôuneiyeue templeut, wehque menadcheunniyeue templeut, kishke altarut kah templeut, kishke ketass8tamwut waéenu.
E.23.10 And he set all the people, every man having his weapon in his hand, from the right side of the temple to the left side of the temple, along by the altar and the temple, by the king round about.

α.23.11 Neit sohh8wunáog ketass8t wunnaumonáuh, kah upponamauóuh chetukquab, kah wauwáonk, kah ukketass8tamuhkonuh: kah Jehojada kah wunnaumonuh sussequnóuh, kah n8wáog, Ketass8t pomontaj.
E.23.11 Then they brought out the king's son, and put upon him the crown, and gave him the testimony, and made him king. And Jehoiada and his sons anointed him, and said, God save the king.

α.23.12 Kah Athaliah n8tog 8wadtàuatonkqussuongan8 missinninnúog, quagquehettit waweeuomáhettit ketass8tamwoh, noh peyaonau missinninnúh ut wekit Jehovah.
E.23.12 Now when Athaliah heard the noise of the people running and praising the king, she came to the people into the house of the LORD:

α.23.13 Kah natawompu kah kusseh, ketass8t neepau kishke wunneepattunkquonganit, ahhut petutteamuk, kah sontimóog, kah monopuhpegquaénuog kishke ketass8tut, kah wame missinninnúog ne ohkeit muskouanatamwog, kah monopuhpequáog: wonk kodt8homoncheg, nashpe wunónt8wae auwohteaongash, kah neg kohk8tomauutcheg wowénomae ketahom[á]onk: neit Athaliah nehnegukom wuthogk8unash, kah n8wau, wunnombeukohteaonk wunnombeukohteaonk.
E.23.13 And she looked, and, behold, the king stood at his pillar at the entering in, and the princes and the trumpets by the king: and all the people of the land rejoiced, and sounded with trumpets, also the singers with instruments of musick, and such as taught to sing praise. Then Athaliah rent her clothes, and said, Treason, Treason.

α.23.14 Neit Jehojada sephausuen, sohh8wunau pasuk8e mugquompuh, neg nanawunnumwáitcheg: chippan8oh, kah nah wuttinuh, sohh8wunok wutch ussukkompóonganit, kah howan asukauont nushonch nashpe togkodteg newutche sephausuen anwop ahque nush8k ut wekit Jehovah.
E.23.14 Then Jehoiada the priest brought out the captains of hundreds that were set over the host, and said unto them, Have her forth of the ranges: and whoso followeth her, let him be slain with the sword. For the priest said, Slay her not in the house of the LORD.

α.23.15 Neit wuttohqunóuh, kah paont ahhut petutteamuk horsese squont, kishke ketass8t wekit na wuttit nushoneau.
E.23.15 So they laid hands on her; and when she was come to the entering of the horse gate by the king's house, they slew her there.

α.23.16 Kah Jehojada 8n8wonáuh nashaue nagum, kah nashawe wame missinninnúog, kah nashaue ketass8tamut, nag woh Jehovah 8missinninneumuneat.
E.23.16 And Jehoiada made a covenant between him, and between all the people, and between the king, that they should be the LORD's people.

α.23.17 Kah wame missinninnúog auog wekit Baal, kah wussóquttahhamuneau, kah soquttahhamauouh wut-altarumash, kah wuttinneukontunkoh, kah nusháog Mattanoh wussephausuéneumoh Baal, ut anaquohtag altarash.
E.23.17 Then all the people went to the house of Baal, and brake it down, and brake his altars and his images in pieces, and slew Mattan the priest of Baal before the altars.

α.23.18 Wonk Jehojada kehtimau aninnohsuénúh ut wekit Jehov[à]h, nashpe wunnutchegan8óut sephausuénuog kah Levitsog, neh David kéhtimoncheh ut wekit Lord, sephamauónat chikohtae mag8ongash en Lordut, neansukwhosik ut wuttinnaumatuonganit Moses, nashpe wekontamóonk kah keta8hamáonk, nashpe wunnutcheganit David.
E.23.18 Also Jehoiada appointed the offices of the house of the LORD by the hand of the priests the Levites, whom David had distributed in the house of the LORD, to offer the burnt offerings of the LORD, as it is written in the law of Moses, with rejoicing and with singing, as it was ordained by David.

α.23.19 Kah noh ponau nanausquontaménúh, ut squontamehtu wekit Jehovah; wanne howan noh nishqueneunkqussit ne teag nashpe woh petutteaou.
E.23.19 And he set the porters at the gates of the house of the LORD, that none which was unclean in any thing should enter in.

α.23.20 Kah neemunau nequt pasuk8e mugquompuh, kah kehtauáog, kah nanawunnuénuog ut missinninnúut, kah wame missinninnuog ut ohkeit, kah nag womuss[uu]naog ketass8toh wutch wekit Jehovah, kah pannupwush[à]og qunuhqui squontamut en ketass8t wekit, kah ponáog ketass8toh ketass8tamwáe appuonganit.
E.23.20 And he took the captains of hundreds, and the nobles, and the governors of the people, and all the people of the land, and brought down the king from the house of the LORD: and they came through the high gate into the king's house, and set the king upon the throne of the kingdom.

α.23.21 Kah wame missinninnúog ne ohkeit wekontamog, kah keitotan chequnohteau, mahche nushahettit Athaliahoh nashpe togkodteg.
E.23.21 And all the people of the land rejoiced: and the city was quiet, after that they had slain Athaliah with the sword.

α.24.1 IOash nesausuk tahshe kodtumwohkom n8che ketass8tam8it, kah yauunchage kodtumwáe ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem: wonk ohkasoh ussowesu Zibiah wutch Beersheba.
E.24.1 Joash was seven years old when he began to reign, and he reigned forty years in Jerusalem. His mother's name also was Zibiah of Beersheba.

α.24.2 Kah Joash usseu ne sampwag ut anaquabit Jehovah, nisohkepomontog Jehojada sephausuenin.
E.24.2 And Joash did that which was right in the sight of the LORD all the days of Jehoiada the priest.

α.24.3 Kah Jehojada wunnees8kauáheuh, kah wunnaumonieu, kah wuttauneu.
E.24.3 And Jehoiada took for him two wives; and he begat sons and daughters.

α.24.4 Kah n$niyeup mahche yeu n$nag, Joash unnantam onchteauunat wek Jehovah.
E.24.4 And it came to pass after this, that Joash was minded to repair the house of the LORD.

α.24.5 Kah miyanau sephausu[é]núh kah Levitsoh, kah nah wuttinuh, sohham8k en Judae keitotanahtu, kah pummunum8k wutch wame Israelut, teaguash onchteauunat wek kum-Manitt8mw8 wutch kogkodtumwáe kah naum8k kukkenuppe ussenaóont, qut Levitsog matta ukkenuppe usseneau.
E.24.5 And he gathered together the priests and the Levites, and said to them, Go out unto the cities of Judah, and gather of all Israel money to repair the house of your God from year to year, and see that ye hasten the matter. Howbeit the Levites hastened it not.

α.24.6 Kah ketass8t wehkomau Jehojadahoh kahcheyeuunitcheh, kah wuttinuh, tohwutch matta wehquetumauóadt Levitsog, petakodtauunat uppummenum8ongan8ash wutch Judah, kah wutch Jerusalem, nean8wadt Moses[,] wuttinneumoh Jehovah: kah wutch Israelle mukkinneonganit, wutche wauwáe tabernakle?
E.24.6 And the king called for Jehoiada the chief, and said unto him, Why hast thou not required of the Levites to bring in out of Judah and out of Jerusalem the collection, according to the commandment of Moses the servant of the LORD, and of the congregation of Israel, for the tabernacle of witness?

α.24.7 Newutche wunnaumonuh Athaliah noh matcheetowae mittumwossis, nag soquetahhamwog wek God, kah wonk wame waneetupanatamwahteómukish wekit Jehovah, nash wuttinnumauáoash Baalim.
E.24.7 For the sons of Athaliah, that wicked woman, had broken up the house of God; and also all the dedicated things of the house of the LORD did they bestow upon Baalim.

α.24.8 Kah ketass8t ann8teamit, ayimwog chest, kah poquodchit upponamuneau, ut squontamut Jehovah wekit.
E.24.8 And at the king's commandment they made a chest, and set it without at the gate of the house of the LORD.

α.24.9 Kah wahteauwáhuwaog pannuppe Judah kah Jerusalem, paudtauunat pumminnum8onk Lordut, ne Moses wuttinneumoh God anann8homp Israeloh ut touohkomukqut.
E.24.9 And they made a proclamation through Judah and Jerusalem, to bring in to the LORD the collection that Moses the servant of God laid upon Israel in the wilderness.

α.24.10 Kah wame sontimóog, kah wame missinninnúog, wekontamwog kah petukodtóog, kah uppetuhkoneau chestut nô pajeh ummahche ussenaóont.
E.24.10 And all the princes and all the people rejoiced, and brought in, and cast into the chest, until they had made an end.

α.24.11 Kah n$niyeup, na ahquompak chest pas8it ketass8t wutannohsuonganit, nashpe wunnutchegan8óut Levitsog, kah nag namohettit monatash teaguash, ketass8t wus-Scribumoh, kah kehche sephausuen wutannohsuéneumoh, peyaog, kah sequnáog chestoh, kah wunnunnumunáoash, kah wonk wutuss8wuttauuneau en wutayeuonganit, yeu wutusseneau asekesukokish, kah m8cheke pumminnumwog teaguash.
E.24.11 Now it came to pass, that at what time the chest was brought unto the king's office by the hand of the Levites, and when they saw that there was much money, the king's scribe and the high priest's officer came and emptied the chest, and took it, and carried it to his place again. Thus they did day by day, and gathered money in abundance.

α.24.12 Kah ketass8t, kah Jehojada, wuttinnumauóneau wuttinneume anakausuonk wekit Jehovah, kah ann8náog masonsoh, kah carpentersoh onchteauunat Jehovah wek: kah wame neg anakausuetunkig missehchuog kah brasse, onchteauunat wek Jehovah.
E.24.12 And the king and Jehoiada gave it to such as did the work of the service of the house of the LORD, and hired masons and carpenters to repair the house of the LORD, and also such as wrought iron and brass to mend the house of the LORD.

α.24.13 Neit anakausuitcheg anakausuog, kah anakausuonk wunnehteauun nashpe nag; kah wunnehteauog wek God, kah ummenuhkehtineau.
E.24.13 So the workmen wrought, and the work was perfected by them, and they set the house of God in his state, and strengthened it.

α.24.14 Kah kesteauhettit, nag paudtóog teaguash nish asqsheunkish, ut anaquabhettit ketass8t, kah Jehojada, ne wunnashpe ayimuneau wishquash wutch wekit Jehovah, wuttinneumuhkausue auwohteaongash, kah mag8e auwohteaongash, kah kenamóog, kah golde kah silvere auwohteaongash, kah nag mag8og chikohtae mag8ongash ut wekit Jehovah nagwutteáeu, nisahkepomontog Jehojada.
E.24.14 And when they had finished it, they brought the rest of the money before the king and Jehoiada, whereof were made vessels for the house of the LORD, even vessels to minister, and to offer withal, and spoons, and vessels of gold and silver. And they offered burnt offerings in the house of the LORD continually all the days of Jehoiada.

α.24.15 Qut Jehojada nano kechisu8, kah numwohteau kesukodtumash napuk; nequt pasuk8, kah nishwinchage kodtumwohkom ne nápuk.
E.24.15 But Jehoiada waxed old, and was full of days when he died; an hundred and thirty years old was he when he died.

α.24.16 Kah upposekinóuh ukkeitotanat David, ut kenugke ketass8tamwéhtu, newutche wunnesu ut Israel, na neeswe en nogque Godut, kah nogque en wekit.
E.24.16 And they buried him in the city of David among the kings, because he had done good in Israel, both toward God, and toward his house.

α.24.17 Kah mahche nupuk Jehojada, Judae sontimóog peyaog, kah wonkumáog ketass8tamwoh, neit ketass8t nah ukkehkitauoh.
E.24.17 Now after the death of Jehoiada came the princes of Judah, and made obeisance to the king. Then the king hearkened unto them.

α.24.18 Kah nag nukkodtumwog wek Jehovah 8sh8oh um-Manitt8m8uh, kah nag wuttinneumuhkontamwog kuppahtuash kah nunneukontunkoh: kah musquanittam8onk nuhkuhkonk Judah, kah Jerusalem, newutche yeu ummatcheseongan8.
E.24.18 And they left the house of the LORD God of their fathers, and served groves and idols: and wrath came upon Judah and Jerusalem for this their trespass.

α.24.19 Qut onch na wuttin ann8non quoshoadumwaénuh, wonk nah uppas8wónaóont Jehovahut: kah wutayeuuhkonittue 8wauwonáuh: qut matta kukkeitamóog.
E.24.19 Yet he sent prophets to them, to bring them again unto the LORD; and they testified against them: but they would not give ear.

α.24.20 Kah wunnashauanitt8moh God, nuhkuhkau Zachariahoh, wunnaumonuh Jehojada sephausuen, noh ánunkompau8mont missinninnúh, kah wuttinuh, yeu wussin God, tohwaj pannesehtamóg wutann8team8ongash Jehovah, newaj matta wunniyeóg? newutche kenukonomw8 Jehovah noh wonk kenukonukou.
E.24.20 And the Spirit of God came upon Zechariah the son of Jehoiada the priest, which stood above the people, and said unto them, Thus saith God, Why transgress ye the commandments of the LORD, that ye cannot prosper? because ye have forsaken the LORD, he hath also forsaken you.

α.24.21 Kah 8nombeukonóuh, kah ukqussukquantahwhouh, an8teamwit ketass8t ut chippinneutonganit wekit Jehovah.
E.24.21 And they conspired against him, and stoned him with stones at the commandment of the king in the court of the house of the LORD.

α.24.22 Yeu in Joash matta mehquontam8 womoausuonk, ne Jehojadahoh 8shoh anhukquneup, qut wunnehtauuh wunnaumonuh: kah nappuk, n8wau, Jehovah mononeaj, kah wutchimmuaj.
E.24.22 Thus Joash the king remembered not the kindness which Jehoiada his father had done to him, but slew his son. And when he died, he said, The LORD look upon it, and require it.

α.24.23 Kah n$niyeup, adt mahtshunkkodtum8 Syriae chippan8onk ukkuhkuhquehtunkoh: kah peyaog Judah, kah Jerusalem, kah nushauog wame wussontimom8uh missinninnúog, wutche kenugke missinninnúut, kah negonshhuau Damaskuse ketass8t wame sequttahham8ongan8oash.
E.24.23 And it came to pass at the end of the year, that the host of Syria came up against him: and they came to Judah and Jerusalem, and destroyed all the princes of the people from among the people, and sent all the spoil of them unto the king of Damascus.

α.24.24 Newutche Syrianse ayeuhteaog, oggushisháog, kah Jehovah mag8 mishe ayeuteuh en wunnutchegan8óut, newutche ahquanumáog Jehovah 8sh8oh um-Manitt8m8uh: neit unneheáog Joashoh wussittumóonk.
E.24.24 For the army of the Syrians came with a small company of men, and the LORD delivered a very great host into their hand, because they had forsaken the LORD God of their fathers. So they executed judgment against Joash.

α.24.25 Kah nogkonáhettit (newutche wunnukonóuh ut mishe mahchinaonganehtu) nehenwonche wuttinneumoh wunnombeukonuk, wutche 8sqheonk wunnaumonuh Jehojada sephausuen, kah wunnushóuh ut wutapinneat, kah nupp8: kah upposekinóuh wutotanat David, qut matta nah upposekinóuh ut ketass8tamwe weenohkit.
E.24.25 And when they were departed from him, (for they left him in great diseases,) his own servants conspired against him for the blood of the sons of Jehoiada the priest, and slew him on his bed, and he died: and they buried him in the city of David, but they buried him not in the sepulchres of the kings.

α.24.26 Kah yeug nag wanambeukonácheg, Zabad wunnaumonuh Shimeath, wut-Amonitesse, kah Jehozabad wunnaumonuh Shimrith um-Moabitesse.
E.24.26 And these are they that conspired against him; Zabad the son of Shimeath an Ammonitess, and Jehozabad the son of Shimrith a Moabitess.

α.24.27 Kah papaume wunnaumonuh, kah mógagish wéanash nish upponamauonáoash; kah onchteóonk wek God, kusséh nash wussukwhosuash, ut wutaunchem8kae b8k8wóut ketass8tamwog: kah Amaziahoh wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tamómukquoh.
E.24.27 Now concerning his sons, and the greatness of the burdens laid upon him, and the repairing of the house of God, behold, they are written in the story of the book of the kings. And Amaziah his son reigned in his stead.

α.25.1 AMaziah nesnehchage kah napanna tahshe kodtomwohkom n8che ketass8tam8it, kah ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem, nesnehchage kah pask8gun kodtumwae, kah ohkassoh ussowesuoh Jehoadan, wutch Jerusalem.
E.25.1 Amaziah was twenty and five years old when he began to reign, and he reigned twenty and nine years in Jerusalem. And his mother's name was Jehoaddan of Jerusalem.

α.25.2 Kah ussu ne sampwag ut anaquabit Jehovah, qut matta nashpe pannuppée metah.
E.25.2 And he did that which was right in the sight of the LORD, but not with a perfect heart.

α.25.3 Kah n$niyeup, wutass8tam8onk manuhkag, nushau wuttinneumoh neg nashompanneg 8shoh ketass8t.
E.25.3 Now it came to pass, when the kingdom was established to him, that he slew his servants that had killed the king his father.

α.25.4 Qut matta nushóou wunneechan8oh neansukwhosik ut naumatue up-b8kumut Moses, uttoh adt Jehovah ann8teamwop, n8wop, wut8shineunk matta pish nupp8og wutche wunneechan8oh, asuh matta pish mukkiog nupp8og wutch 8sh8óuh: qut nish$noh pasuk pish nupp8 wutch nehenwonche ummatcheseonk.
E.25.4 But he slew not their children, but did as it is written in the law in the book of Moses, where the LORD commanded, saying, The fathers shall not die for the children, neither shall the children die for the fathers, but every man shall die for his own sin.

α.25.5 Kah wonk Amaziah miyanau Judahoh, kah wutáyeuoh muttannongane mugquompuh, kah pasuk8e mugquompuh, neaunak 8sh8oh wek8óash pannuppe wame Judah kah Benjamin: kah nah wutogkemuh wutch wunnesnechage kodtumwohkomununeat kah paámeu, kah nah wunnamheuh, nishwudt pasuk8e muttannonganogkussuoh pepenauutcheg, sohhamunat en ayeuwuttinneat, neg nohtónukeg qunuhtug kah ogqunneg.
E.25.5 Moreover Amaziah gathered Judah together, and made them captains over thousands, and captains over hundreds, according to the houses of their fathers, throughout all Judah and Benjamin: and he numbered them from twenty years old and above, and found them three hundred thousand choice men, able to go forth to war, that could handle spear and shield.

α.25.6 Kah wonk onkquttauau nequt pasuk8e muttannonganog kussuoh menuhkesuenúog wutch Israel, wutche nequt pasuk8e silvere talentsash.
E.25.6 He hired also an hundred thousand mighty men of valour out of Israel for an hundred talents of silver.

α.25.7 Qut Manittowompuh peyaonuh, n8wau, woi ketass8t, Israelle kenauwameonk ahque weechógqush: newutche Jehovah matta weetomau Israeloh, wame wunneechanoh Ephraim.
E.25.7 But there came a man of God to him, saying, O king, let not the army of Israel go with thee; for the LORD is not with Israel, to wit, with all the children of Ephraim.

α.25.8 Qut kod weetaan ussish, menuhkesish wutch ayeuwuttineat: God pish kukkepshahuk anaquabhettit matwáog: newutch God ummenuhkesuonganuen wutanóhsineat, kah ukkepuhkausuonat.
E.25.8 But if thou wilt go, do it; be strong for the battle: God shall make thee fall before the enemy: for God hath power to help, and to cast down.

α.25.9 Kah Amaziah unnau Manittowompuh, qut toh pish nuttinteo nequt pasuk8e talentsu8, ne anumauóg Israelle kenauwameonk? kah Manittowomp namp8ham, Jehovah tapenum kutánue yeu tahshe aninnumukqunat.
E.25.9 And Amaziah said to the man of God, But what shall we do for the hundred talents which I have given to the army of Israel? And the man of God answered, The LORD is able to give thee much more than this.

α.25.10 Neit Amaziah nah wutchippinuh, ne kenauwameonk páuhonukqunat wutch Ephraimut, wonk ummonchenaóut: newaj ummusquanittam8ongan8 ayeuuhkonittue mishe nashquneau Judah, kah nag qushqueog nashpe mishe musquanittam8onk.
E.25.10 Then Amaziah separated them, to wit, the army that was come to him out of Ephraim, to go home again: wherefore their anger was greatly kindled against Judah, and they returned home in great anger.

α.25.11 Kah Amaziah menehkheau wuhhogkuh, kah sohwhe sagkompagunau ummissinninneumoh, kah au salte 8nokoiyeuut kah togtannonganogkussuog.
E.25.11 And Amaziah strengthened himself, and led forth his people, and went to the valley of salt, and smote of the children of Seir ten thousand.

α.25.12 Kah piogque muttannonganogkussuoh keteáe tohqunau, kah wunnaumonuh Judah ummissináe monchanóuh, kah uppas8óuh kodtompskôag: kah wunn8kuhkonut wutch woskeche-pisk, newaj wame sokqsinhettit.
E.25.12 And other ten thousand left alive did the children of Judah carry away captive, and brought them unto the top of the rock, and cast them down from the top of the rock, that they all were broken in pieces.

α.25.13 Qut chippan8wongane matwàoh neh Amaziah quoshkeáheoncheh, matta 8weechógk8unat en ayeuwuttinneat, nag quentamwog Judae keitotanash, wutch Samaria wéhque Beth-horon, kah togkomáog nishwudt muttannonganogkussuoh, kah amaunumwog m8cheke sequttahhamóonk.
E.25.13 But the soldiers of the army which Amaziah sent back, that they should not go with him to battle, fell upon the cities of Judah, from Samaria even unto Bethhoron, and smote three thousand of them, and took much spoil.

α.25.14 Kah n$niyeup Amaziah mahche 8k uppaguanonat Edomitsoh pas8au um-manitt8m8uh wunnaumonuh Seir, kah upponuh 8manitt8muneuh, kah nah wunnauwaéhtauoh, kah wutchikossumau wetemungquok.
E.25.14 Now it came to pass, after that Amaziah was come from the slaughter of the Edomites, that he brought the gods of the children of Seir, and set them up to be his gods, and bowed down himself before them, and burned incense unto them.

α.25.15 Newaj ummusquantamóonk Jehovah nashqunaeitunkqut Amaziah: kah noh wuttin ann8non quoshodtumwaenúh, neh ánukqutcheh, toh wutch natinnewhadt ummanitt8m8oh missinninnúog, neg matta pohquohwhunukig ummissinninneumoh wutch kenutcheganit?
E.25.15 Wherefore the anger of the LORD was kindled against Amaziah, and he sent unto him a prophet, which said unto him, Why hast thou sought after the gods of the people, which could not deliver their own people out of thine hand?

α.25.16 Kah n$niyeup, keket8hkauont, wuttinuh, sun ken pasuk ketass8t ukken8nuwaéneumoh? netohshúash, tohwutch woh togkomunumuk, neit quoshodtumwaen, ne wutteashuon, kah n8wau, n8wahteoh God pakodtantam kuttoúskkoméhtóhukqunat, newutche yeu kutussen, kah matta kukkéihketám8h nukken8suaonk.
E.25.16 And it came to pass, as he talked with him, that the king said unto him, Art thou made of the king's counsel? forbear; why shouldest thou be smitten? Then the prophet forbare, and said, I know that God hath determined to destroy thee, because thou hast done this, and hast not hearkened unto my counsel.

α.25.17 Neit Amaziah Judae ketass8t, nemunum ken8nittuonk, kah ann8team8 en Joashut, wunnaumonuh Jehoahaz wunnaumonuh Jehu, Israelle ketass8t, n8wau, peyaush, natitteuh.
E.25.17 Then Amaziah king of Judah took advice, and sent to Joash, the son of Jehoahaz, the son of Jehu, king of Israel, saying, Come, let us see one another in the face.

α.25.18 Kah Joash Israelle ketass8t ann8team8 en Amaziahut Judae ketass8t, n8wau, kôgkôunogkohquohhou, ne ut Lebanon, ann8team8 en Cedarut ne ut Lebanon, n8wau, nunnaumon ummittamwositch kuttaunoh; kah na pomushon touohkomukque puppinushim, ut Lebanon, kah taskuhkauau, kôgkôunogkohquohhouoh.
E.25.18 And Joash king of Israel sent to Amaziah king of Judah, saying, The thistle that was in Lebanon sent to the cedar that was in Lebanon, saying, Give thy daughter to my son to wife: and there passed by a wild beast that was in Lebanon, and trode down the thistle.

α.25.19 Kussim, kusseh, nuttogkom Edomitsog, kah kuttah kutashinuk woweenoónat: yeuyeu apsh kekit, tohwutch woh weogkekeadt, wutch k8woskhitteáonk, woh kuppenushonat, ken kah Judah weeche ken?
E.25.19 Thou sayest, Lo, thou hast smitten the Edomites; and thine heart lifteth thee up to boast: abide now at home; why shouldest thou meddle to thine hurt, that thou shouldest fall, even thou, and Judah with thee?

α.25.20 Qut Amaziah matta n8tam8, newutche 8m88 Godut, nah woh uppononat ut wunnutcheganit, newutche natinneahwhaog Edome manitt8h.
E.25.20 But Amaziah would not hear; for it came of God, that he might deliver them into the hand of their enemies, because they sought after the gods of Edom.

α.25.21 Neit Joash Israelle ketass8t kuhkuhqueu, kah naettúog ut wuskesuk8óut, nagum kah Amaziah Judae ketass8t, en Bethshemesh ne wadchiik Judah.
E.25.21 So Joash the king of Israel went up; and they saw one another in the face, both he and Amaziah king of Judah, at Bethshemesh, which belongeth to Judah.

α.25.22 Kah Judah togkomau ut anaquabit Israel, kah uspuhh8waog nish$noh pasuk en wekit.
E.25.22 And Judah was put to the worse before Israel, and they fled every man to his tent.

α.25.23 Kah Joash Israelle ketass8t, tohqunau Amaziahoh Judae ketass8t, wunnaumonuh Joash, wunnaumonuh Joahaz, ut Bethshemesh, kah uppas8oh Jerusalem, kah touwutchathamwog Jerusaleme pum̃eneutunk, wutch Ephraime squontamut, en p8chekehégane squontamut, yaue pasuk8e ishquonogkodtash.
E.25.23 And Joash the king of Israel took Amaziah king of Judah, the son of Joash, the son of Jehoahaz, at Bethshemesh, and brought him to Jerusalem, and brake down the wall of Jerusalem from the gate of Ephraim to the corner gate, four hundred cubits.

α.25.24 Kah wame gold kah silver, kah wame wishquash, nish nampteomukish ut wekit God, wadchanukish Obed-Edom; kah nompak8unash ketass8t wekit, kah kônohtohsimukeg wonk, kah qushkeu en Samaria
E.25.24 And he took all the gold and the silver, and all the vessels that were found in the house of God with Obededom, and the treasures of the king's house, the hostages also, and returned to Samaria.

α.25.25 Kah Amaziah wunnaumonuh Joash Judae ketass8t, noh asukoue pomontam, mahche nupuk Joash, wunnaumonuh Jehoahaz Israelle ketass8t, nabo napanna tahshe kodtumwae.
E.25.25 And Amaziah the son of Joash king of Judah lived after the death of Joash son of Jehoahaz king of Israel fifteen years.

α.25.26 Kah onkatogish wutusseongash Amaziah negonne kah maumachish, sunnummatta wussukwhosinash ut up-b8kum8óut Israelle, kah Judae ketass8tamwog.
E.25.26 Now the rest of the acts of Amaziah, first and last, behold, are they not written in the book of the kings of Judah and Israel?

α.25.27 Kah mahche Amaziah qushkeit wutch asuhkauónat Lord, 8nambeukonóuh ut Jerusalem, kah uspuhh8au Lachish; qut ann8team8og Lachish asuhkaue, kah na wuttit nushoneau.
E.25.27 Now after the time that Amaziah did turn away from following the LORD they made a conspiracy against him in Jerusalem; and he fled to Lachish: but they sent to Lachish after him, and slew him there.

α.25.28 Kah uppas8ó ut woskeche horsesut, kah upposekinóuh kenugke 8shut ut Judae keitotanat.
E.25.28 And they brought him upon horses, and buried him with his fathers in the city of Judah.

α.26.1 NEit wame Judae missinninnuog neemunaog Uzziahoh, noh nabo nequtta adtahshe kodtumwohkog, kah wunnompe kehtass8tamuhkonauh 8shoh Amaziah.
E.26.1 Then all the people of Judah took Uzziah, who was sixteen years old, and made him king in the room of his father Amaziah.

α.26.2 Ayim Eloth, kah wunnompenumun en Judah, mahche ketass8t weesequom8mont 8shoh.
E.26.2 He built Eloth, and restored it to Judah, after that the king slept with his fathers.

α.26.3 Nabo nequtta tahshe kodtumwohkom Uzziah n8che ketass8tam8it, kah ketass8tam88 napan[n]a tahshinchage kodtumwae kah nees, ut Jerusalem: wonk ohkasoh uss8wesuoh Jecoliah wutch Jerusalem.
E.26.3 Sixteen years old was Uzziah when he began to reign, and he reigned fifty and two years in Jerusalem. His mother's name also was Jecoliah of Jerusalem.

α.26.4 Kah usseu ne an sampwag ut anaquabit Jehovah, wame ne 8shoh Amaziahoh aseneup.
E.26.4 And he did that which was right in the sight of the LORD, according to all that his father Amaziah did.

α.26.5 Kah natinnewhau Godoh pomontog Zechariah, noh wohwohtam8wontog Manitt8e monomonsinn8wongash, kah nisahke natinnewhout Jehovah, God 8niehheuh.
E.26.5 And he sought God in the days of Zechariah, who had understanding in the visions of God: and as long as he sought the LORD, God made him to prosper.

α.26.6 Kah sohham, ayeuuhkonau Philistiansoh, kah touwutchahtham Gathe pummeneutunk, kah Jabneheh pummeneutunk, kah Ashdode pummeneutuk, kah ayim keitototanash, kishke Ashdod, kah kenugké Philistiansut.
E.26.6 And he went forth and warred against the Philistines, and brake down the wall of Gath, and the wall of Jabneh, and the wall of Ashdod, and built cities about Ashdod, and among the Philistines.

α.26.7 Kah God wutannumauoh ayeuuhkonittue Philistiansoh, kah ayeuuhkonittue Arabiansoh, neg ayitcheg ut Gur-Baal, kah Mehunimsog.
E.26.7 And God helped him against the Philistines, and against the Arabians that dwelt in Gurbaal, and the Mehunims.

α.26.8 Kah Ammonitsog aninnumauog mag8ongash, Uzziahoh, kah 8wesuonk sepakem8 wehque ahhut petutteamuk Egypt, newutche mishe menehkheau wuhhogkuh.
E.26.8 And the Ammonites gave gifts to Uzziah: and his name spread abroad even to the entering in of Egypt; for he strengthened himself exceedingly.

α.26.9 Kah wonk Uzziah ayim wonkon8sinash ut Jersualem, ut p8chekuhhegane squontamut, kah ut 8nouhkoiyeue squontamut, kah adt quttukqushunk, kah ummenuhkehteauunash.
E.26.9 Moreover Uzziah built towers in Jerusalem at the corner gate, and at the valley gate, and at the turning of the wall, and fortified them.

α.26.10 Wonk ayim wonkan8sinash ut touohkomuk, kah m8cheke wutahamunganehteau newutche m8naoh wunneetasseumoh, naneeswe 8nouhkoiyeue ohkeit, kah mukoshqutuhtu, kah ohkehteaenuog, kah weenominneohketeaenuog, ut wadchuuhkontu, kah ut Carmél, newutche womontam ohkehteaenuin.
E.26.10 Also he built towers in the desert, and digged many wells: for he had much cattle, both in the low country, and in the plains: husbandmen also, and vine dressers in the mountains, and in Carmel: for he loved husbandry.

α.26.11 Wonk Uzziah wutayeuwehteaenumu, neg chadchabpanuongane sohhogig ayeuuhkonat, nean ogkemut, nashpe wuñutcheganit Jehiel wus$scribe: kah Maasiah nanánuénin, ut agwe wunnutcheganit Hananiah, noh pasuk8 ketass8t ummummugquompomuh.
E.26.11 Moreover Uzziah had an host of fighting men, that went out to war by bands, according to the number of their account by the hand of Jeiel the scribe and Maaseiah the ruler, under the hand of Hananiah, one of the king's captains.

α.26.12 Mamusse nean ogkemut, kehche wut8shinneunk ut menuhkesuenuut, neese muttannunganog kussuog, kah nequtta tahshe pasuk88og.
E.26.12 The whole number of the chief of the fathers of the mighty men of valour were two thousand and six hundred.

α.26.13 Kah agwe wunnutchegan8out, kenauwameonganu8, nishwudt pasuk8e muttannonganog kussuog, kah nesausuk tahshe muttannonganogkussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasuk88og, yeu menuhkayeuhteaog, weech8humonat ketass8t ayeuuhkonittue matwáoh.
E.26.13 And under their hand was an army, three hundred thousand and seven thousand and five hundred, that made war with mighty power, to help the king against the enemy.

α.26.14 Kah Uzziah nah ukquagquoshwuñumauoh pannuppe wame kenauwameonganehtu ogqunegash, kah qunuhtukquash, kah uppuhkukqut ahhohtagish, kah habergeonsash kah ohtampeh, kah s8wompagenehegash.
E.26.14 And Uzziah prepared for them throughout all the host shields, and spears, and helmets, and habergeons, and bows, and slings to cast stones.

α.26.15 Kah ayim ut Jerusalem, awohteaongash nish ayimohetticheh wunnummoeu usseaenuog, ohtaut wonkon8sinit, kah ut pummeneutonganehtu , kôuhquodtash puminneat, kah mogge qussukquanash: kah 8wesuonk nôadtut in sepakem8, newutche noh monchanatamwe aninnumauau, nô pajeh menuhkesinneat.
E.26.15 And he made in Jerusalem engines, invented by cunning men, to be on the towers and upon the bulwarks, to shoot arrows and great stones withal. And his name spread far abroad; for he was marvellously helped, till he was strong.

α.26.16 Manuhkesit, wuttah tahshem8 en wutonkapunnaonganit: newutche panneussehtauau Jehovah um-Manitt8moh, kah petutteau wuttemplumut Jehovah, chikossumunat weetemungquok, ut weetemungquokque Altarut.
E.26.16 But when he was strong, his heart was lifted up to his destruction: for he transgressed against the LORD his God, and went into the temple of the LORD to burn incense upon the altar of incense.

α.26.17 Kah Azariah sephausuen wutasukaue petutteam8, kah weechog shwosuk tahshinchag kussuoh wussephausueneumoh Jehovah, neg menuhkesuenuog.
E.26.17 And Azariah the priest went in after him, and with him fourscore priests of the LORD, that were valiant men:

α.26.18 Kah nag wutamehheaag Uzziahhoh ketass8toh, kah wuttinouh, matta wutchiin8h kuhhogkat, Uzziah, chikohsumauonat weetemungquok Jehovah, qut sephausuenuut wunnaumonuh Aaron, neg waneetupanatamwahitcheg wutchikohsumunnaoont weetemungquok, sohhash wutch Sanctuary newutche kuppanneussem, kah matta pish ne k8quehtianumukqussein, wutch Jehovah Manitt8ut.
E.26.18 And they withstood Uzziah the king, and said unto him, It appertaineth not unto thee, Uzziah, to burn incense unto the LORD, but to the priests the sons of Aaron, that are consecrated to burn incense: go out of the sanctuary; for thou hast trespassed; neither shall it be for thine honour from the LORD God.

α.26.19 Neit Uzziah musquantam, kah censer ohteau wunnutcheganit chikohsumunat weetemungquok: kah musquanumont sephausuenuh, wutchek8onk waapem8 ut wuskodtukqut ut anaquabhettit sephausuenuog, ut wekit Lord wutch kishke wetemungquoke Altarut.
E.26.19 Then Uzziah was wroth, and had a censer in his hand to burn incense: and while he was wroth with the priests, the leprosy even rose up in his forehead before the priests in the house of the LORD, from beside the incense altar.

α.26.20 Kah Azariah kehche sephausuen, kah wame sephausuenuog, ukkehkeneauouh, kah kusseh, wutchek8 ut wuskodtukqut, kah na wutch sohwohkoneau, nux, nagum wonk kenuppe sohham, newutche Jehovah wuttogkomau.
E.26.20 And Azariah the chief priest, and all the priests, looked upon him, and, behold, he was leprous in his forehead, and they thrust him out from thence; yea, himself hasted also to go out, because the LORD had smitten him.

α.26.21 Kah Uzzia ketass8t wutchek8 pajeh wunnupunat, kah chippitteau newutche wutchek8 newutche tummetahwhau wutch wekit Jehovah, kah Jothan wunnaumonuh nanawunnum ketass8t wek, wussumau missinninnuh ut ohkeit.
E.26.21 And Uzziah the king was a leper unto the day of his death, and dwelt in a several house, being a leper; for he was cut off from the house of the LORD: and Jotham his son was over the king's house, judging the people of the land.

α.26.22 Kah onkatogish wutusseongash Uzziah negonne kah maumachish, Isayah qushodtumwaen wunnaumonuh Amoz, 8sukuhkumunash.
E.26.22 Now the rest of the acts of Uzziah, first and last, did Isaiah the prophet, the son of Amoz, write.

α.26.23 Neit Uzziah weesequom8mau 8shoh, kah upposekinouh weeche 8shoh, kah upposekinnittue ahkeyeuout ketass8tamwoh: newutche nag n8waog, noh wutchek8: kah Jothamoh wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tamomukquoh.
E.26.23 So Uzziah slept with his fathers, and they buried him with his fathers in the field of the burial which belonged to the kings; for they said, He is a leper: and Jotham his son reigned in his stead.

α.27.1 IOtham nesnehchage kah napanna tahshe kodtumwohkom n8che ketass8tam8it, kah nabo nequtta tahshe kodtumwae ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem, wonk ohkasoh ussowesuoh Jerushah wuttaunoh Zadok.
E.27.1 Jotham was twenty and five years old when he began to reign, and he reigned sixteen years in Jerusalem. His mother's name also was Jerushah, the daughter of Zadok.

α.27.2 Kah ussu ne sampwagk ut anaquabit Jehovah, neaunak wame ne aseneup Uzziahoh 8shoh: qut matta petutteou wut-templeumut Jehovah. Kah missinninnúog ashpume aninnue usseog.
E.27.2 And he did that which was right in the sight of the LORD, according to all that his father Uzziah did: howbeit he entered not into the temple of the LORD. And the people did yet corruptly.

α.27.3 Ayim qunuhque ushquont wekit Jehovah, kah ut Ophelle pummeneutunkanit, m8cheke ayim.
E.27.3 He built the high gate of the house of the LORD, and on the wall of Ophel he built much.

α.27.4 Wonk ayim keitotanash ut Judae wádchuuhkontu, kah ut touohkomukqut ayim wonkon8sinush kah qunúhquikomukquash.
E.27.4 Moreover he built cities in the mountains of Judah, and in the forests he built castles and towers.

α.27.5 Wonk ayeuuhkonau Ammonitse keitass8tamwoh, kah wussohkauuh, kah wunnaumonuh Ammon nenan kodtumuk nequt pasuk88ash silvere talentsash, kah piogque muttannongane quttuhwhosuash wheatash, kah piogque muttannongane, barlyhash, ne wutteashe ôadtuhkauoneau wunnaumonuh Ammon nahohtôeu kodtum8, kah nashwunnu8.
E.27.5 He fought also with the king of the Ammonites, and prevailed against them. And the children of Ammon gave him the same year an hundred talents of silver, and ten thousand measures of wheat, and ten thousand of barley. So much did the children of Ammon pay unto him, both the second year, and the third.

α.27.6 Nemehkuh Jotham nano missugken, newutche quogquashwehtam ummayash ut anaquabit Jehovah um-Manitt8moh.
E.27.6 So Jotham became mighty, because he prepared his ways before the LORD his God.

α.27.7 Kah onkatogish wutusseongash Jotham kah wame wutáyeuwehteaongash, kah ummayash, kusseh, wussukwhosuash ut 8sukuhwhosuongan8óut Israelle, kah Judae ketass8tamwog.
E.27.7 Now the rest of the acts of Jotham, and all his wars, and his ways, lo, they are written in the book of the kings of Israel and Judah.

α.27.8 Nog nesnehchage kah napanna tahshe kodtumwohkom n8che ketass8tam8it, kah nabo nequtta tahshe kodtumwae ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem.
E.27.8 He was five and twenty years old when he began to reign, and reigned sixteen years in Jerusalem.

α.27.9 Kah Jotham weesequom8mau 8shoh, kah upposekinóuh ut ukkeitotanat David, kah Ahaz wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tamomukquoh.
E.27.9 And Jotham slept with his fathers, and they buried him in the city of David: and Ahaz his son reigned in his stead.

α.28.1 AHaz nesnehchage kodtumwohkom n8che ketass8tam8it, kah nabo nequtta tahshe kodtumwae ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem: qut matta ussu ne sampwagk ut anaquabit Jehovah, onatuh David 8shoh.
E.28.1 Ahaz was twenty years old when he began to reign, and he reigned sixteen years in Jerusalem: but he did not that which was right in the sight of the LORD, like David his father:

α.28.2 Newutche pomushau ut ummayut Israelle ketass8tamwog, wonk ayimauau sabasumwe nunneukontungoh Baalimoh.
E.28.2 For he walked in the ways of the kings of Israel, and made also molten images for Baalim.

α.28.3 Wonk, chikohsum wetemungquok ut wut8nôuhkóiyeumut wunnaumonuh Hinnom, kah chikoswau wunneechanoh ut n8taut: neaunak wunnishkeneunkquott8m8 pen8wohteáog, neh Jehovah sohwohteompuh ut anaquabhettit wunnaumonuh Israel.
E.28.3 Moreover he burnt incense in the valley of the son of Hinnom, and burnt his children in the fire, after the abominations of the heathen whom the LORD had cast out before the children of Israel.

α.28.4 Wonk sephausu, kah chikohsue weetemungquok ut qunuhqui ayeuonganehtu, kah wadchuuhkontu, kah ut agwe nish$noh ashkunkquamut.
E.28.4 He sacrificed also and burnt incense in the high places, and on the hills, and under every green tree.

α.28.5 Newaj Jehovah um-Manitt8moh upponuh ut wunnutcheganit Syriae ketass8t, kah nah wuttogkomóuh, kah monchanáog monaoh missinoh, kah uppas8ouh Damaskus, kah wonk magunáh ut wunnutcheganit Israelle ketass8t, noh wuttogkomuh nashpe mishe paguanittuonk.
E.28.5 Wherefore the LORD his God delivered him into the hand of the king of Syria; and they smote him, and carried away a great multitude of them captives, and brought them to Damascus. And he was also delivered into the hand of the king of Israel, who smote him with a great slaughter.

α.28.6 Newutche Pekah wunnaumonuh Remaliah nushehteau ut Judah nequt pasuk8e muttannonganogkussuog, kah nesnehchage muttannonganogkussuog, pasuk kesuk, neg wame menuhkesuénuog, newutche ohquánumóag Jehovah 8sh8oh um-Manitt8m8oh.
E.28.6 For Pekah the son of Remaliah slew in Judah an hundred and twenty thousand in one day, which were all valiant men; because they had forsaken the LORD God of their fathers.

α.28.7 Kah Zichri Ephraimme menuhkesuen, nushau Maasejahoh wunnaumonuh ketass8t, kah Azrikam nánawunnúen ut wetuómut, kah Elkanah noh asukauont ketass8t.
E.28.7 And Zichri, a mighty man of Ephraim, slew Maaseiah the king's son, and Azrikam the governor of the house, and Elkanah that was next to the king.

α.28.8 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel missinwohteáog weemat8oh neese pasuk8e muttannonganogkussuoh, mittamwussissoh, wunnaumoniinneuh, kah wuttôninneuh, kah wonk wutamaunumauoh m8cheke sequttahham8ongash, kah paudtóog sequttahham8ongash en Samariah.
E.28.8 And the children of Israel carried away captive of their brethren two hundred thousand, women, sons, and daughters, and took also away much spoil from them, and brought the spoil to Samaria.

α.28.9 Qut ukquoshodtumwaenumoh Jehovah na wutappinah, noh ussowesu Oded: kah sohham en anaquabenit kenauwameonguh, neg paoncheg Samaria, kah nah wuttinuh, kusseh, newutche Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh k8sh8óog musquanumau Judahoh, nah upponuh kenutchegan8óut, kah nag kenushôóog, nashpe musquantam8onk ne masiṣshik kesukqut.
E.28.9 But a prophet of the LORD was there, whose name was Oded: and he went out before the host that came to Samaria, and said unto them, Behold, because the LORD God of your fathers was wroth with Judah, he hath delivered them into your hand, and ye have slain them in a rage that reacheth up unto heaven.

α.28.10 Kah yeuyeu kuppogkodtantumumw8 agwe pononaóont Judah kah Jerusalem wunnaumonuh, wutche k8missinnominneaóont: sunnummatta kenugke kenaau, nux kenaau, matche neheoncheg Jehovahoh kum-Manitt8m8uh?
E.28.10 And now ye purpose to keep under the children of Judah and Jerusalem for bondmen and bondwomen unto you: but are there not with you, even with you, sins against the LORD your God?

α.28.11 Newutche yeuyeu n8tiegk, kah wonk moncheáheuk missináog, neg masinóhteágig wutch kematt8óut, newutche ummishe musquanittam8onk God ketapehtunkumw8.
E.28.11 Now hear me therefore, and deliver the captives again, which ye have taken captive of your brethren: for the fierce wrath of the LORD is upon you.

α.28.12 Neit nawhutch wabuhkuhk8itcheg wutch wunnaumonat Ephraim, Azariah wunnaumonuh Johanan, Berechiah wunnaumonuh Meshillemoth, kah Jehizkiah wunnaumonuh Shallum, kah Amasa wunnaumonuh Hadlai; wutayeuuhkonittue neepauwehtauóuh, neg wagig ayeuwuttinneat.
E.28.12 Then certain of the heads of the children of Ephraim, Azariah the son of Johanan, Berechiah the son of Meshillemoth, and Jehizkiah the son of Shallum, and Amasa the son of Hadlai, stood up against them that came from the war,

α.28.13 Kah nag wuttinuh, matta pish yeu kuppas8óuneau missinóog, newutche mahche matcheneheogkut Jehovah, kukkod k8tnehteomw8 nummatcheseonganunonash, kah nuppaneseonganunonash, newutche nummatcheseonk missi, kah mishe musquanittam8onk ayeuuhkonau Israeloh.
E.28.13 And said unto them, Ye shall not bring in the captives hither: for whereas we have offended against the LORD already, ye intend to add more to our sins and to our trespass: for our trespass is great, and there is fierce wrath against Israel.

α.28.14 Kah kenauwameog nukkonáog missinuh, kah sequttahham8onk anaquabhettit sontimóog, kah wame mukkinneonk.
E.28.14 So the armed men left the captives and the spoil before the princes and all the congregation.

α.28.15 Kah wosketompaog neg másawhutcheg, neep8og, kah neemunáog missinuh, kah nashpe sequttahham8onk, wuthogquonóneau, wame poskissinitcheh ut kenugke nag, kah wuthogquanóuh, kah 8mokussinuhkauóuh, kah wuttinnumauóuh metsuonk kah wuttattam8on, kah wussusséqunóuh, kah wame n8chumwesinutcheh ukquenashóuh assesut, kah uppas8óuh Jericho; palmuhtugque keitotan, en weematt8óuh; kah nag qushkeog en Samaria.
E.28.15 And the men which were expressed by name rose up, and took the captives, and with the spoil clothed all that were naked among them, and arrayed them, and shod them, and gave them to eat and to drink, and anointed them, and carried all the feeble of them upon asses, and brought them to Jericho, the city of palm trees, to their brethren: then they returned to Samaria.

α.28.16 Na ahquompak Ahaz ketass8t, ann8team8 en Assyriae ketass8tamut wuttannumauunat.
E.28.16 At that time did king Ahaz send unto the kings of Assyria to help him.

α.28.17 Newutche wonk Edomitsog peyaog, kah togkodtamwog Judah, & missinóhteáog.
E.28.17 For again the Edomites had come and smitten Judah, and carried away captives.

α.28.18 Wonk Philistiansog sohkomwog w8muhkôáge keitotanash, kah sowaniyeuut Judah, kah sohkomwog Bethshemesh, kah Ajalon, Gederoth, kah Shocho, nashpe nish 8tanamesash, wonk Timnah nashpe nish 8tanamesash Gimzo nashpe nish 8tanamesash; kah na wuttaiinneau.
E.28.18 The Philistines also had invaded the cities of the low country, and of the south of Judah, and had taken Bethshemesh, and Ajalon, and Gederoth, and Shocho with the villages thereof, and Timnah with the villages thereof, Gimzo also and the villages thereof: and they dwelt there.

α.28.19 Newutche Jehovah tiahquonkheau Judahoh, newutche Ahaz Israelle ketass8t: newutche Judahoh poskisseheau, kah mishe matcheneheau Jehovahoh.
E.28.19 For the LORD brought Judah low because of Ahaz king of Israel; for he made Judah naked, and transgressed sore against the LORD.

α.28.20 Kah Tilgath-Pilneser Assyriae ketass8t uppeyaonuh, wutunkquanumwéheuh, qut matta ummenuhkeheuh.
E.28.20 And Tilgathpilneser king of Assyria came unto him, and distressed him, but strengthened him not.

α.28.21 Newutche Ahaz amaunum wutchippiyeumun wutch wekit Jehovah, kah wutch wekit ketass8t, kah wutch sontimóog, kah wuttinnumauóneau Assyriae ketass8toh, qut matta wuttannumauuh.
E.28.21 For Ahaz took away a portion out of the house of the LORD, and out of the house of the king, and of the princes, and gave it unto the king of Assyria: but he helped him not.

α.28.22 Kah ut wutonkapunnaonganit, wonk m8cheke panneussehtauau Jehovahoh: noh yeuoh ketass8t Ahaz.
E.28.22 And in the time of his distress did he trespass yet more against the LORD: this is that king Ahaz.

α.28.23 Newutche sephamauau Damaskusse manitt8h noh togkomont: kah n8wau, newutche Assyriae ketass8tamwog, ummanitt8m8oh nah wutannumunk8uh, newaj nag sephamauog, onk woh nag nuttannumunkquog: qut nah wutch paguanónuh, kah wame Israel.
E.28.23 For he sacrificed unto the gods of Damascus, which smote him: and he said, Because the gods of the kings of Syria help them, therefore will I sacrifice to them, that they may help me. But they were the ruin of him, and of all Israel.

α.28.24 Kah Ahaz mukkinnum auwohteaongash ut wekit God, kah wussukqussamunáoash auwohteaongash wekit God, kah yanittanum 8squontamash wekit Jehovah, kah wutaltaruhkauoh nish$noh ut p8chekeheganit ut Jerusalem.
E.28.24 And Ahaz gathered together the vessels of the house of God, and cut in pieces the vessels of the house of God, and shut up the doors of the house of the LORD, and he made him altars in every corner of Jerusalem.

α.28.25 Kah nishnoh ut Judae keitotanat áyim qunuhqui ayeuongash, chikossumau[ô]nat wetemungquok onkatogig manitt8oh, kah m8m8skqheau Jehovahoh um-Manitt8m8oh 8sh8oh.
E.28.25 And in every several city of Judah he made high places to burn incense unto other gods, and provoked to anger the LORD God of his fathers.

α.28.26 Kah onkatogish wutusseongash, kah wame ummayash nequt kah machish, kusseh, wussukwhosuash ut 8sukuhwhonganit Judae kah Israelle ketass8tamwog.
E.28.26 Now the rest of his acts and of all his ways, first and last, behold, they are written in the book of the kings of Judah and Israel.

α.28.27 Kah Ahaz weesequom8mau 8shoh, kah upposekinóuh otanat ut Jerusalem: qut matta uppas8óuh ut 8weenohkeyeuóut Israelle ketass8tamwog, kah Hezekiahoh wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tamomukquoh.
E.28.27 And Ahaz slept with his fathers, and they buried him in the city, even in Jerusalem: but they brought him not into the sepulchres of the kings of Israel: and Hezekiah his son reigned in his stead.

α.29.1 Hezechiah n8che ketass8tam8it nesnehchage kah napanna adtahshe kodtumwohkog, kah nesnehchage kah pask8gun tahshe kodtum8ash ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem kah ohkasoh ussowesuoh Abijah wuttaunoh Zechariah
E.29.1 Hezekiah began to reign when he was five and twenty years old, and he reigned nine and twenty years in Jerusalem. And his mother's name was Abijah, the daughter of Zechariah.

α.29.2 Kah ussu ne sampwag ut anaquabit Jehovah, neaunak wame ne David asit.
E.29.2 And he did that which was right in the sight of the LORD, according to all that David his father had done.

α.29.3 Nagum, negonohtàg ukketass8tamwe kodtum8, negonne nepauz, woshwunum wutushquontamash ut wekit Jehovah, kah wutonchteauunash.
E.29.3 He in the first year of his reign, in the first month, opened the doors of the house of the LORD, and repaired them.

α.29.4 Kah petukonau sephausuenuh kah Levitsoh, kah nah ummiyanuh, en wutchepwoae toumaogquehtu.
E.29.4 And he brought in the priests and the Levites, and gathered them together into the east street,

α.29.5 Kah nah wuttinuh n8tiegk kenaau Levitsog, yeuyeu wunneetupanatamwahuk, kuhhogkaóog, káh wunnetupanatamwáhteo8k wek Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh k8sh8óog kah sohh8wuttau8k nishkeneunkquok wutch wunneetupanatamwe ayeuonganit.
E.29.5 And said unto them, Hear me, ye Levites, sanctify now yourselves, and sanctify the house of the LORD God of your fathers, and carry forth the filthiness out of the holy place.

α.29.6 Newutche n8shunonog panneseupanneg kah usseog ne machuk ut wuskesukqut Jehovah, num-Manitt8mun, kah wutohquanumouh, kah qunnuppenumwog wuskesuk8ash wutch wutayeuonganit Jehovah, kah quinnuppenumwog uppusquanoash.
E.29.6 For our fathers have trespassed, and done that which was evil in the eyes of the LORD our God, and have forsaken him, and have turned away their faces from the habitation of the LORD, and turned their backs.

α.29.7 Wonk kuppuhhamwog Porche squontamash, kah onthamwog lampsash, kah matta chikohsumóog wetemungquok, & matta mag8og chikohtae mag8ongash ut wunneetupanatamwe ayeuonganit en ummanitt8m8out Israel.
E.29.7 Also they have shut up the doors of the porch, and put out the lamps, and have not burned incense nor offered burnt offerings in the holy place unto the God of Israel.

α.29.8 Newaj ummusquanittam8onk Jehovah nuhkuhkok Judah, kah Jerusalem, kah nah upponuh wuttamehpunaonganit, chepshaonganit, kah mishananumonat, neane naumog ut kuksesuk8out.
E.29.8 Wherefore the wrath of the LORD was upon Judah and Jerusalem, and he hath delivered them to trouble, to astonishment, and to hissing, as ye see with your eyes.

α.29.9 Newutche kusseh n8shunonog pénushaog nashpe togkodteg kah nunnaumonónog, kah nuttaununonog, kah nummittamwussinnonog, neg yeu 8tch missinnainneau.
E.29.9 For, lo, our fathers have fallen by the sword, and our sons and our daughters and our wives are in captivity for this.

α.29.10 Yeuyeu ohteau ut nuttahut n8n8wonanonut um-Manitt8moh Israel, onk woh ummishe musquanittam8onk nukqushkinnumunkqunan.
E.29.10 Now it is in mine heart to make a covenant with the LORD God of Israel, that his fierce wrath may turn away from us.

α.29.11 Nunnaumonunk, yeuyeu ahque mehshane ussek: newutche Jehovah kuppepenunkou neepauinneat ut anaquabit, wuttinneumuhkauonat, kah woh k8wowussumonaóont kah chikohsumunat weetemungquok.
E.29.11 My sons, be not now negligent: for the LORD hath chosen you to stand before him, to serve him, and that ye should minister unto him, and burn incense.

α.29.12 Neit Levitsog neepóog, Mahath wunnaumonuh Amasai, kah Joel wunnaumonuh Azariah wutch wunnaumonat Kohathitsog, kah wutch wunnaumonat Merari, Kish wunnaumonuh Abdi, kah Azariah wunnaumonuh Jahalelel: kah wutch Gershonitsog, Joah wunnaumonuh Zimmah, kah Eden wunnaumonuh Joah.
E.29.12 Then the Levites arose, Mahath the son of Amasai, and Joel the son of Azariah, of the sons of the Kohathites: and of the sons of Merari, Kish the son of Abdi, and Azariah the son of Jehalelel: and of the Gershonites; Joah the son of Zimmah, and Eden the son of Joah:

α.29.13 Kah wutch wunnaumonuh Elizaphan, Shimri, kah Jehiel: kah wutch wunnaumonuh Asaph, Zechariah, kah Mattaniah.
E.29.13 And of the sons of Elizaphan; Shimri, and Jeiel: and of the sons of Asaph; Zechariah, and Mattaniah:

α.29.14 Kah wutch wunnaumonuh Heman, Jehiel, kah Shimei: kah wutch wunnaumonuh Jeduthiun, Shemajah, kah Uzziel.
E.29.14 And of the sons of Heman; Jehiel, and Shimei: and of the sons of Jeduthun; Shemaiah, and Uzziel.

α.29.15 Kah miyanáog wematt8oh kah wunnetupanatamwaheàog wuhhogkáuh, kah peyaog neaunak wuttinn8waonk ketass8t, nashpe wuttinn8waongash Jehovah, pahketeauunat wek Jehovah.
E.29.15 And they gathered their brethren, and sanctified themselves, and came, according to the commandment of the king, by the words of the LORD, to cleanse the house of the LORD.

α.29.16 Kah sephausuen petutteau en anómiye ut wekit Jehovah, pahketeauunat, kah soh8wuttóog wame nishkeneunkquok, ne nampteaumuk ut wut-templeumut Jehovah, en chippinneutunkanit wekit Jehovah, kah Levitsog wunnemunnumuneau sohh8wuttauunat, en poquadchit, en Kidrone sepuissut
E.29.16 And the priests went into the inner part of the house of the LORD, to cleanse it, and brought out all the uncleanness that they found in the temple of the LORD into the court of the house of the LORD. And the Levites took it, to carry it out abroad into the brook Kidron.

α.29.17 Kah n8che wunnetupanatamwahuwaog, ut negonne kesukok, ut negonne nepauzsaut, kah ut shwosuk tahshikquinogkodtut, peyaog porchumut Jehovah, neit wunnetupanatamwahteauog wek Jehovah, en shwosuk tahshikquinogkodtut, kah nabo nequtta adtahshikquinahog negonne nepauz uppogkodche usseneau.
E.29.17 Now they began on the first day of the first month to sanctify, and on the eighth day of the month came they to the porch of the LORD: so they sanctified the house of the LORD in eight days; and in the sixteenth day of the first month they made an end.

α.29.18 Néit petutteáog en Hezekiah$ut ketass8tamut, kah nag n8waog, nuppahketeomun wame wek Jehovah, kah chikohtae mag8ongane altar, kah nish wame auwohteaongash, kah nahtitteae petukqunnongane table, kah nish wame auwohteaongash.
E.29.18 Then they went in to Hezekiah the king, and said, We have cleansed all the house of the LORD, and the altar of burnt offering, with all the vessels thereof, and the shewbread table, with all the vessels thereof.

α.29.19 Wonk wame auwohteaongash, nish ketass8t Ahaz kohtass8tam8it, pagkeetogupash, panneusseit, nummahche quagquashwehtamumun, kah n8neetupanatamwahteauunan, kah kusseh, nish ut anaquohtag wut-altarum Jehovah.
E.29.19 Moreover all the vessels, which king Ahaz in his reign did cast away in his transgression, have we prepared and sanctified, and, behold, they are before the altar of the LORD.

α.29.20 Neit Hezekiah ketass8t nompoáe neepau, kah miyanau keitotanáe nanawunnuénuog, kah kuhkuhqueu en wekit Jehovah.
E.29.20 Then Hezekiah the king rose early, and gathered the rulers of the city, and went up to the house of the LORD.

α.29.21 Kah nag pas8waog nesausuk tahsuog oxenog, kah nesausuk tahsuog ramsog, kah nesausuk tahsuog lambsog, kah nesausuk tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog, wutche matcheseongane mag8onk, wutche ass8tam8onk: kah wutche Sanctuary, kah wutche Judah; kah ann8nau sephausuénuh, wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausineat ut wut-altarumut Jehovah.
E.29.21 And they brought seven bullocks, and seven rams, and seven lambs, and seven he goats, for a sin offering for the kingdom, and for the sanctuary, and for Judah. And he commanded the priests the sons of Aaron to offer them on the altar of the LORD.

α.29.22 Neit nushaog oxenoh, kah sephausuenuog attumunumwog wusqueheonk, kah seauhkonau ut Altarut: wonk nasháhettit ramsoh, nag seáhhamwog wusqueheonk ut Altarut: wonk nushaog lambsoh, kah seahhamwog wusqueheonk ut Altarut.
E.29.22 So they killed the bullocks, and the priests received the blood, and sprinkled it on the altar: likewise, when they had killed the rams, they sprinkled the blood upon the altar: they killed also the lambs, and they sprinkled the blood upon the altar.

α.29.23 Kah pas8óog nomposhimwe goatsoh, wutche matcheseongane mag8ongash, ut anaquabit ketass8t, kah mukkinneonk, kah upponamauóuh wunnutchegan8óash.
E.29.23 And they brought forth the he goats for the sin offering before the king and the congregation; and they laid their hands upon them:

α.29.24 Kah sephausuénuog wunnushóuh, kah wunóhteahuwahtóog nashpe wusqueheonk, ut altarut 8nóhteahuwanshonaóont wame Israeloh: newutche ketass8t ann8team8, ne chikohtáe mag8onk, kah ne matcheseáe mag8onk, mag8wanshinash wame Israel.
E.29.24 And the priests killed them, and they made reconciliation with their blood upon the altar, to make an atonement for all Israel: for the king commanded that the burnt offering and the sin offering should be made for all Israel.

α.29.25 Kah ponau Levitsoh wekit Jehovah, nashpe cymbalsash, psalterisash, kah harpsash, neaunak wutann8team8onk David, kah Gad ketass8t wunnaumaéneumoh, kah Nathan quoshodtumwaen: newutche ne wuttin ann8teamun Jehovah, nashpe ukquoshodtumwaéneumoh.
E.29.25 And he set the Levites in the house of the LORD with cymbals, with psalteries, and with harps, according to the commandment of David, and of Gad the king's seer, and Nathan the prophet: for so was the commandment of the LORD by his prophets.

α.29.26 Kah Levitsog neepóog nashpe wutauwohteaongash David, kah sephausuénuog nashpe monopuhpequonash.
E.29.26 And the Levites stood with the instruments of David, and the priests with the trumpets.

α.29.27 Kah Hezekiah ann8team8 magunat chikohtáe mag8ongash ut Altarut: kah chikohtáe mag8ongash n8cheyeu88k, ket8homauáonk Jehovah wonk n8tshin, nashpe puhpequanash, kah nashpe auwohteaongash, nish kohquttukupash David Israelle ketass8t.
E.29.27 And Hezekiah commanded to offer the burnt offering upon the altar. And when the burnt offering began, the song of the LORD began also with the trumpets, and with the instruments ordained by David king of Israel.

α.29.28 Kah wame mukkinneonk wowussummuwaog ket8hamaénuog ket8ham8og, kah monópuhpéqunaenúog puhpequáog: wame, nô pajeh chikohtáe mag8onk pakodche ussemuk.
E.29.28 And all the congregation worshipped, and the singers sang, and the trumpeters sounded: and all this continued until the burnt offering was finished.

α.29.29 Kah mahche maghettit, ketass8t, kah wame neh weetomukqutcheh, nauwaéog, kah wowussumáog.
E.29.29 And when they had made an end of offering, the king and all that were present with him bowed themselves, and worshipped.

α.29.30 Wonk, Hezekiah ketass8t, kah sontimóog, nag ann8náog Levitsoh, 8weenomáe ket8hamauónat Jehovah, nashpe wuttinn8waongash David, kah Asaph naumwáen: kah nag wekontamwe wowénómu8hamáog, kah nauwanumwog uppuhkuk8oash, kah wowussumáog.
E.29.30 Moreover Hezekiah the king and the princes commanded the Levites to sing praise unto the LORD with the words of David, and of Asaph the seer. And they sang praises with gladness, and they bowed their heads and worshipped.

α.29.31 Neit Hezekiah naɱph8ham, kah n8wau, yeuyeu k8neetupanatamwaheómw8 kuhhogka[ò]og en Jehovah$ut, pas8tshagk, kah paudtau8k sephausuongash, kah tabattantam8e mag8ongash en wekit Jehovah: kah mukkinneonk paudtauog sephausuongash, kah tabuttantamóe mag8ongash kah neadtahshe nanóuwutteahahettit, chikohtáe mag8ongash.
E.29.31 Then Hezekiah answered and said, Now ye have consecrated yourselves unto the LORD, come near and bring sacrifices and thank offerings into the house of the LORD. And the congregation brought in sacrifices and thank offerings; and as many as were of a free heart burnt offerings.

α.29.32 Kah ne adtahshik chikohtáe mag8ongash, nish mukkinneonk paudtunkish: nequtta tahshinchag kussuog oxenog, kah nequt pasuk8e ramsog, neese pasuk88og lambsog: wame yeug wutch chikohtáe mag8onk en Jehovahut.
E.29.32 And the number of the burnt offerings, which the congregation brought, was threescore and ten bullocks, an hundred rams, and two hundred lambs: all these were for a burnt offering to the LORD.

α.29.33 Kah waneettupanatamweyeuugish, nequtta tahshe pasuk88og oxenog, kah nishwe muttannonganog kussuog shepsog.
E.29.33 And the consecrated things were six hundred oxen and three thousand sheep.

α.29.34 Qut sephausuénuog wussaum ogguhsuog, newaj n8náhettit wunnushonaóont wame chikohtáe mag8ongash: newaj wematt8oh Levitsoh aninnumungqhettit, noh pajeh anakausuonk kesteauunat, kah noh pajeh onkatoganog sephausuenuog wunneetupanatamwaheonaóont wuhhogkuh, newutche Levitsog, ánue sampweteáhaog wunneetupanatamwaheonaóont wuhhogkáuh, onk neg sephausuénuog.
E.29.34 But the priests were too few, so that they could not flay all the burnt offerings: wherefore their brethren the Levites did help them, till the work was ended, and until the other priests had sanctified themselves: for the Levites were more upright in heart to sanctify themselves than the priests.

α.29.35 Kah wonk chikohtáe mag8ongash monatash, weeche wunohteáe sephausue wes, kah wuttatam8e mag8ongash ut nish$noh chikohtáe mag8onk: neit wowussumóonk ut wekit Jehovah wunohtausu.
E.29.35 And also the burnt offerings were in abundance, with the fat of the peace offerings, and the drink offerings for every burnt offering. So the service of the house of the LORD was set in order.

α.29.36 Kah Hezekiah wekontam, kah wame missinninnúog, newutche God quagquoshwunau missinninnùh; newutche ne tiadche n$niyeup.
E.29.36 And Hezekiah rejoiced, and all the people, that God had prepared the people: for the thing was done suddenly.

α.30.1 KAh Hezekiah ann8team8 en wame Israelut kah Judahut, kah wonk wussuk[ham]auau Ephraimoh, kah Manassehoh, nag woh uppeyáunaóut wekit Jehovah ut Jerusalem, wunnanawéhtinneaóont paumukôadtuonk, en Lordut um-Manitt8moh Israel.
E.30.1 And Hezekiah sent to all Israel and Judah, and wrote letters also to Ephraim and Manasseh, that they should come to the house of the LORD at Jerusalem, to keep the passover unto the LORD God of Israel.

α.30.2 Newutche ketass8t nemunumup ken8nittuonk, kah wussontimósimoh, kah wame mukkinneonk ut Jerusalem, nanawéhtineat paumukôadtuonk ut nahohtôe nepâuzsaut.
E.30.2 For the king had taken counsel, and his princes, and all the congregation in Jerusalem, to keep the passover in the second month.

α.30.3 Newutche n8nanum8og nanawehtinneat na ahquompak, newutche sephausuénuog asquam pannuppe wunnetupanatamwáheau8og wuhhogkauh, asuh asquam missinninnuog miyaéog ut Jerusalem.
E.30.3 For they could not keep it at that time, because the priests had not sanctified themselves sufficiently, neither had the people gathered themselves together to Jerusalem.

α.30.4 Kah ne wutapeneamun ketass8t, kah wame mukkinneonk.
E.30.4 And the thing pleased the king and all the congregation.

α.30.5 Neit menehkehteóog kukquttumóonk, wahteauwahuwonat pa$pannuppe wame Israel, wutch Beersheba wehque Dan, nag woh uppeyonaóont, wunnanawehtinneaóont paumukôadtuonk, en Jehovah$ut um-Manitt8moh Israel, ut Jerusalem: newutche nag matta wutusseneau sepe, neansukwhosik.
E.30.5 So they established a decree to make proclamation throughout all Israel, from Beersheba even to Dan, that they should come to keep the passover unto the LORD God of Israel at Jerusalem: for they had not done it of a long time in such sort as it was written.

α.30.6 Neit konupwushacheg, kenunnumwog lettersash wutch wunnutcheganit ketass8t, kah wussontimósumoh, pannuppe wame Israelut kah Judahut, kah neaunak wutann8team8onk ketass8t, n8waog, kenaau wunnaumonuh Israel, qushkek wonk en Lord um-Manitt8mit Abraham, Isaak, kah Israel, kah noh pish qushkeu en kenaau sequtteáógish, kah tom8ógish, wutch wunnutcheganit Assyriae ketass8t.
E.30.6 So the posts went with the letters from the king and his princes throughout all Israel and Judah, and according to the commandment of the king, saying, Ye children of Israel, turn again unto the LORD God of Abraham, Isaac, and Israel, and he will return to the remnant of you, that are escaped out of the hand of the kings of Assyria.

α.30.7 Kah ahque tatuppeyauek k8sh8óog, kah kematt8oog neg pannesehtauoncheg Jehovah 8sh8oh um-Manitt8m8oh, newaj maguk en touushinit, neane naum8k.
E.30.7 And be not ye like your fathers, and like your brethren, which trespassed against the LORD God of their fathers, who therefore gave them up to desolation, as ye see.

α.30.8 Yeuyeu chetauussittipukanuhteogk, neasehetteup k8sh8woog: aninnumok kenutchegan8 Jehovah, kah petutteag wussanctuariumut, ne micheme waneetupanatamwahteunk: kah wowussumok Jehóvah kum-Manitt8mw8, onk woh ummishe musquanittam8onk kutamaetunkquneau.
E.30.8 Now be ye not stiffnecked, as your fathers were, but yield yourselves unto the LORD, and enter into his sanctuary, which he hath sanctified for ever: and serve the LORD your God, that the fierceness of his wrath may turn away from you.

α.30.9 Newutche quinnuppeog en Jehóvahut, kematt8óog kah keneechan8oog, pish namehteóog kiteamonteanittuonk ut anaquabenit neh sagkompagunukqutcheh en missinnainneat, neit wonk pish yeu peyoneau ohkeit: newutche Jehovah kum-Manitt8mw8 kittemonteanitteau, kah monanitteau, kah matta quinnuppenum8 wuksesuk wutch kuhhogkaout, nóh en qushkeog.
E.30.9 For if ye turn again unto the LORD, your brethren and your children shall find compassion before them that lead them captive, so that they shall come again into this land: for the LORD your God is gracious and merciful, and will not turn away his face from you, if ye return unto him.

α.30.10 Neit konupshoncheg papamshaog keitotanash, pannuppe Ephraimme wutohtimoineat kah Manasseh, kah Zebulun: qut ummamanauontamwe hahanehtauouh.
E.30.10 So the posts passed from city to city through the country of Ephraim and Manasseh even unto Zebulun: but they laughed them to scorn, and mocked them.

α.30.11 Qut monaog wutch Asher, kah Manasseh, kah Zebulun, nag hohpaheaog wuhhogkauh, kah peyaog J[u]rusalem.
E.30.11 Nevertheless divers of Asher and Manasseh and of Zebulun humbled themselves, and came to Jerusalem.

α.30.12 Wonk ut Judah, ne wunnutcheg God wunnequttutteahohkauáonk, ussenat wutann8team8onk ketass8t kah sontimóog, nashpe wuttinn8waonk Jehovah.
E.30.12 Also in Judah the hand of God was to give them one heart to do the commandment of the king and of the princes, by the word of the LORD.

α.30.13 Kah na wuttit moenau monaog missinninnuog ut Jerusalem, nanauwehtinneat mat seane petukqunegane mishadtup8onk, ut nahohtoeu nepauzsaut, ahche mishe mukkinneunk.
E.30.13 And there assembled at Jerusalem much people to keep the feast of unleavened bread in the second month, a very great congregation.

α.30.14 Kah neepoog kah amaunaog Altarsoh nish ut Jerusalem, kah wame weetemungquokeh Altaroh wutamaunauh kah uttinuhkonouh en Cidrone sepuesut.
E.30.14 And they arose and took away the altars that were in Jerusalem, and all the altars for incense took they away, and cast them into the brook Kidron.

α.30.15 Neit nehtóog paumukoadtuonk nabo yeuquinohhog nahohtôeu nepauz, kah sephausuenuog kah Levitsog akodchuog, kah nag wunneetupanatamwaheaog wuhhogkauh, kah petukodtoog chikohtae mag8ongash en wekit Jehovah.
E.30.15 Then they killed the passover on the fourteenth day of the second month: and the priests and the Levites were ashamed, and sanctified themselves, and brought in the burnt offerings into the house of the LORD.

α.30.16 Kah nag neep8og ut wutayeuongan8out, ne asehettit, neaunak wuttinnaumatuonk Moses Manittowomp: sephausuenuog seáohteaog wusquehéonk, wutch wunnutchegan8out Levits[o]g.
E.30.16 And they stood in their place after their manner, according to the law of Moses the man of God: the priests sprinkled the blood, which they received of the hand of the Levites.

α.30.17 Newutche monaog ut mukkinneonganit neg mátta waneetupanatamwaheoncheg: newutche Levitsog ahtoog meechumuhkonittuonk wunnehtauwonshonat paumukóadtuonk, nish$noh howan mat pahkeseg, nah 8neetupanatamwaheonat en Jehovah$ut.
E.30.17 For there were many in the congregation that were not sanctified: therefore the Levites had the charge of the killing of the passovers for every one that was not clean, to sanctify them unto the LORD.

α.30.18 Newutche mataánukeg missinninnuog, monaog wutch Ephraim, kah Manasseh, Ishachar kah Zebulun, matta pahkheauog wuhhogkauh, qut meechuog paumukoadtuonk, panneonk neansukwhosik, qut Hezechiah uppeantamwanshuh, n8wau: noh wunneetou Lord ahquontamauonch nish$noh pasuk8,
E.30.18 For a multitude of the people, even many of Ephraim, and Manasseh, Issachar, and Zebulun, had not cleansed themselves, yet did they eat the passover otherwise than it was written. But Hezekiah prayed for them, saying, The good LORD pardon every one

α.30.19 Quagquoshwunuk wuttah natinneawhonat God, Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh 8sh8oh, toh$kónogque matta wuttinne pahkesein, Sánctuarie pahkesuonk.
E.30.19 That prepareth his heart to seek God, the LORD God of his fathers, though he be not cleansed according to the purification of the sanctuary.

α.30.20 Kah Jehovah n8tauau Hezechiahoh, kah netskeheau missinninnuh.
E.30.20 And the LORD hearkened to Hezekiah, and healed the people.

α.30.21 Kah wunnáumonuh Israel, neg apitcheg Jerusalem, nag nanawehteauog mat seane petukqunnegane mishadtup8onk, nesausuk tahshikquinne, nashpe mishe weekontamóonk, kah Levitsog kah sephausuenuog, woweenomaog Jehovahoh asekesukokish, nashpe mishont8wâe aúwohteaongásh en Jehovah$ut.
E.30.21 And the children of Israel that were present at Jerusalem kept the feast of unleavened bread seven days with great gladness: and the Levites and the priests praised the LORD day by day, singing with loud instruments unto the LORD.

α.30.22 Kah Hezechiah wunneetahhae ken8nau wame Levitsoh neg kohk8tomwehteacheg wunne kuhk8tomwehteaonk Jehovah: kah nag meetsuog, pannuppe wame mishadtupp8ongash nesausuk tahshikquinne, maghettit wunohteae mag8ongash, & sompuahettit, Jehovahoh 8sh8oh um-Manitt8m8uh.
E.30.22 And Hezekiah spake comfortably unto all the Levites that taught the good knowledge of the LORD: and they did eat throughout the feast seven days, offering peace offerings, and making confession to the LORD God of their fathers.

α.30.23 Kah mamusse mukkinneonk ken8nittuog nanawehtinneat, onkatogish nesausuk tahshikquinogkodtash: kah nanawehteaog onkatogish nesausuk tahshikquinogkodtash nashpe wekontamoonk.
E.30.23 And the whole assembly took counsel to keep other seven days: and they kept other seven days with gladness.

α.30.24 Newutche Hezechiàh Judae ketass8t aninnumauau mukkinneongoh nequt muttannonganogkussuoh oxinoh, kah nesausuk tahshe muttannonganogkussuog shepsoh: kah Sontim[ô]og aninnumauaog mukkiñeongh, nequt muttannonganogkussuoh oxinoh, & piogque muttannonganogkussuoh shepsoh, kah monaóg sephausuenuog wunnetupanatamwaheog wuhhogkauh.
E.30.24 For Hezekiah king of Judah did give to the congregation a thousand bullocks and seven thousand sheep; and the princes gave to the congregation a thousand bullocks and ten thousand sheep: and a great number of priests sanctified themselves.

α.30.25 Kah wame Judae mukkinneonk weeche sephausuenuog kah Levitsog, kah wame mukkinneonk neg sohhogig wutch Israel, kah pen8wohteaog neg sohhogig wutch ohkit Israel kah nag apitcheg Judah, weekontamwog.
E.30.25 And all the congregation of Judah, with the priests and the Levites, and all the congregation that came out of Israel, and the strangers that came out of the land of Israel, and that dwelt in Judah, rejoiced.

α.30.26 Neit missi wekontamóonk ut Jerusalem, newutche nadteoh pomontog Solomon wunnaumonuh David Israelle ketass8t, wanne wuttinnauouh ut Jerusalem.
E.30.26 So there was great joy in Jerusalem: for since the time of Solomon the son of David king of Israel there was not the like in Jerusalem.

α.30.27 Neit sephausuenuog kah Levitsog nepauog & wunnanumaog missinninnuh: kah wuttauatonkquodt n8tunkquodt: & uppeantam8ongan8 kuhkuhquem8 ut 8neetupanatamwe ayeuonganit, en kesukqut.
E.30.27 Then the priests the Levites arose and blessed the people: and their voice was heard, and their prayer came up to his holy dwelling place, even unto heaven.

α.31.1 KAh yeu wame pakodjteomuk, wame Israel neg na apitcheg, sohhamwog en Judae keitotanáhtu, kah sohquttahwhaog nunneukontunkoh, & m8sittahhamwog kuppiyeuash, kah n8konteáog qunuhqui ayeuongash, kah altarsash wutch Judah, kah Benjain, kah wonk ut Ephraim kah Manasseh; nô pajeh uppapaquanne ushkoméhtinneaóont: neit wame wunnaumonuh Israel qushkeog, nish$noh wosketomp en wutoht[ó]onganit, en nehenwonche wutotanaóont.
E.31.1 Now when all this was finished, all Israel that were present went out to the cities of Judah, and brake the images in pieces, and cut down the groves, and threw down the high places and the altars out of all Judah and Benjamin, in Ephraim also and Manasseh, until they had utterly destroyed them all. Then all the children of Israel returned, every man to his possession, into their own cities.

α.31.2 Kah Hezekiah kuhquttum, 8nappuongan8oash sephausuenuog, kah Levitsog neaunak 8nappuongan8oash, nishnoh wosketomp neaunak wutannunôsuonk, sephausuénuog, kah Levitsog, wutche chikohtáe mag8ongash, kah wutche wunohteáe mag8ongash, wuttinneumuhkausinneat, kah tabuttantamunat, kah wowenomuwónat, ut weeke squontamut Jehovah.
E.31.2 And Hezekiah appointed the courses of the priests and the Levites after their courses, every man according to his service, the priests and Levites for burnt offerings and for peace offerings, to minister, and to give thanks, and to praise in the gates of the tents of the LORD.

α.31.3 Kah wonk ketass8t wutchippiyeum wutch ummaumachiit wutch chikohtáe mag8onk, wutch nompoáe kah wunnonkquae chikohtáe mag8onk, kah Sabath$daye chikohtáe mag8ongash, kah wutch wuske nepâuzsahtu, kah wutch kukquttum8e mishadtupp8ongash, neansukwhosik ut wuttinnaumatuonganit Jehovah.
E.31.3 He appointed also the king's portion of his substance for the burnt offerings, to wit, for the morning and evening burnt offerings, and the burnt offerings for the sabbaths, and for the new moons, and for the set feasts, as it is written in the law of the LORD.

α.31.4 Kah wonk ann8nau missinninnúh neg wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, aninnumauónat wutchippiyeum8 sephausuénuog kah Levitsog, onk woh wutt8anatamwog ut wuttinnaumatuonganit Jehovah.
E.31.4 Moreover he commanded the people that dwelt in Jerusalem to give the portion of the priests and the Levites, that they might be encouraged in the law of the LORD.

α.31.5 Kah ann8team8onk quenau sohweem8uk, wunnaumonuh Israel m8cheke paudtauoh, kakeneumunne weatchiminneash, wine, kah oyle, kah hony, kah nish$noh teag piogqu[é] chippáe m8cheke petakodtóog.
E.31.5 And as soon as the commandment came abroad, the children of Israel brought in abundance the firstfruits of corn, wine, and oil, and honey, and of all the increase of the field; and the tithe of all things brought they in abundantly.

α.31.6 Kah papaume wunnaumonuh Israel kah Judah, neg wadohkitcheg Judae keitotanahtu: nag wonk petakodtóog uppapiogque chippissuongan8óash oxenog, kah shepsog, kah piogque chippágish waneetupanatamweyeu8gish, nis hwaneetupanatamwahteomukish en Jehovah$ut um-Manitt8m8óut, kah wunannomwunkquottauunaóash.
E.31.6 And concerning the children of Israel and Judah, that dwelt in the cities of Judah, they also brought in the tithe of oxen and sheep, and the tithe of holy things which were consecrated unto the LORD their God, and laid them by heaps.

α.31.7 Ut nash8it nepâuz n8che ponamwog newaj kutungquag, kah uppakodche usseneau ut nesausuk adtahs8it nepâuz.
E.31.7 In the third month they began to lay the foundation of the heaps, and finished them in the seventh month.

α.31.8 Kah Hezekiah, kah sontimóog paáhettit, kah naumohettit numwonkquâu, nag wunnanumáog Jehovahoh, kah ummissinninneumoh Israeloh.
E.31.8 And when Hezekiah and the princes came and saw the heaps, they blessed the LORD, and his people Israel.

α.31.9 Neit Hezekiah nat8tomauau sephausuénúh & Levitsoh papaume nomwonkquagish.
E.31.9 Then Hezekiah questioned with the priests and the Levites concerning the heaps.

α.31.10 Kah Azariah kehche sephausuénin, wutch wekit Zadok wunnamp8hamauoh kah n8wau, nadteuh n8che paudtauéhettit mag8ongash ut wekit Jehovah, wamat nummetsuonganun, kah numm8cheke sequtteamumun: newutche Jehovah wunnanumau ummissinninneumoh, kah ne sequtteamuk, yeu monak.
E.31.10 And Azariah the chief priest of the house of Zadok answered him, and said, Since the people began to bring the offerings into the house of the LORD, we have had enough to eat, and have left plenty: for the LORD hath blessed his people; and that which is left is this great store.

α.31.11 Neit Hezekiah ann8teamo quagquashwunnumunat chambersash ut wekit Jehovah, kah nag quagquashwunnumunáoash.
E.31.11 Then Hezekiah commanded to prepare chambers in the house of the LORD; and they prepared them,

α.31.12 Kah petukodtóog mag8ongash kah piogque chippagish, kah wunnetupanatamwéyeu8gish, pabuhtánumwe: kah Cononiah wul-Levit yeu nanawunuk, kah Shimeioh weematoh wutasukunkquoh.
E.31.12 And brought in the offerings and the tithes and the dedicated things faithfully: over which Cononiah the Levite was ruler, and Shimei his brother was the next.

α.31.13 Kah Jehiel, kah Azasiah, kah Nahath, kah Asahel, kah Jerimoth, kah Jozabad, kah Eliel, kah Ismachiah, kah Mahath, kah Benajah, aninnohsuénuog ut wunnutcheganit Cononiah, kah Shemeioh weematoh, nean ann8teamwit Hezekiah ketass8t, kah Azariah nanánuwáen ut wekit God.
