E.31.13 And Jehiel, and Azaziah, and Nahath, and Asahel, and Jerimoth, and Jozabad, and Eliel, and Ismachiah, and Mahath, and Benaiah, were overseers under the hand of Cononiah and Shimei his brother, at the commandment of Hezekiah the king, and Azariah the ruler of the house of God.

α.31.14 Kah Kore wunnaumonuh Im[m]ah wul-Levit, nanausquontamwáen nogque en wutchepwoiyeu, nánawunnum nano[u]we mag8ongash en Godut, wutchadchabenumunat mag8ongash en Jehovahut, kah ánue wunneetupanatamweyeu8gish.
E.31.14 And Kore the son of Imnah the Levite, the porter toward the east, was over the freewill offerings of God, to distribute the oblations of the LORD, and the most holy things.

α.31.15 Kah asuhkunk, Edenoh, kah Minjamin, kah Jeshua, kah Shemajah, Amariah, kah Shechaniah, ut wut8tanaóut sephausueénuog, ut kukquttumóe anninnohsuonganit, wuttinnumauonaóont weemat8óuh, ut wutchadchepuongan8óut, naneese matikenutche, kah papeissisinitcheh.
E.31.15 And next him were Eden, and Miniamin, and Jeshua, and Shemaiah, Amariah, and Shecaniah, in the cities of the priests, in their set office, to give to their brethren by courses, as well to the great as to the small:

α.31.16 Chaubokish mukkachukqussueu ontseongash, wutch nishwe kodtumwohkumunat, kah piáme, wehque nish$noh pasuk noh petutteadt ut wekit Jehovah, kesukodtae wutchippiyeum, wutche wuttinneumuhkausuonk, ut meechumuhkónaongan8óut, neaunak 8nappuongan8óash.
E.31.16 Beside their genealogy of males, from three years old and upward, even unto every one that entereth into the house of the LORD, his daily portion for their service in their charges according to their courses;

α.31.17 Na$neswe ut wutontseongan8óut sephausuénuog, nashpe wek8oash 8sh8oh, kah ut Levitsut, wutch nesnehchage kodtumwohkomunat, kah piáme, ut 8nappuongan8 ut meechumuhkonaongan8óut.
E.31.17 Both to the genealogy of the priests by the house of their fathers, and the Levites from twenty years old and upward, in their charges by their courses;

α.31.18 Kah ut wutontseongan8óut wame uppeississum8uh, ummittamwuss8uh, kah wunnaumonáut, kah wuttaun8oh, pannuppe wame mukkinneonganit: newutche ut ummeechumuhkonaonganon8óut, wunneetupanatamwaheáog ut wunneetupanatam8onganit.
E.31.18 And to the genealogy of all their little ones, their wives, and their sons, and their daughters, through all the congregation: for in their set office they sanctified themselves in holiness:

α.31.19 Kah wonk wunnuamonuh Aaron, sephausuénuog, neg ut ohteuhkonehtu sussippoiyeue otanat, ut nishnoh chippe keitotanat[,] [w]osketompaog neg wesuongane agkemutcheg, aninnumauónat wutchippiyeumash, wame nompaésuog ut kenugke sephausuenúut, kah en wame nag agkemutcheg ut wutontseongan8óut Levitsog.
E.31.19 Also of the sons of Aaron the priests, which were in the fields of the suburbs of their cities, in every several city, the men that were expressed by name, to give portions to all the males among the priests, and to all that were reckoned by genealogies among the Levites.

α.31.20 Kah yeu wutussen Hezekiah pannuppu[-] wame Judah, kah usseu ne wanegik kah sampwagk, kah wanumuhkuteyeu8k ut anaquabit Jehovah um-Manitt8moh.
E.31.20 And thus did Hezekiah throughout all Judah, and wrought that which was good and right and truth before the LORD his God.

α.31.21 Kah ut nishnoh anakausuonganit ne n8che usseit, wutche wuttinneumuhkausuonk ut wekit God: kah ut [en]naumatuonganit, kah ut ann8team8onganit wunnátinnewhonat um-Manitt8moh, wutussen nashpe mamusse wuttah, kah wunniyeu.
E.31.21 And in every work that he began in the service of the house of God, and in the law, and in the commandments, to seek his God, he did it with all his heart, and prospered.

α.32.1 MAhche yeush nnag, kah manuhkehteomuk Senakrip Assiyriae ketass8t, peyau, kah petutteau Judah, kah ayeuuhkonittue tuppuksinn8wontam pummeneutausué keitotanash, kah unnantam nag nussohkomonunk.
E.32.1 After these things, and the establishment thereof, Sennacherib king of Assyria came, and entered into Judah, and encamped against the fenced cities, and thought to win them for himself.

α.32.2 Kah Hezekiah nag* Sinakrib mahche peyau, kah pakodtantam wutayeuuhkontamunat Jerusalem.
E.32.2 And when Hezekiah saw that Sennacherib was come, and that he was purposed to fight against Jerusalem,

α.32.3 Nagum kah wussontimosimoh, kah ummenuhkesueneumoh ken8nittuog, kah kuppuhhamunat wuttahhamongash, nish poquodchu otani: kah nag wutannumauouh.
E.32.3 He took counsel with his princes and his mighty men to stop the waters of the fountains which were without the city: and they did help him.

α.32.4 Newaj monaog missinninnuog miyaehettit, neg kobhogeg wame wuttahhamongash, kah sepuiṡ ne panupushonk nashaue ohkekontu, n8waog Assyriae ketass8tamwog paáhettit, toh$wutch woh nemehteauahettit monat nippe.
E.32.4 So there was gathered much people together, who stopped all the fountains, and the brook that ran through the midst of the land, saying, Why should the kings of Assyria come, and find much water?

α.32.5 Kah wonk menehkheau wuhhogkuh, kah onchehteau wame pummenutunk, ne tauwutchashonkup, kah ukqunuhqutteauun wehque wonkon8sinut, kah onkatog pummeneutunk poquadchit, kah onchehteao Millo ut wutotanat David, kah ayim dartsash kah ogqunegash monatash.
E.32.5 Also he strengthened himself, and built up all the wall that was broken, and raised it up to the towers, and another wall without, and repaired Millo in the city of David, and made darts and shields in abundance.

α.32.6 Kah kehtimau ayeuteae mugquompuh ut missinninnutu, kah ummianumauonuh, ut squontamwe toumaogwehtu ut otanat, kah 8nanakumoh, n8wau.
E.32.6 And he set captains of war over the people, and gathered them together to him in the street of the gate of the city, and spake comfortably to them, saying,

α.32.7 Menuhkesek, kah wutt8anatam8k, wabesehtok asuh chepshuhteok, wutche Assyriae ketass8t, asuh wutch mataanutcheh neh weechogqutcheh: newutche monaog k8weech8humukumun, onk neh weetomukqutcheh.
E.32.7 Be strong and courageous, be not afraid nor dismayed for the king of Assyria, nor for all the multitude that is with him: for there be more with us than with him:

α.32.8 Noh weechayeumuk weyausue muhpit, qut k8wetomukumun Jehovah num-Manitt8mun kuttannumunkqunnanonut, & wutayeuuhkonat kutayeuwehteaonganunonut, kah missinninnuog anwôsinnawontamwog ukkutt8wongash Hezekiah Judae ketass8t.
E.32.8 With him is an arm of flesh; but with us is the LORD our God to help us, and to fight our battles. And the people rested themselves upon the words of Hezekiah king of Judah.

α.32.9 Mahche yeu nag, Senakrib Assyriae ketass8t ann8nau wuttinneumoh en Jerusalem (qut nagum ayeuuhkontam Lachish, kah wame ummenuhkesuonk weechog,) en Hezekiah ut Judae ketass8t, kah en wame Judah, neg apitcheg Jerusalem, n8wau.
E.32.9 After this did Sennacherib king of Assyria send his servants to Jerusalem, (but he himself laid siege against Lachish, and all his power with him,) unto Hezekiah king of Judah, and unto all Judah that were at Jerusalem, saying,

α.32.10 Yeu wussin Synakreb Assyriae ketass8t teaguas kuppabahtantamumw8, waj chequnehtamog weenuhkoadtuonk ut Jerusalem?
E.32.10 Thus saith Sennacherib king of Assyria, Whereon do ye trust, that ye abide in the siege in Jerusalem?

α.32.11 Sunnummatta Hezekiah kenupweshanukw8, magunat kuhhogkaoog en mashagqunneae kah kuhkutt8n8e nuppunat, an8wadt, Jehovah num-Manitt8mun pish kuttomhukqun wutch wunnutcheganit Assyriae ketass8t?
E.32.11 Doth not Hezekiah persuade you to give over yourselves to die by famine and by thirst, saying, The LORD our God shall deliver us out of the hand of the king of Assyria?

α.32.12 Sunnummatta nenan Hezekiah amaunum8 ukqunniyeuongash, kah wut-Altarumash, kah ann8nau Judahhoh kah Jerusalemoh, n8wau, pish k8wowussummuwom8 ut anaquohtag pasuk Altar, kah pish kuttit chikossumuneau wetemungquok.
E.32.12 Hath not the same Hezekiah taken away his high places and his altars, and commanded Judah and Jerusalem, saying, Ye shall worship before one altar, and burn incense upon it?

α.32.13 Sunnummatta k8wahteomw8 uttoh n8sh kah neen anheogkut wame wutohtimoinne missinninnuog: sunnum$Manitt8m8oh yeug wutohtimoneunk, tapenumwussahhaneg wuttomwutteauunnaóont wutch nunnutcheganit.
E.32.13 Know ye not what I and my fathers have done unto all the people of other lands? were the gods of the nations of those lands any ways able to deliver their lands out of mine hand?

α.32.14 Howan kenugke wame Manitt8og, ut yeush wutohtimoneash, nish n8sh ôshkomehtuhhogkupash, noh woh tomheont ummissinninneumoh, wutch nunnutcheganit, newaj woh kum-Manitt8mw8 tapenuk kuttomhukqunnaoont wutch nunnutcheganit.
E.32.14 Who was there among all the gods of those nations that my fathers utterly destroyed, that could deliver his people out of mine hand, that your God should be able to deliver you out of mine hand?

α.32.15 Newutche yeuyeu, ahque Hezekiah as8kekomuk8k, asuh yeu$in nupweshanuk8k, asuh ahque wunnamptok: newutche matta howae Manit ut ne teague wutohtimoineat, asuh ass8tam8onganit, tapenum8 wuttomheonat ummissinninneumoh wutch nunnutcheganit, kah wutch wunnutcehganit n8sh, uttoh an woh ogguhse, kum-Manitt8mw8 kuppohquohwhunukquneau wutch nunnutcheganit?
E.32.15 Now therefore let not Hezekiah deceive you, nor persuade you on this manner, neither yet believe him: for no god of any nation or kingdom was able to deliver his people out of mine hand, and out of the hand of my fathers: how much less shall your God deliver you out of mine hand?

α.32.16 Kah wonk nano wuttinneumoh matcheunnaog Jehovahoh Manitt8h, kah wuttinneumoh Hezekiahoh.
E.32.16 And his servants spake yet more against the LORD God, and against his servant Hezekiah.

α.32.17 Kah wonk wussukhum mamatcheunnonat Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh Israel, kah ummamatcheunnonat, n8waog, neane onkatogish wutohtimoneash um-Manitt8m8uh matta tomwehheo8og ummissinninneum8uh wutch nunnutcheganit, netatuppe Hezekiah um-Manitt8moh matta woh tomweheunk ummissinninneumoh wutch nunnutcheganit.
E.32.17 He wrote also letters to rail on the LORD God of Israel, and to speak against him, saying, As the gods of the nations of other lands have not delivered their people out of mine hand, so shall not the God of Hezekiah deliver his people out of mine hand.

α.32.18 Neit mishont8wae ann8tauwahtauwaog Jewsont8waonk Jerusalem missinninnuh, neg apitcheg woskeche neutunganit, wussiaskishononaoont kah 8tamehheonaoont, woh wussohkomunaóont kitotan.
E.32.18 Then they cried with a loud voice in the Jews' speech unto the people of Jerusalem that were on the wall, to affright them, and to trouble them; that they might take the city.

α.32.19 Kah matche unnaog Jerusaleme Manitto, neane matcheunahettit wutohtimoinne Manitto, neh wunnutchegane anakausuonk wosketomp.
E.32.19 And they spake against the God of Jerusalem, as against the gods of the people of the earth, which were the work of the hands of man.

α.32.20 Newaj Hezekiah ketass8t, kah quoshodtumwaen Isaiah, wunnaumonuh Amoz, peantamwog, kah móog en kesukqut.
E.32.20 And for this cause Hezekiah the king, and the prophet Isaiah the son of Amoz, prayed and cried to heaven.

α.32.21 Kah Jehovah ann8nau Angeloh, noh tametahwhont wame menuhkesuenunnuh: kah negonshanutcheh, kah mugquompuh ut wuttuppukkussinn8onganit ketass8t ut Assyria, neit akodchuwuskesukquae qushkeu en nehenwonche wutohkit, kah petutteadt um-Manitt8moh wekit, nah sohhamunutcheh wutch nehenwonche wunnohkussit, nawuttit nushoneau nashpe togkodteg.
E.32.21 And the LORD sent an angel, which cut off all the mighty men of valour, and the leaders and captains in the camp of the king of Assyria. So he returned with shame of face to his own land. And when he was come into the house of his god, they that came forth of his own bowels slew him there with the sword.

α.32.22 Yeu wuttinne Jehovah tomheon Hezekiahoh, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, wutch wunnutcheganit Senakerib Assyria ketass8t, kah wutch wame wunnutchegan8out, kah wutuss8unuh waeenu.
E.32.22 Thus the LORD saved Hezekiah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem from the hand of Sennacherib the king of Assyria, and from the hand of all other, and guided them on every side.

α.32.23 Kah monaog paudtoog mag8ongash en Jerusalemut, kah mag8ongash en Hezekiah ut Judae ketáss8tamut: newaj misheheont ut anaquohtag wame wutohtimoneash, newutch n8che.
E.32.23 And many brought gifts unto the LORD to Jerusalem, and presents to Hezekiah king of Judah: so that he was magnified in the sight of all nations from thenceforth.

α.32.24 Yeush kesukodtash nupp8e mahchinau Hezekiah, kah peantamauau Jehováhoh, kah ukken8nuh, kah ukkehkenasukauoh.
E.32.24 In those days Hezekiah was sick to the death, and prayed unto the LORD: and he spake unto him, and he gave him a sign.

α.32.25 Qut Hezekiah matta nompoadtehtea8 neaunak wuteiyeuongash nish aseanshitcheh, newutche wuttah tahshem8, newaj musquanumit, kah ut Judah, kah ut Jerusalem.
E.32.25 But Hezekiah rendered not again according to the benefit done unto him; for his heart was lifted up: therefore there was wrath upon him, and upon Judah and Jerusalem.

α.32.26 Qut Hezekiah hohpaheau wuhhogkuh, wutche wuttah pittuanumóonk (naneeswe nagum kah wadokitcheg Jerusalem) newaj ummusquantamòonk Jehovah matta nuhkuhkunk8og ashpomontog Hezekiah.
E.32.26 Notwithstanding Hezekiah humbled himself for the pride of his heart, both he and the inhabitants of Jerusalem, so that the wrath of the LORD came not upon them in the days of Hezekiah.

α.32.27 Kah Hezekiah mishenauwetu, kah quttianumukqussu: kah ayimauau wuhhogkuh nompakouune ahhohtagish, ohtaut Silver, kah Gold, kah magoadtikish qussukquanash, kah Spicash, kag ogqunegash, kah wame eiyane tapenunkquotte nompakouunash
E.32.27 And Hezekiah had exceeding much riches and honour: and he made himself treasuries for silver, and for gold, and for precious stones, and for spices, and for shields, and for all manner of pleasant jewels;

α.32.28 Kah wonk meechumikkomukquash ponamunat nano neekinee weatchiminneash, kah wine, kah pumme kah stalsash wutch wame eiyane puppinashimwog kah flockse kommukquash.
E.32.28 Storehouses also for the increase of corn, and wine, and oil; and stalls for all manner of beasts, and cotes for flocks.

α.32.29 Nano quohquashwehtamun keitotanash kah flockse, kah heardse ahtoongash m8cheke: newutch God wuttinnumau monatash maumachiash.
E.32.29 Moreover he provided him cities, and possessions of flocks and herds in abundance: for God had given him substance very much.

α.32.30 Ne nan wonk Hezekiah kuppuhham onk[ó]ue anohtag Giheone sepuemes, kah uppiuhsuke w8mussuuttauun, wutcheksueiyeu wutotanat David, kah Hezekiah wunniyeum8ash wame wutanakausuongash
E.32.30 This same Hezekiah also stopped the upper watercourse of Gihon, and brought it straight down to the west side of the city of David. And Hezekiah prospered in all his works.

α.32.31 Qut ne ut, papaume wutan8naeneumoh Bab[a]lone sontimóog, neh noh ain ann8nahetticheh, nat8tamuhkonat ne monchanatam8onk, aunak ne ohkeit, God wunnukkonuh, ukqutchheonat, woh 8wahteauunat wame ne wuttahhut.
E.32.31 Howbeit in the business of the ambassadors of the princes of Babylon, who sent unto him to enquire of the wonder that was done in the land, God left him, to try him, that he might know all that was in his heart.

α.32.32 Kah onkatogish wutusseongash Hezechiah, kah 8nneseonk, kusseh, nish wussukwhosuash, ut ummonomonsuonganit Isayah quoshodtumwaen wunnaumonuh Amoz, kah 8sukuhwhongan8out Judae kah Israelle ketass8tamwog.
E.32.32 Now the rest of the acts of Hezekiah, and his goodness, behold, they are written in the vision of Isaiah the prophet, the son of Amoz, and in the book of the kings of Judah and Israel.

α.32.33 Kah Hezekiah weesequom8mau 8sh8oh, kah nah upposekinouh, ut kehcheu weenohkeit wunnaumonuh David: kah wame Judah, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, ukquehtianumouh, kah napunit, kah Manassehoh wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tamomukquoh.
E.32.33 And Hezekiah slept with his fathers, and they buried him in the chiefest of the sepulchres of the sons of David: and all Judah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem did him honour at his death. And Manasseh his son reigned in his stead.

α.33.1 MAnasseh nabo neese kodtumwohkomup n8che ketass8tam8it, kah napanna tahshinchage kah napanna tahshe kodtum8 ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem,
E.33.1 Manasseh was twelve years old when he began to reign, and he reigned fifty and five years in Jerusalem:

α.33.2 Qut usseu ne machuk ut anaquabit Jehovah, neaunak wannishkeneunkquott8m8ash penuohteáog, neh Jehovah pagkenoncheh ut anaquabhettit wunnaumonuh Israel.
E.33.2 But did that which was evil in the sight of the LORD, like unto the abominations of the heathen, whom the LORD had cast out before the children of Israel.

α.33.3 Newutche wonk ayim qunuhqui ayeuongash nish 8shoh Hezekiah n8ketahhamineupash; kah ayima[u]au altarsash Baalim, kah ayim kuppiyeuash, kah wowussumau wame kesukque kenauwameonk, kah nah 8tinninneumuhkauoh.
E.33.3 For he built again the high places which Hezekiah his father had broken down, and he reared up altars for Baalim, and made groves, and worshipped all the host of heaven, and served them.

α.33.4 Wonk ayim altarsash ut wekit Jehovah, ne papaume Jehovah n8wop, ut Jerusalem pish n8wesuonk ohtau micheme.
E.33.4 Also he built altars in the house of the LORD, whereof the LORD had said, In Jerusalem shall my name be for ever.

α.33.5 Kah ayimauau altarsash wame kesukque kenauwameonk, ut neese chippinneutunkanit, wekit Jehovah.
E.33.5 And he built altars for all the host of heaven in the two courts of the house of the LORD.

α.33.6 Kah pannupwusháheau wunneechanoh n8táut ut 8nóuhkoiyeuut wunnaumonuh Hinnon: kahwonk kuhkinneasu utt8cheyeu8ash, kah auwohteau pauwauwongash, kah auwohteau mamontamó8onk, kah auwohteau matche nashauonk, kah kôsikquomoh: usseu ne m8cheke machuk ut anaquabit Jehovah, m8mosqheónat.
E.33.6 And he caused his children to pass through the fire in the valley of the son of Hinnom: also he observed times, and used enchantments, and used witchcraft, and dealt with a familiar spirit, and with wizards: he wrought much evil in the sight of the LORD, to provoke him to anger.

α.33.7 Ponau kogoximwe nunneukontungoh (nunneukontunkoh ne kezheumpoh) ut wekit God, ne papaume God anomp Davidoh, kah Solomonoh wunnaumonuh, yeuut wetuómut, kah ut Jerusalem, ne pepenamomp ánue onk wame wutchippan8ongash Israel, ne nummicheme ponamun n8wesuonk.
E.33.7 And he set a carved image, the idol which he had made, in the house of God, of which God had said to David and to Solomon his son, In this house, and in Jerusalem, which I have chosen before all the tribes of Israel, will I put my name for ever:

α.33.8 Kah matta wonk nutontahtóou wusseet Israel, wutch ohkeit ne kahtimog k8sh8óut: nunnukqussehettit wame nean ann8nog, neanussit mamusse naumatuonk, kah kuhkinnum8ongash kah kuhk8waongash náshpe wunnutcheganit Moses.
E.33.8 Neither will I any more remove the foot of Israel from out of the land which I have appointed for your fathers; so that they will take heed to do all that I have commanded them, according to the whole law and the statutes and the ordinances by the hand of Moses.

α.33.9 Kah Manasse uppanneusseáheuh Judah kah neg wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, kah ánue matcheseumónat penuwohteáog, neh Jehovah ushkomehtahwhoncheh wutch anaquabhettit wunnaumonuh Israel.
E.33.9 So Manasseh made Judah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem to err, and to do worse than the heathen, whom the LORD had destroyed before the children of Israel.

α.33.10 Kah Jehovah ken8nau Manassehoh, kah ummissinninneumoh, qut nag matta n8tam8og.
E.33.10 And the LORD spake to Manasseh, and to his people: but they would not hearken.

α.33.11 Newaj Jehovah nukkuhkauwáheont Assyriae ketass8t ukkenauwamée mugquomp8moh, neg tohqunoncheg Manasseh, ut kenugke assinnekôussehtu, kah wutohtogkupinóuh nashpe chainsash, kah wutuss8unóuh Babylon.
E.33.11 Wherefore the LORD brought upon them the captains of the host of the king of Assyria, which took Manasseh among the thorns, and bound him with fetters, and carried him to Babylon.

α.33.12 Kah onkquanumwit, nanompassumau Lord um-Manitt8moh, kah mishe hohpaheau wuhhogkuh anaquabenit um-Manitt8moh 8sh8oh.
E.33.12 And when he was in affliction, he besought the LORD his God, and humbled himself greatly before the God of his fathers,

α.33.13 Kah uppeantamauoh, kah wussohkukquoh, kah wunn8tamauoh 8wéhquetumóonk, kah wonk uppas8oh Jerusalem, en wutass8tam8onganit, neit Manasseh wahteoh, Jehovah noh Manit.
E.33.13 And prayed unto him: and he was intreated of him, and heard his supplication, and brought him again to Jerusalem into his kingdom. Then Manasseh knew that the LORD he was God.

α.33.14 Kah mahche yeu nnag ayim pummeneutunk ut poquadche wutotanat David, wutcheksuiyeu Gihon, ut 8nouhkóiyeuut wehque ahhut petutteamuk namohse squontamut, kah woweenúhsheau Ophel, kah ukqunuhqueteauun, kah ayeuteae mugquompuh upponuh ut wame Judae pummeneutausue keitotanahtu.
E.33.14 Now after this he built a wall without the city of David, on the west side of Gihon, in the valley, even to the entering in at the fish gate, and compassed about Ophel, and raised it up a very great height, and put captains of war in all the fenced cities of Judah.

α.33.15 Kah amaunau pen8e manitt8h, kah nunneukontunk wutch wekit Jehovah, kah wame altarsash nish ayikupash, ut wadchuut wekit Jehovah, kah ut Jerusalem, kah wussohw[a]uhkonuh wutch otanat.
E.33.15 And he took away the strange gods, and the idol out of the house of the LORD, and all the altars that he had built in the mount of the house of the LORD, and in Jerusalem, and cast them out of the city.

α.33.16 Kah onchteau wut-altarum Lord, kah na wuttit sephausin wunohteáe sephausuongash, kah tabuttantamóe mag8ongash, kah ann8nau Jodahoh wowussumónat Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel.
E.33.16 And he repaired the altar of the LORD, and sacrificed thereon peace offerings and thank offerings, and commanded Judah to serve the LORD God of Israel.

α.33.17 Qut missinninnuog ashpummeu sephausuog ut qunuhqui ayeuonganit, qut webe en Jehovahut um-Manitt8m8uh.
E.33.17 Nevertheless the people did sacrifice still in the high places, yet unto the LORD their God only.

α.33.18 Kah onkatogish wutusseongash Manasseh, kah uppeantamóonk en um-Manitt8mut, kah ukkutt8wongash naumwaenúog neg kônono[n]cheg ut 8wesuonganit Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh nish ut up-b8kum8óut Israelle ketass8tamwog.
E.33.18 Now the rest of the acts of Manasseh, and his prayer unto his God, and the words of the seers that spake to him in the name of the LORD God of Israel, behold, they are written in the book of the kings of Israel.

α.33.19 Uppeantamóonk wonk, kah uttoh an God nashpe nupweshanómukup, kah wame ummatcheseonk, kah uppanneusseonk, kah ayeuongash ne adt ayikup qunuhqui ayeuongash, kah ponukup kuppiyeuash, kah kogoxumwe nunneukontunkoh, [a]sq ohhohpog: kusseh nish wussekwhosuash ut kenugke ukkutt8wongan8ut naumwaenúog.
E.33.19 His prayer also, and how God was intreated of him, and all his sins, and his trespass, and the places wherein he built high places, and set up groves and graven images, before he was humbled: behold, they are written among the sayings of the seers.

α.33.20 Neit Manasseh weesequom8mau 8shoh, kah upposekinóuh ut nehenwonche wekit: kah Ammonoh wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tamomukquoh.
E.33.20 So Manasseh slept with his fathers, and they buried him in his own house: and Amon his son reigned in his stead.

α.33.21 Amon nesnehchage & neese kodtumwohkom n8che ketass8tam8it, kah neese kodtumwáe ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem.
E.33.21 Amon was two and twenty years old when he began to reign, and reigned two years in Jerusalem.

α.33.22 Qut usseu ne machuk ut anaquabit Jehovah, ne aseneup Manassehoh 8shoh, newutche Ammon sephamauau wame kogoxumwe nunneukontunkoh, nish Manasseh 8shoh ayimuneupash, kah nah 8tinneumuhkauoh.
E.33.22 But he did that which was evil in the sight of the LORD, as did Manasseh his father: for Amon sacrificed unto all the carved images which Manasseh his father had made, and served them;

α.33.23 Kah matta hohpahéoou wuhhogkuh ut anaquabit Lord, neane 8shoh Manassehoh hohpaheoneup wuhhogkuh: qut Ammon nano panneussu.
E.33.23 And humbled not himself before the LORD, as Manasseh his father had humbled himself; but Amon trespassed more and more.

α.33.24 Kah wuttinneumoh wunnombeukonuk, kah wunnushóuh ut nehenwonche wekit.
E.33.24 And his servants conspired against him, and slew him in his own house.

α.33.25 Kah missinnin[n]úog ohkeit nusháog wame neg wanombeukononcheg ketass8t Ammon, kah missinninnúog ne ohkeit nompe ketass8tamwehteáog Josiahoh wunnaumonuh.
E.33.25 But the people of the land slew all them that had conspired against king Amon; and the people of the land made Josiah his son king in his stead.

α.34.1 IOsiah shwosuk tahshe kodtumwohkom n8che ketass8tam8it, kah ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem nishwinchage kah nequtte kodtumwáe.
E.34.1 Josiah was eight years old when he began to reign, and he reigned in Jerusalem one and thirty years.

α.34.2 Kah usseu ne sampwag ut anaquabit Jehovah, kah pomushau ummayut Davidoh 8shoh, kah matta panneau en wuttinohkôuneiyeu, asuh menadcheuneiyeu.
E.34.2 And he did that which was right in the sight of the LORD, and walked in the ways of David his father, and declined neither to the right hand, nor to the left.

α.34.3 Newutche shwosuk adtahshik kodtumwae ketass8tam8it, ash peississit, n8che natinneahwhau um-Manitt8moh 8shoh David, kah nabo neese kodtum8k, n8che pahkehteau Judah kah Jerusalem wutch qunuhqui ayeuonganéhtu, kah kuppahtu, kah kogoxumwe nunneukontunkoh, kah sabassumwe nunneukontunkoh.
E.34.3 For in the eighth year of his reign, while he was yet young, he began to seek after the God of David his father: and in the twelfth year he began to purge Judah and Jerusalem from the high places, and the groves, and the carved images, and the molten images.

α.34.4 Kah pohquetahwau wut-altarumash Baalim ut anaquabit, kah nunneukontunkoh waabappéhtunkqhetticheh, wuttummetahwhoh, kah kuppiyeuash, kah kogoxumwe nunneukontunkoh, kah sabassumwe nunneukontunkoh, wussóquttahwhoh, kah uppuppissiyeuhkonuh, kah wusseauhkon ut woskeche 8weenohkeóont neg sephama[n]oncheg.
E.34.4 And they brake down the altars of Baalim in his presence; and the images, that were on high above them, he cut down; and the groves, and the carved images, and the molten images, he brake in pieces, and made dust of them, and strowed it upon the graves of them that had sacrificed unto them.

α.34.5 Chikossum wuskonn8ash sephausuénuog, ut wut-altarum8ôut, kah pahketeo Judah kah Jerusalem.
E.34.5 And he burnt the bones of the priests upon their altars, and cleansed Judah and Jerusalem.

α.34.6 Kah ukkeitotanáhtu Manasseh kah Ephraim, kah Simeon, wehque Naphtali, nashpe ummattokum8uh waéenu.
E.34.6 And so did he in the cities of Manasseh, and Ephraim, and Simeon, even unto Naphtali, with their mattocks round about.

α.34.7 
E.34.7 And when he had broken down the altars and the groves, and had beaten the graven images into powder, and cut down all the idols throughout all the land of Israel, he returned to Jerusalem.

α.34.8 
E.34.8 Now in the eighteenth year of his reign, when he had purged the land, and the house, he sent Shaphan the son of Azaliah, and Maaseiah the governor of the city, and Joah the son of Joahaz the recorder, to repair the house of the LORD his God.

α.34.9 
E.34.9 And when they came to Hilkiah the high priest, they delivered the money that was brought into the house of God, which the Levites that kept the doors had gathered of the hand of Manasseh and Ephraim, and of all the remnant of Israel, and of all Judah and Benjamin; and they returned to Jerusalem.

α.34.10 
E.34.10 And they put it in the hand of the workmen that had the oversight of the house of the LORD, and they gave it to the workmen that wrought in the house of the LORD, to repair and amend the house:

α.34.11 
E.34.11 Even to the artificers and builders gave they it, to buy hewn stone, and timber for couplings, and to floor the houses which the kings of Judah had destroyed.

α.34.12 
E.34.12 And the men did the work faithfully: and the overseers of them were Jahath and Obadiah, the Levites, of the sons of Merari; and Zechariah and Meshullam, of the sons of the Kohathites, to set it forward; and other of the Levites, all that could skill of instruments of musick.

α.34.13 
E.34.13 Also they were over the bearers of burdens, and were overseers of all that wrought the work in any manner of service: and of the Levites there were scribes, and officers, and porters.

α.34.14 
E.34.14 And when they brought out the money that was brought into the house of the LORD, Hilkiah the priest found a book of the law of the LORD given by Moses.

α.34.15 
E.34.15 And Hilkiah answered and said to Shaphan the scribe, I have found the book of the law in the house of the LORD. And Hilkiah delivered the book to Shaphan.

α.34.16 
E.34.16 And Shaphan carried the book to the king, and brought the king word back again, saying, All that was committed to thy servants, they do it.

α.34.17 
E.34.17 And they have gathered together the money that was found in the house of the LORD, and have delivered it into the hand of the overseers, and to the hand of the workmen.

α.34.18 
E.34.18 Then Shaphan the scribe told the king, saying, Hilkiah the priest hath given me a book. And Shaphan read it before the king.

α.34.19 
E.34.19 And it came to pass, when the king had heard the words of the law, that he rent his clothes.

α.34.20 
E.34.20 And the king commanded Hilkiah, and Ahikam the son of Shaphan, and Abdon the son of Micah, and Shaphan the scribe, and Asaiah a servant of the king's, saying,

α.34.21 
E.34.21 Go, enquire of the LORD for me, and for them that are left in Israel and in Judah, concerning the words of the book that is found: for great is the wrath of the LORD that is poured out upon us, because our fathers have not kept the word of the LORD, to do after all that is written in this book.

α.34.22 
E.34.22 And Hilkiah, and they that the king had appointed, went to Huldah the prophetess, the wife of Shallum the son of Tikvath, the son of Hasrah, keeper of the wardrobe; (now she dwelt in Jerusalem in the college:) and they spake to her to that effect.

α.34.23 
E.34.23 And she answered them, Thus saith the LORD God of Israel, Tell ye the man that sent you to me,

α.34.24 
E.34.24 Thus saith the LORD, Behold, I will bring evil upon this place, and upon the inhabitants thereof, even all the curses that are written in the book which they have read before the king of Judah:

α.34.25 
E.34.25 Because they have forsaken me, and have burned incense unto other gods, that they might provoke me to anger with all the works of their hands; therefore my wrath shall be poured out upon this place, and shall not be quenched.

α.34.26 
E.34.26 And as for the king of Judah, who sent you to enquire of the LORD, so shall ye say unto him, Thus saith the LORD God of Israel concerning the words which thou hast heard;

α.34.27 
E.34.27 Because thine heart was tender, and thou didst humble thyself before God, when thou heardest his words against this place, and against the inhabitants thereof, and humbledst thyself before me, and didst rend thy clothes, and weep before me; I have even heard thee also, saith the LORD.

α.34.28 
E.34.28 Behold, I will gather thee to thy fathers, and thou shalt be gathered to thy grave in peace, neither shall thine eyes see all the evil that I will bring upon this place, and upon the inhabitants of the same. So they brought the king word again.

α.34.29 
E.34.29 Then the king sent and gathered together all the elders of Judah and Jerusalem.

α.34.30 
E.34.30 And the king went up into the house of the LORD, and all the men of Judah, and the inhabitants of Jerusalem, and the priests, and the Levites, and all the people, great and small: and he read in their ears all the words of the book of the covenant that was found in the house of the LORD.

α.34.31 
E.34.31 And the king stood in his place, and made a covenant before the LORD, to walk after the LORD, and to keep his commandments, and his testimonies, and his statutes, with all his heart, and with all his soul, to perform the words of the covenant which are written in this book.

α.34.32 
E.34.32 And he caused all that were present in Jerusalem and Benjamin to stand to it. And the inhabitants of Jerusalem did according to the covenant of God, the God of their fathers.

α.34.33 
E.34.33 And Josiah took away all the abominations out of all the countries that pertained to the children of Israel, and made all that were present in Israel to serve, even to serve the LORD their God. And all his days they departed not from following the LORD, the God of their fathers.

α.35.1 
E.35.1 Moreover Josiah kept a passover unto the LORD in Jerusalem: and they killed the passover on the fourteenth day of the first month.

α.35.2 
E.35.2 And he set the priests in their charges, and encouraged them to the service of the house of the LORD,

α.35.3 
E.35.3 And said unto the Levites that taught all Israel, which were holy unto the LORD, Put the holy ark in the house which Solomon the son of David king of Israel did build; it shall not be a burden upon your shoulders: serve now the LORD your God, and his people Israel,

α.35.4 
E.35.4 And prepare yourselves by the houses of your fathers, after your courses, according to the writing of David king of Israel, and according to the writing of Solomon his son.

α.35.5 
E.35.5 And stand in the holy place according to the divisions of the families of the fathers of your brethren the people, and after the division of the families of the Levites.

α.35.6 
E.35.6 So kill the passover, and sanctify yourselves, and prepare your brethren, that they may do according to the word of the LORD by the hand of Moses.

α.35.7 
E.35.7 And Josiah gave to the people, of the flock, lambs and kids, all for the passover offerings, for all that were present, to the number of thirty thousand, and three thousand bullocks: these were of the king's substance.

α.35.8 
E.35.8 And his princes gave willingly unto the people, to the priests, and to the Levites: Hilkiah and Zechariah and Jehiel, rulers of the house of God, gave unto the priests for the passover offerings two thousand and six hundred small cattle and three hundred oxen.

α.35.9 
E.35.9 Conaniah also, and Shemaiah and Nethaneel, his brethren, and Hashabiah and Jeiel and Jozabad, chief of the Levites, gave unto the Levites for passover offerings five thousand small cattle, and five hundred oxen.

α.35.10 
E.35.10 So the service was prepared, and the priests stood in their place, and the Levites in their courses, according to the king's commandment.

α.35.11 
E.35.11 And they killed the passover, and the priests sprinkled the blood from their hands, and the Levites flayed them.

α.35.12 
E.35.12 And they removed the burnt offerings, that they might give according to the divisions of the families of the people, to offer unto the LORD, as it is written in the book of Moses. And so did they with the oxen.

α.35.13 
E.35.13 And they roasted the passover with fire according to the ordinance: but the other holy offerings sod they in pots, and in caldrons, and in pans, and divided them speedily among all the people.

α.35.14 
E.35.14 And afterward they made ready for themselves, and for the priests: because the priests the sons of Aaron were busied in offering of burnt offerings and the fat until night; therefore the Levites prepared for themselves, and for the priests the sons of Aaron.

α.35.15 
E.35.15 And the singers the sons of Asaph were in their place, according to the commandment of David, and Asaph, and Heman, and Jeduthun the king's seer; and the porters waited at every gate; they might not depart from their service; for their brethren the Levites prepared for them.

α.35.16 
E.35.16 So all the service of the LORD was prepared the same day, to keep the passover, and to offer burnt offerings upon the altar of the LORD, according to the commandment of king Josiah.

α.35.17 
E.35.17 And the children of Israel that were present kept the passover at that time, and the feast of unleavened bread seven days.

α.35.18 
E.35.18 And there was no passover like to that kept in Israel from the days of Samuel the prophet; neither did all the kings of Israel keep such a passover as Josiah kept, and the priests, and the Levites, and all Judah and Israel that were present, and the inhabitants of Jerusalem.

α.35.19 
E.35.19 In the eighteenth year of the reign of Josiah was this passover kept.

α.35.20 
E.35.20 After all this, when Josiah had prepared the temple, Necho king of Egypt came up to fight against Charchemish by Euphrates: and Josiah went out against him.

α.35.21 
E.35.21 But he sent ambassadors to him, saying, What have I to do with thee, thou king of Judah? I come not against thee this day, but against the house wherewith I have war: for God commanded me to make haste: forbear thee from meddling with God, who is with me, that he destroy thee not.

α.35.22 
E.35.22 Nevertheless Josiah would not turn his face from him, but disguised himself, that he might fight with him, and hearkened not unto the words of Necho from the mouth of God, and came to fight in the valley of Megiddo.

α.35.23 
E.35.23 And the archers shot at king Josiah; and the king said to his servants, Have me away; for I am sore wounded.

α.35.24 
E.35.24 His servants therefore took him out of that chariot, and put him in the second chariot that he had; and they brought him to Jerusalem, and he died, and was buried in one of the sepulchres of his fathers. And all Judah and Jerusalem mourned for Josiah.

α.35.25 
E.35.25 And Jeremiah lamented for Josiah: and all the singing men and the singing women spake of Josiah in their lamentations to this day, and made them an ordinance in Israel: and, behold, they are written in the lamentations.

α.35.26 
E.35.26 Now the rest of the acts of Josiah, and his goodness, according to that which was written in the law of the LORD,

α.35.27 
E.35.27 And his deeds, first and last, behold, they are written in the book of the kings of Israel and Judah.

α.36.1 NEit missinninnuog ne ohkeit nemunaog Jehoahazoh wunnaumonuh Josiah, kah wunnompe ketass8tamuhkonouh ut Jerusalem.
E.36.1 Then the people of the land took Jehoahaz the son of Josiah, and made him king in his father's stead in Jerusalem.

α.36.2 Kah Jehoahaz nesnehchage kodtumwohkom kah nish, n8che ketass8tam8it, kah nishuoh nepáuzoh ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem.
E.36.2 Jehoahaz was twenty and three years old when he began to reign, and he reigned three months in Jerusalem.

α.36.3 Kah [E]gypte ketass8t wutontsapheuh ut Jerusalem, kah ôadtehteaheau ne ohke nequt pasuk8e silvere talentsash, kah pasuk golde talent.
E.36.3 And the king of Egypt put him down at Jerusalem, and condemned the land in an hundred talents of silver and a talent of gold.

α.36.4 Kah [E]gypte ketass8t Eliakimoh wematoh ketass8tamwaheau ut Judah kah Jerusalem, káh wutôs8wunnaumauoh 8wesuonk Jehojakim, kah Necho nemunau Jehoahazoh wematoh, kah wutuss8wunuh Egypt.
E.36.4 And the king of Egypt made Eliakim his brother king over Judah and Jerusalem, and turned his name to Jehoiakim. And Necho took Jehoahaz his brother, and carried him to Egypt.

α.36.5 Jehojakim noh nesnechage kodtumwohkom, kah napanna n8che ketass8tam8it, kah nabo nequtte kodtumwae ketass8tam88 ut Jerusalem, kah ussu ne machuk ut anaquabit Jehovahoh ummanitt8moh.
E.36.5 Jehoiakim was twenty and five years old when he began to reign, and he reigned eleven years in Jerusalem: and he did that which was evil in the sight of the LORD his God.

α.36.6 Nebuchadnezzar Babiloné ketass8t wutayeuuhkonuh, kah wuttohtogkupunoh, fettersash, kah wutuss8wunuh Babilon.
E.36.6 Against him came up Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon, and bound him in fetters, to carry him to Babylon.

α.36.7 Nebuchadnezzar wonk monchadtoou nawutch auwohteaongash wutch wekit Jehovah en Babilon, kah upponamunash wuttemplumut ut Babilon.
E.36.7 Nebuchadnezzar also carried of the vessels of the house of the LORD to Babylon, and put them in his temple at Babylon.

α.36.8 Kah onkatogish wutusseongash Jehojakim, kah wunnishkeneunkquott8mash nish aseipash, kah ne namehteauit, kusseh nish wussukwhosuash ut up-b8kum8out Israelle kah Judae ketass8twamwog kah Jehojakinoh wunnaumonuh wunnompass8tamomukquoh.
E.36.8 Now the rest of the acts of Jehoiakim, and his abominations which he did, and that which was found in him, behold, they are written in the book of the kings of Israel and Judah: and Jehoiachin his son reigned in his stead.

α.36.9 Jehoiachin shwosuk tahshe kodtumwohkomup n8che ketass8tam8it, kah ketass8tam88 nishuoh nepauzoh, jah piogkuk[-]kesukquae ut Jerusalem, kah usseu ne machut ut anaquabit Jehovah.
E.36.9 Jehoiachin was eight years old when he began to reign, and he reigned three months and ten days in Jerusalem: and he did that which was evil in the sight of the LORD.

α.36.10 Kah kodtum8 mahtshunk, Nebuchadnezzar ketass8t, wunnegont8ónuh, kah uppas8óuh Babylon nashpe tapeneunkquotte wishquash ut wekit Jehovah, kah Zedekiahoh wematoh ketass8tamwaheau ut Judah kah Jerusalem.
E.36.10 And when the year was expired, king Nebuchadnezzar sent, and brought him to Babylon, with the goodly vessels of the house of the LORD, and made Zedekiah his brother king over Judah and Jerusalem.

α.36.11 Zedekiah nesnechage kah nequtta kodtumwohkom n8che ketass8tam8it, kah nabo nequtta kodtumwáe ketass8tum88 ut Jerusalem,
E.36.11 Zedekiah was one and twenty years old when he began to reign, and reigned eleven years in Jerusalem.

α.36.12 Kah ussu ne machuk ut anaquabit Jehovah, um-Manitt8moh, matta hohpáheaou ut anaquabit Jeremiah quoshodtuk wutch wutt8nut Jehovah.
E.36.12 And he did that which was evil in the sight of the LORD his God, and humbled not himself before Jeremiah the prophet speaking from the mouth of the LORD.

α.36.13 Wonk cheketauau Nebuchadnezzaroh neh chadchekeyeuwáhikqutcheh nashpe Godoh, qut chetauwèhteau wussittipuk, kah menehkéhteau wuttah, matta woh ukquinnuppeinat en Jehovahut um-Manitt8moh Isral.
E.36.13 And he also rebelled against king Nebuchadnezzar, who had made him swear by God: but he stiffened his neck, and hardened his heart from turning unto the LORD God of Israel.

α.36.14 Nano wame kehcheyeue sephausuén[u]og kah missinninnúog m8cheke panneusseog, neaunag wame wunnishkeneunkqott8m8ash penuwohteaog, kah nishketeauog wek Jehovah, ne waneetupanatamwahteunkup ut Jerusalem. 
E.36.14 Moreover all the chief of the priests, and the people, transgressed very much after all the abominations of the heathen; and polluted the house of the LORD which he had hallowed in Jerusalem.

α.36.15 Kah Jehovah 8sh8oh um-Manitt8m8oh n$noh wuttin ann8non nashpe wunnutchegan8out wutann8naénumoh, nompoáeu omohkeu, kah ann8team8 newutche kitteamonteanumau nummissinninneumoh, kah wutappuonganit.
E.36.15 And the LORD God of their fathers sent to them by his messengers, rising up betimes, and sending; because he had compassion on his people, and on his dwelling place:

α.36.16 Qut nag momonehtauaog wutann8naenumoh God, kah mishanantamwog wuttinn8waongash, kah onkquanumwehteaog ukquoshodtumwaeneumoh, nô pajeh umm8squanittam8onk Jehovah ayeuuhkonittue neepauwehtauau ummissinninneumoh, n[ó] pajeh wanne netskehettinneát.
E.36.16 But they mocked the messengers of God, and despised his words, and misused his prophets, until the wrath of the LORD arose against his people, till there was no remedy.

α.36.17 Newaj nukkuhkomwaheont Caldee ketass8t, noh nohtauont 8skeneumoh ut wunneetupanatamwe wetuomut, kah wanne kitteamonteanumoou wuskeniñuh, asuh nunksquaesoh, kehchiis, asuh noh mattauntog, wame ummagun ut wunnutcheganit.
E.36.17 Therefore he brought upon them the king of the Chaldees, who slew their young men with the sword in the house of their sanctuary, and had no compassion upon young man or maiden, old man, or him that stooped for age: he gave them all into his hand.

α.36.18 Káh wame auwohteaongash ut wekit God, magogish kah papeississinitcheh, kah nompak8unash wekit Jehovah, kah wunnompak8unash ketass8t, kah wussontimosumoh, wame yeush uppaudtauunash Babilon
E.36.18 And all the vessels of the house of God, great and small, and the treasures of the house of the LORD, and the treasures of the king, and of his princes; all these he brought to Babylon.

α.36.19 Kah chikkosumwog wek God, kah tauwutchahthamwog Jerusaleme pummeneutunk, kah chikosum wáme mishittae komukqutash nashpé n8tau, kah matchehteau wame tapeneunkquttue wishquash.
E.36.19 And they burnt the house of God, and brake down the wall of Jerusalem, and burnt all the palaces thereof with fire, and destroyed all the goodly vessels thereof.

α.36.20 Kah neh tomwuttamunutcheh togkodteg, wutuss8wunah Babilon: uttoh adt wuttinneumoh, kah wunnaumonuh, nó pajeh ketass8tam8it Persiae ketass8tamoonk.
E.36.20 And them that had escaped from the sword carried he away to Babylon; where they were servants to him and his sons until the reign of the kingdom of Persia:

α.36.21 Pak[o]dche ussenat wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nashpe wutt8n Jeremiah, nó pajeh ohke nanawehteomuk wussabbath8mash, newutché nisahke touwussik, nanawehteau wussabbat8mash, papogkodche nesausuk tahshinchage kodtumwae.
E.36.21 To fulfil the word of the LORD by the mouth of Jeremiah, until the land had enjoyed her sabbaths: for as long as she lay desolate she kept sabbath, to fulfil threescore and ten years.

α.36.22 Kah negonne kodtum8k Cyrus Persiae ketass8t (ne ukkutt8onk Jehovah ne an8wop wutt8n Jeremiah woh pakodche nnih) Jehovah wogkouunau wunnashauonguh Cyrus Persiae ketass8t: newaj wahteauwahuau papashpe wame wutass8tam8onganit, kah wonk 8sukuhhumun, n8wau,
E.36.22 Now in the first year of Cyrus king of Persia, that the word of the LORD spoken by the mouth of Jeremiah might be accomplished, the LORD stirred up the spirit of Cyrus king of Persia, that he made a proclamation throughout all his kingdom, and put it also in writing, saying,

α.36.23 Yeu wussin Cyrus Persiae ketass8t, wame ketass8tam8ongash ut ohkeit Jehovah kesukque Manit nuttinnumunkqunash, kah nummeechumuhkonuk n8wekuhkauonat, ut Jerusalem, ne ut Judah, howan noh, kenugke kenaau wame ummissinninneumoh: Jehovahoh um-Manitt8moh weetomukqutch, kah kuhkuhqueitch.
E.36.23 Thus saith Cyrus king of Persia, All the kingdoms of the earth hath the LORD God of heaven given me; and he hath charged me to build him an house in Jerusalem, which is in Judah. Who is there among you of all his people?  The LORD his God be with him, and let him go up.
